00174 #define CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(_bp, _port, _phy_addr, _bank, _addr, _val) \
00175     bnx2x_cl45_write(_bp, _port, 0, _phy_addr, \
00176         DEFAULT_PHY_DEV_ADDR, \
00177         (_bank + (_addr & 0xf)), \
00178         _val)
00179 
00180 #define CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(_bp, _port, _phy_addr, _bank, _addr, _val) \
00181     bnx2x_cl45_read(_bp, _port, 0, _phy_addr, \

00184         _val)

00186 static void bnx2x_set_serdes_access(struct link_params *params)
00187 {
00188     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00189     u32 emac_base = (params->port) ? GRCBASE_EMAC1 : GRCBASE_EMAC0;
00190 
00191     /* Set Clause 22 */
00192     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_SERDES0_CTRL_MD_ST + params->port*0x10, 1);
00193     REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, 0x245f8000);
00194     udelay(500);
00195     REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, 0x245d000f);
00196     udelay(500);
00197      /* Set Clause 45 */
00198     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_SERDES0_CTRL_MD_ST + params->port*0x10, 0);
00199 }
00200 static void bnx2x_set_phy_mdio(struct link_params *params, u8 phy_flags)
00201 {
00202     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00203 
00204     if (phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
00205         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_MD_ST +
00206                params->port*0x18, 0);
00207         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_MD_DEVAD + params->port*0x18,
00208                DEFAULT_PHY_DEV_ADDR);
00209     } else {
00210         bnx2x_set_serdes_access(params);
00211 
00212         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_SERDES0_CTRL_MD_DEVAD +
00213                params->port*0x10,
00214                DEFAULT_PHY_DEV_ADDR);
00215     }
00216 }

00218 static u32 bnx2x_bits_en(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 reg, u32 bits)
00219 {
00220     u32 val = REG_RD(bp, reg);
00221 
00222     val |= bits;
00223     REG_WR(bp, reg, val);
00224     return val;
00225 }
00226 
00227 static u32 bnx2x_bits_dis(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 reg, u32 bits)
00228 {
00229     u32 val = REG_RD(bp, reg);
00230 
00231     val &= ~bits;
00232     REG_WR(bp, reg, val);
00233     return val;
00234 }
00235 
00236 static void bnx2x_emac_init(struct link_params *params,
00237                struct link_vars *vars)
00238 {
00239     /* reset and unreset the emac core */
00240     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00241     u8 port = params->port;
00242     u32 emac_base = port ? GRCBASE_EMAC1 : GRCBASE_EMAC0;
00243     u32 val;
00244     u16 timeout;
00245 
00246     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_CLEAR,
00247            (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_EMAC0_HARD_CORE << port));
00248     udelay(5);
00249     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_SET,
00250            (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_EMAC0_HARD_CORE << port));
00251 
00252     /* init emac - use read-modify-write */
00253     /* self clear reset */
00254     val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE);
00255     EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE, (val | EMAC_MODE_RESET));
00256 
00257     timeout = 200;
00258     do {
00259         val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE);
00260         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "EMAC reset reg is %u\n", val);
00261         if (!timeout) {
00262             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "EMAC timeout!\n");
00263             return;
00264         }
00265         timeout--;
00266     } while (val & EMAC_MODE_RESET);
00267 
00268     /* Set mac address */
00269     val = ((params->mac_addr[0] << 8) |
00270         params->mac_addr[1]);
00271     EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_MAC_MATCH, val);
00272 
00273     val = ((params->mac_addr[2] << 24) |
00274            (params->mac_addr[3] << 16) |
00275            (params->mac_addr[4] << 8) |
00276         params->mac_addr[5]);
00277     EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_MAC_MATCH + 4, val);
00278 }
00279 
00280 static u8 bnx2x_emac_enable(struct link_params *params,
00281               struct link_vars *vars, u8 lb)
00282 {
00283     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00284     u8 port = params->port;
00285     u32 emac_base = port ? GRCBASE_EMAC1 : GRCBASE_EMAC0;
00286     u32 val;
00287 
00288     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enabling EMAC\n");
00289 
00290     /* enable emac and not bmac */
00291     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_EMAC0_PORT + port*4, 1);
00292 
00293     /* for paladium */
00294     if (CHIP_REV_IS_EMUL(bp)) {
00295         /* Use lane 1 (of lanes 0-3) */
00296         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_LANE_SEL_P0 + port*4, 1);
00297         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_SERDES0_MODE_SEL +
00298                 port*4, 1);
00299     }
00300     /* for fpga */
00301     else
00302 
00303     if (CHIP_REV_IS_FPGA(bp)) {
00304         /* Use lane 1 (of lanes 0-3) */
00305         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_emac_enable: Setting FPGA\n");
00306 
00307         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_LANE_SEL_P0 + port*4, 1);
00308         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_SERDES0_MODE_SEL + port*4,
00309                 0);
00310     } else
00311     /* ASIC */
00312     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
00313         u32 ser_lane = ((params->lane_config &
00314                 PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_MASK) >>
00315                 PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_SHIFT);
00316 
00317         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS\n");
00318         /* select the master lanes (out of 0-3) */
00319         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_LANE_SEL_P0 +
00320                port*4, ser_lane);
00321         /* select XGXS */
00322         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_SERDES0_MODE_SEL +
00323                port*4, 1);
00324 
00325     } else { /* SerDes */
00326         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes\n");
00327         /* select SerDes */
00328         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_SERDES0_MODE_SEL +
00329                port*4, 0);
00330     }
00331 
00332     bnx2x_bits_en(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_RX_MODE,
00333             EMAC_RX_MODE_RESET);
00334     bnx2x_bits_en(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_TX_MODE,
00335             EMAC_TX_MODE_RESET);
00336 
00337     if (CHIP_REV_IS_SLOW(bp)) {
00338         /* config GMII mode */
00339         val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE);
00340         EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE,
00341                 (val | EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII));
00342     } else { /* ASIC */
00343         /* pause enable/disable */
00344         bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_RX_MODE,
00345                    EMAC_RX_MODE_FLOW_EN);
00346         if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX)
00347             bnx2x_bits_en(bp, emac_base +
00348                     EMAC_REG_EMAC_RX_MODE,
00349                     EMAC_RX_MODE_FLOW_EN);
00350 
00351         bnx2x_bits_dis(bp,  emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_TX_MODE,
00352                  (EMAC_TX_MODE_EXT_PAUSE_EN |
00353                   EMAC_TX_MODE_FLOW_EN));
00354         if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX)
00355             bnx2x_bits_en(bp, emac_base +
00356                     EMAC_REG_EMAC_TX_MODE,
00357                    (EMAC_TX_MODE_EXT_PAUSE_EN |
00358                     EMAC_TX_MODE_FLOW_EN));
00359     }
00360 
00361     /* KEEP_VLAN_TAG, promiscuous */
00362     val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_RX_MODE);
00363     val |= EMAC_RX_MODE_KEEP_VLAN_TAG | EMAC_RX_MODE_PROMISCUOUS;
00364     EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_RX_MODE, val);
00365 
00366     /* Set Loopback */
00367     val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE);
00368     if (lb)
00369         val |= 0x810;
00370     else
00371         val &= ~0x810;
00372     EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE, val);
00373 
00374     /* enable emac */
00375     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_EMAC0_EN + port*4, 1);
00376 
00377     /* enable emac for jumbo packets */
00378     EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_RX_MTU_SIZE,
00379         (EMAC_RX_MTU_SIZE_JUMBO_ENA |
00380          (ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE + ETH_OVREHEAD)));
00381 
00382     /* strip CRC */
00383     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_INGRESS_EMAC0_NO_CRC + port*4, 0x1);
00384 
00385     /* disable the NIG in/out to the bmac */
00386     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_IN_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00387     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_PAUSE_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00388     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00389 
00390     /* enable the NIG in/out to the emac */
00391     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_IN_EN + port*4, 0x1);
00392     val = 0;
00393     if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX)
00394         val = 1;
00395 
00396     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_PAUSE_OUT_EN + port*4, val);
00397     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_EMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x1);
00398 
00399     if (CHIP_REV_IS_EMUL(bp)) {
00400         /* take the BigMac out of reset */
00401         REG_WR(bp,
00402                GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_SET,
00403                (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_BMAC0 << port));
00404 
00405         /* enable access for bmac registers */
00406         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_REGS_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x1);
00407     } else
00408         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_REGS_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00409 
00410     vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_EMAC;
00411     return 0;
00412 }
00413 
00414 
00415 static u8 bnx2x_bmac1_enable(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars,
00416               u8 is_lb)
00417 {
00418     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00419     u8 port = params->port;
00420     u32 bmac_addr = port ? NIG_REG_INGRESS_BMAC1_MEM :
00421                    NIG_REG_INGRESS_BMAC0_MEM;
00422     u32 wb_data[2];
00423     u32 val;
00424 
00425     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Enabling BigMAC1\n");
00426 
00427     /* XGXS control */
00428     wb_data[0] = 0x3c;
00429     wb_data[1] = 0;
00430     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr +
00431               BIGMAC_REGISTER_BMAC_XGXS_CONTROL,
00432               wb_data, 2);
00433 
00434     /* tx MAC SA */
00435     wb_data[0] = ((params->mac_addr[2] << 24) |
00436                (params->mac_addr[3] << 16) |
00437                (params->mac_addr[4] << 8) |
00438             params->mac_addr[5]);
00439     wb_data[1] = ((params->mac_addr[0] << 8) |
00440             params->mac_addr[1]);
00441     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_TX_SOURCE_ADDR,
00442             wb_data, 2);
00443 
00444     /* tx control */
00445     val = 0xc0;
00446     if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX)
00447         val |= 0x800000;
00448     wb_data[0] = val;
00449     wb_data[1] = 0;
00450     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_TX_CONTROL,
00451             wb_data, 2);
00452 
00453     /* mac control */
00454     val = 0x3;
00455     if (is_lb) {
00456         val |= 0x4;
00457         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enable bmac loopback\n");
00458     }
00459     wb_data[0] = val;
00460     wb_data[1] = 0;
00461     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00462             wb_data, 2);
00463 
00464     /* set rx mtu */
00465     wb_data[0] = ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE + ETH_OVREHEAD;
00466     wb_data[1] = 0;
00467     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_RX_MAX_SIZE,
00468             wb_data, 2);
00469 
00470     /* rx control set to don't strip crc */
00471     val = 0x14;
00472     if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX)
00473         val |= 0x20;
00474     wb_data[0] = val;
00475     wb_data[1] = 0;
00476     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_RX_CONTROL,
00477             wb_data, 2);
00478 
00479     /* set tx mtu */
00480     wb_data[0] = ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE + ETH_OVREHEAD;
00481     wb_data[1] = 0;
00482     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_TX_MAX_SIZE,
00483             wb_data, 2);
00484 
00485     /* set cnt max size */
00486     wb_data[0] = ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE + ETH_OVREHEAD;
00487     wb_data[1] = 0;
00488     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_CNT_MAX_SIZE,
00489             wb_data, 2);
00490 
00491     /* configure safc */
00492     wb_data[0] = 0x1000200;
00493     wb_data[1] = 0;
00494     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_RX_LLFC_MSG_FLDS,
00495             wb_data, 2);
00496     /* fix for emulation */
00497     if (CHIP_REV_IS_EMUL(bp)) {
00498         wb_data[0] = 0xf000;
00499         wb_data[1] = 0;
00500         REG_WR_DMAE(bp,
00501                 bmac_addr + BIGMAC_REGISTER_TX_PAUSE_THRESHOLD,
00502                 wb_data, 2);
00503     }
00504 
00505 
00506     return 0;
00507 }
00508 
00509 static u8 bnx2x_bmac2_enable(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars,
00510               u8 is_lb)
00511 {
00512     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00513     u8 port = params->port;
00514     u32 bmac_addr = port ? NIG_REG_INGRESS_BMAC1_MEM :
00515                    NIG_REG_INGRESS_BMAC0_MEM;
00516     u32 wb_data[2];
00517     u32 val;
00518 
00519     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Enabling BigMAC2\n");
00520 
00521     wb_data[0] = 0;
00522     wb_data[1] = 0;
00523     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00524             wb_data, 2);
00525     udelay(30);
00526 
00527     /* XGXS control: Reset phy HW, MDIO registers, PHY PLL and BMAC */
00528     wb_data[0] = 0x3c;
00529     wb_data[1] = 0;
00530     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr +
00531               BIGMAC2_REGISTER_BMAC_XGXS_CONTROL,
00532               wb_data, 2);
00533 
00534     udelay(30);
00535 
00536     /* tx MAC SA */
00537     wb_data[0] = ((params->mac_addr[2] << 24) |
00538                (params->mac_addr[3] << 16) |
00539                (params->mac_addr[4] << 8) |
00540             params->mac_addr[5]);
00541     wb_data[1] = ((params->mac_addr[0] << 8) |
00542             params->mac_addr[1]);
00543     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_TX_SOURCE_ADDR,
00544               wb_data, 2);
00545 
00546     udelay(30);
00547 
00548     /* Tx control */
00549     val = 0xc0;
00550     if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX)
00551         val |= 0x800000;
00552     wb_data[0] = val;
00553     wb_data[1] = 0;
00554     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_TX_CONTROL,
00555             wb_data, 2);
00556 
00557     /* Configure SAFC */
00558     wb_data[0] = 0x1000200;
00559     wb_data[1] = 0;
00560     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_RX_LLFC_MSG_FLDS,
00561               wb_data, 2);
00562     udelay(30);
00563 
00564     /* set rx mtu */
00565     wb_data[0] = ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE + ETH_OVREHEAD;
00566     wb_data[1] = 0;
00567     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_RX_MAX_SIZE,
00568               wb_data, 2);
00569     udelay(30);
00570 
00571     /* set tx mtu */
00572     wb_data[0] = ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE + ETH_OVREHEAD;
00573     wb_data[1] = 0;
00574     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_TX_MAX_SIZE,
00575               wb_data, 2);
00576     udelay(30);
00577 
00578     /* Set rx control: Strip CRC and enable BigMAC to relay
00579     control packets to the system as well*/
00580     val = 0x54;
00581     if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX)
00582         val |= 0x20;
00583     wb_data[0] = val;
00584     wb_data[1] = 0;
00585     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_RX_CONTROL,
00586               wb_data, 2);
00587     udelay(30);
00588 
00589     if (params->feature_config_flags & FEATURE_CONFIG_PFC_ENABLED) {
00590         wb_data[0] = 0xb; /* Enable RFC RX & TX and set 8 COS */
00591         wb_data[1] = 0;
00592         REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_PFC_CONTROL,
00593                   wb_data, 2);
00594     }
00595 
00596     /* mac control */
00597     val = 0x3; /* Enable RX and TX */
00598     if (is_lb) {
00599         val |= 0x4; /* Local loopback */
00600         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enable bmac loopback\n");
00601     }
00602     /* When PFC enabled, Pass pause frames towards the NIG. */
00603     if (params->feature_config_flags & FEATURE_CONFIG_PFC_ENABLED)
00604         val |= (1<<6);
00605 
00606     wb_data[0] = val;
00607     wb_data[1] = 0;
00608     REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr + BIGMAC2_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00609               wb_data, 2);
00610 
00611     return 0;
00612 }
00613 
00614 static u8 bnx2x_bmac_enable(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars,
00615               u8 is_lb)
00616 {
00617     u8 rc, port = params->port;
00618     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00619     u32 val;
00620     /* reset and unreset the BigMac */
00621     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_CLEAR,
00622            (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_BMAC0 << port));
00623     msleep(1);
00624 
00625     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_SET,
00626            (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_BMAC0 << port));
00627 
00628     /* enable access for bmac registers */
00629     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_REGS_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x1);
00630 
00631     /* Enable BMAC according to BMAC type*/
00632     if (CHIP_IS_E2_NOT_PHASE0(params->chip_id))
00633         rc = bnx2x_bmac2_enable(params, vars, is_lb);
00634     else
00635         rc = bnx2x_bmac1_enable(params, vars, is_lb);
00636 
00637     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_SERDES0_MODE_SEL + port*4, 0x1);
00638     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS_LANE_SEL_P0 + port*4, 0x0);
00639     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_EMAC0_PORT + port*4, 0x0);
00640     val = 0;
00641     if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX)
00642         val = 1;
00643     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_PAUSE_OUT_EN + port*4, val);
00644     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_EMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00645     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_IN_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00646     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_PAUSE_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x0);
00647     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_IN_EN + port*4, 0x1);
00648     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0x1);
00649 
00650     vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_BMAC;
00651     return rc;
00652 }
00653 
00654 static void bnx2x_phy_deassert(struct link_params *params, u8 phy_flags)
00655 {
00656     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00657     u32 val;
00658 
00659     if (phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
00660         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_phy_deassert:XGXS\n");
00661         val = XGXS_RESET_BITS;
00662 
00663     } else { /* SerDes */
00664         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_phy_deassert:SerDes\n");
00665         val = SERDES_RESET_BITS;
00666     }
00667 
00668     val = val << (params->port*16);
00669 
00670     /* reset and unreset the SerDes/XGXS */
00671     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_3_CLEAR,
00672             val);
00673     udelay(500);
00674     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_3_SET,
00675             val);
00676     bnx2x_set_phy_mdio(params, phy_flags);
00677 }
00678 
00679 void bnx2x_link_status_update(struct link_params *params,
00680                 struct link_vars   *vars)
00681 {
00682     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00683     u8 link_10g;
00684     u8 port = params->port;
00685 
00686     if (params->switch_cfg ==  SWITCH_CFG_1G)
00687         vars->phy_flags = PHY_SERDES_FLAG;
00688     else
00689         vars->phy_flags = PHY_XGXS_FLAG;
00690     vars->link_status = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
00691                       offsetof(struct shmem_region,
00692                        port_mb[port].link_status));
00693 
00694     vars->link_up = (vars->link_status & LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP);
00695 
00696     if (vars->link_up) {
00697         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "phy link up\n");
00698 
00699         vars->phy_link_up = 1;
00700         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
00701         switch (vars->link_status &
00702                     LINK_STATUS_SPEED_AND_DUPLEX_MASK) {
00703             case LINK_10THD:
00704                 vars->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
00705                 /* fall thru */
00706             case LINK_10TFD:
00707                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_10;
00708                 break;
00709 
00710             case LINK_100TXHD:
00711                 vars->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
00712                 /* fall thru */
00713             case LINK_100T4:
00714             case LINK_100TXFD:
00715                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_100;
00716                 break;
00717 
00718             case LINK_1000THD:
00719                 vars->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
00720                 /* fall thru */
00721             case LINK_1000TFD:
00722                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
00723                 break;
00724 
00725             case LINK_2500THD:
00726                 vars->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
00727                 /* fall thru */
00728             case LINK_2500TFD:
00729                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_2500;
00730                 break;
00731 
00732             case LINK_10GTFD:
00733                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
00734                 break;
00735 
00736             case LINK_12GTFD:
00737                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_12000;
00738                 break;
00739 
00740             case LINK_12_5GTFD:
00741                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_12500;
00742                 break;
00743 
00744             case LINK_13GTFD:
00745                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_13000;
00746                 break;
00747 
00748             case LINK_15GTFD:
00749                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_15000;
00750                 break;
00751 
00752             case LINK_16GTFD:
00753                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_16000;
00754                 break;
00755 
00756             default:
00757                 break;
00758         }
00759 
00760         if (vars->link_status & LINK_STATUS_TX_FLOW_CONTROL_ENABLED)
00761             vars->flow_ctrl |= BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX;
00762         else
00763             vars->flow_ctrl &= ~BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX;
00764 
00765         if (vars->link_status & LINK_STATUS_RX_FLOW_CONTROL_ENABLED)
00766             vars->flow_ctrl |= BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX;
00767         else
00768             vars->flow_ctrl &= ~BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX;
00769 
00770         if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
00771             if (vars->line_speed &&
00772                 ((vars->line_speed == SPEED_10) ||
00773                  (vars->line_speed == SPEED_100))) {
00774                 vars->phy_flags |= PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
00775             } else {
00776                 vars->phy_flags &= ~PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
00777             }
00778         }
00779 
00780         /* anything 10 and over uses the bmac */
00781         link_10g = ((vars->line_speed == SPEED_10000) ||
00782                 (vars->line_speed == SPEED_12000) ||
00783                 (vars->line_speed == SPEED_12500) ||
00784                 (vars->line_speed == SPEED_13000) ||
00785                 (vars->line_speed == SPEED_15000) ||
00786                 (vars->line_speed == SPEED_16000));
00787         if (link_10g)
00788             vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_BMAC;
00789         else
00790             vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_EMAC;
00791 
00792     } else { /* link down */
00793         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "phy link down\n");
00794 
00795         vars->phy_link_up = 0;
00796 
00797         vars->line_speed = 0;
00798         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
00799         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
00800 
00801         /* indicate no mac active */
00802         vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_NONE;
00803     }
00804 
00805     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "link_status 0x%x  phy_link_up %x\n",
00806          vars->link_status, vars->phy_link_up);
00807     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "line_speed %x  duplex %x  flow_ctrl 0x%x\n",
00808          vars->line_speed, vars->duplex, vars->flow_ctrl);
00809 }
00810 
00811 static void bnx2x_update_mng(struct link_params *params, u32 link_status)
00812 {
00813     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00814 
00815         REG_WR(bp, params->shmem_base +
00816            offsetof(struct shmem_region,
00817                 port_mb[params->port].link_status),
00818             link_status);
00819 }
00820 
00821 static void bnx2x_bmac_rx_disable(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 chip_id, u8 port)
00822 {
00823     u32 bmac_addr = port ? NIG_REG_INGRESS_BMAC1_MEM :
00824             NIG_REG_INGRESS_BMAC0_MEM;
00825     u32 wb_data[2];
00826     u32 nig_bmac_enable = REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_REGS_OUT_EN +
00827                      port*4);
00828 
00829     /* Only if the bmac is out of reset */
00830     if (REG_RD(bp, MISC_REG_RESET_REG_2) &
00831             (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_BMAC0 << port) &&
00832         nig_bmac_enable) {
00833 
00834         if (CHIP_IS_E2_NOT_PHASE0(chip_id)) {
00835             /* Clear Rx Enable bit in BMAC_CONTROL register */
00836             REG_RD_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr +
00837                       BIGMAC2_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00838                       wb_data, 2);
00839             wb_data[0] &= ~BMAC_CONTROL_RX_ENABLE;
00840             REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr +
00841                       BIGMAC2_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00842                       wb_data, 2);
00843         } else {
00844             /* Clear Rx Enable bit in BMAC_CONTROL register */
00845             REG_RD_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr +
00846                       BIGMAC_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00847                       wb_data, 2);
00848             wb_data[0] &= ~BMAC_CONTROL_RX_ENABLE;
00849             REG_WR_DMAE(bp, bmac_addr +
00850                       BIGMAC_REGISTER_BMAC_CONTROL,
00851                       wb_data, 2);
00852         }
00853         msleep(1);
00854     }
00855 }
00856 
00857 static u8 bnx2x_pbf_update(struct link_params *params, u32 flow_ctrl,
00858              u32 line_speed)
00859 {
00860     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
00861     u8 port = params->port;
00862     u32 init_crd, crd;
00863     u32 count = 1000;
00864 
00865     /* disable port */
00866     REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_DISABLE_NEW_TASK_PROC_P0 + port*4, 0x1);
00867 
00868     /* wait for init credit */
00869     init_crd = REG_RD(bp, PBF_REG_P0_INIT_CRD + port*4);
00870     crd = REG_RD(bp, PBF_REG_P0_CREDIT + port*8);
00871     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "init_crd 0x%x  crd 0x%x\n", init_crd, crd);
00872 
00873     while ((init_crd != crd) && count) {
00874         msleep(5);
00875 
00876         crd = REG_RD(bp, PBF_REG_P0_CREDIT + port*8);
00877         count--;
00878     }
00879     crd = REG_RD(bp, PBF_REG_P0_CREDIT + port*8);
00880     if (init_crd != crd) {
00881         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BUG! init_crd 0x%x != crd 0x%x\n",
00882               init_crd, crd);
00883         return -EINVAL;
00884     }
00885 
00886     if (flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX ||
00887         line_speed == SPEED_10 ||
00888         line_speed == SPEED_100 ||
00889         line_speed == SPEED_1000 ||
00890         line_speed == SPEED_2500) {
00891         REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_P0_PAUSE_ENABLE + port*4, 1);
00892         /* update threshold */
00893         REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_P0_ARB_THRSH + port*4, 0);
00894         /* update init credit */
00895         init_crd = 778;     /* (800-18-4) */
00896 
00897     } else {
00898         u32 thresh = (ETH_MAX_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE +
00899                   ETH_OVREHEAD)/16;
00900         REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_P0_PAUSE_ENABLE + port*4, 0);
00901         /* update threshold */
00902         REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_P0_ARB_THRSH + port*4, thresh);
00903         /* update init credit */
00904         switch (line_speed) {
00905         case SPEED_10000:
00906             init_crd = thresh + 553 - 22;
00907             break;
00908 
00909         case SPEED_12000:
00910             init_crd = thresh + 664 - 22;
00911             break;
00912 
00913         case SPEED_13000:
00914             init_crd = thresh + 742 - 22;
00915             break;
00916 
00917         case SPEED_16000:
00918             init_crd = thresh + 778 - 22;
00919             break;
00920         default:
00921             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Invalid line_speed 0x%x\n",
00922                   line_speed);
00923             return -EINVAL;
00924         }
00925     }
00926     REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_P0_INIT_CRD + port*4, init_crd);
00927     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "PBF updated to speed %d credit %d\n",
00928          line_speed, init_crd);
00929 
00930     /* probe the credit changes */
00931     REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_INIT_P0 + port*4, 0x1);
00932     msleep(5);
00933     REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_INIT_P0 + port*4, 0x0);
00934 
00935     /* enable port */
00936     REG_WR(bp, PBF_REG_DISABLE_NEW_TASK_PROC_P0 + port*4, 0x0);
00937     return 0;
00938 }
00939 
00940 static u32 bnx2x_get_emac_base(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 ext_phy_type, u8 port)
00941 {
00942     u32 emac_base;
00943 
00944     switch (ext_phy_type) {
00945     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
00946     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
00947     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
00948         /* All MDC/MDIO is directed through single EMAC */
00949         if (REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_PORT_SWAP))
00950             emac_base = GRCBASE_EMAC0;
00951         else
00952             emac_base = GRCBASE_EMAC1;
00953         break;
00954     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
00955         emac_base = (port) ? GRCBASE_EMAC0 : GRCBASE_EMAC1;
00956         break;
00957     default:
00958         emac_base = (port) ? GRCBASE_EMAC1 : GRCBASE_EMAC0;
00959         break;
00960     }
00961     return emac_base;
00962 
00963 }
00964 
00965 u8 bnx2x_cl45_write(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port, u32 ext_phy_type,
00966           u8 phy_addr, u8 devad, u16 reg, u16 val)
00967 {
00968     u32 tmp, saved_mode;
00969     u8 i, rc = 0;
00970     u32 mdio_ctrl = bnx2x_get_emac_base(bp, ext_phy_type, port);
00971 
00972     /* set clause 45 mode, slow down the MDIO clock to 2.5MHz
00973      * (a value of 49==0x31) and make sure that the AUTO poll is off
00974      */
00975 
00976     saved_mode = REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00977     tmp = saved_mode & ~(EMAC_MDIO_MODE_AUTO_POLL |
00978                  EMAC_MDIO_MODE_CLOCK_CNT);
00979     tmp |= (EMAC_MDIO_MODE_CLAUSE_45 |
00980         (49 << EMAC_MDIO_MODE_CLOCK_CNT_BITSHIFT));
00981     REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, tmp);
00982     REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00983     udelay(40);
00984 
00985     /* address */
00986 
00987     tmp = ((phy_addr << 21) | (devad << 16) | reg |
00988            EMAC_MDIO_COMM_COMMAND_ADDRESS |
00989            EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY);
00990     REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, tmp);
00991 
00992     for (i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
00993         udelay(10);
00994 
00995         tmp = REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
00996         if (!(tmp & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)) {
00997             udelay(5);
00998             break;
00999         }
01000     }
01001     if (tmp & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY) {
01002         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "write phy register failed\n");
01003         rc = -EFAULT;
01004     } else {
01005         /* data */
01006         tmp = ((phy_addr << 21) | (devad << 16) | val |
01007                EMAC_MDIO_COMM_COMMAND_WRITE_45 |
01008                EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY);
01009         REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, tmp);
01010 
01011         for (i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
01012             udelay(10);
01013 
01014             tmp = REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl +
01015                      EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
01016             if (!(tmp & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)) {
01017                 udelay(5);
01018                 break;
01019             }
01020         }
01021         if (tmp & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY) {
01022             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "write phy register failed\n");
01023             rc = -EFAULT;
01024         }
01025     }
01026 
01027     /* Restore the saved mode */
01028     REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, saved_mode);
01029 
01030     return rc;
01031 }
01032 
01033 u8 bnx2x_cl45_read(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port, u32 ext_phy_type,
01034          u8 phy_addr, u8 devad, u16 reg, u16 *ret_val)
01035 {
01036     u32 val, saved_mode;
01037     u16 i;
01038     u8 rc = 0;
01039 
01040     u32 mdio_ctrl = bnx2x_get_emac_base(bp, ext_phy_type, port);
01041     /* set clause 45 mode, slow down the MDIO clock to 2.5MHz
01042      * (a value of 49==0x31) and make sure that the AUTO poll is off
01043      */
01044 
01045     saved_mode = REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
01046     val = saved_mode & ((EMAC_MDIO_MODE_AUTO_POLL |
01047                  EMAC_MDIO_MODE_CLOCK_CNT));
01048     val |= (EMAC_MDIO_MODE_CLAUSE_45 |
01049         (49L << EMAC_MDIO_MODE_CLOCK_CNT_BITSHIFT));
01050     REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, val);
01051     REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
01052     udelay(40);
01053 
01054     /* address */
01055     val = ((phy_addr << 21) | (devad << 16) | reg |
01056            EMAC_MDIO_COMM_COMMAND_ADDRESS |
01057            EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY);
01058     REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, val);
01059 
01060     for (i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
01061         udelay(10);
01062 
01063         val = REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
01064         if (!(val & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)) {
01065             udelay(5);
01066             break;
01067         }
01068     }
01069     if (val & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY) {
01070         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "read phy register failed\n");
01071 
01072         *ret_val = 0;
01073         rc = -EFAULT;
01074 
01075     } else {
01076         /* data */
01077         val = ((phy_addr << 21) | (devad << 16) |
01078                EMAC_MDIO_COMM_COMMAND_READ_45 |
01079                EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY);
01080         REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, val);
01081 
01082         for (i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
01083             udelay(10);
01084 
01085             val = REG_RD(bp, mdio_ctrl +
01086                       EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
01087             if (!(val & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)) {
01088                 *ret_val = (u16)(val & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_DATA);
01089                 break;
01090             }
01091         }
01092         if (val & EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY) {
01093             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "read phy register failed\n");
01094 
01095             *ret_val = 0;
01096             rc = -EFAULT;
01097         }
01098     }
01099 
01100     /* Restore the saved mode */
01101     REG_WR(bp, mdio_ctrl + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, saved_mode);
01102 
01103     return rc;
01104 }
01105 
01106 static void bnx2x_set_aer_mmd(struct link_params *params,
01107                 struct link_vars   *vars)
01108 {
01109     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01110     u32 ser_lane;
01111     u16 offset;
01112 
01113     ser_lane = ((params->lane_config &
01114              PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_MASK) >>
01115              PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_SHIFT);
01116 
01117     offset = (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) ?
01118         (params->phy_addr + ser_lane) : 0;
01119 
01120     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01121                   params->phy_addr,
01122                   MDIO_REG_BANK_AER_BLOCK,
01123                   MDIO_AER_BLOCK_AER_REG, 0x3800 + offset);
01124 }
01125 
01126 static void bnx2x_set_master_ln(struct link_params *params)
01127 {
01128     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01129     u16 new_master_ln, ser_lane;
01130     ser_lane =  ((params->lane_config &
01131              PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_MASK) >>
01132              PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_SHIFT);
01133 
01134     /* set the master_ln for AN */
01135     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01136                   params->phy_addr,
01137                   MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2,
01138                   MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_TEST_MODE_LANE,
01139                   &new_master_ln);
01140 
01141     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01142                   params->phy_addr,
01143                   MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2 ,
01144                   MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_TEST_MODE_LANE,
01145                   (new_master_ln | ser_lane));
01146 }
01147 
01148 static u8 bnx2x_reset_unicore(struct link_params *params)
01149 {
01150     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01151     u16 mii_control;
01152     u16 i;
01153 
01154     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01155                   params->phy_addr,
01156                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01157                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL, &mii_control);
01158 
01159     /* reset the unicore */
01160     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01161                   params->phy_addr,
01162                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01163                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
01164                   (mii_control |
01165                    MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_RESET));
01166     if (params->switch_cfg == SWITCH_CFG_1G)
01167         bnx2x_set_serdes_access(params);
01168 
01169     /* wait for the reset to self clear */
01170     for (i = 0; i < MDIO_ACCESS_TIMEOUT; i++) {
01171         udelay(5);
01172 
01173         /* the reset erased the previous bank value */
01174         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01175                       params->phy_addr,
01176                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01177                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
01178                   &mii_control);
01179 
01180         if (!(mii_control & MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_RESET)) {
01181             udelay(5);
01182             return 0;
01183         }
01184     }
01185 
01186     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BUG! XGXS is still in reset!\n");
01187     return -EINVAL;
01188 
01189 }
01190 
01191 static void bnx2x_set_swap_lanes(struct link_params *params)
01192 {
01193     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01194     /* Each two bits represents a lane number:
01195        No swap is 0123 => 0x1b no need to enable the swap */
01196     u16 ser_lane, rx_lane_swap, tx_lane_swap;
01197 
01198     ser_lane = ((params->lane_config &
01199              PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_MASK) >>
01200             PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_SHIFT);
01201     rx_lane_swap = ((params->lane_config &
01202                  PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_RX_MASK) >>
01203                 PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_RX_SHIFT);
01204     tx_lane_swap = ((params->lane_config &
01205                  PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_TX_MASK) >>
01206                 PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_TX_SHIFT);
01207 
01208     if (rx_lane_swap != 0x1b) {
01209         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01210                       params->phy_addr,
01211                     MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2,
01212                     MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_RX_LN_SWAP,
01213                     (rx_lane_swap |
01214                     MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_RX_LN_SWAP_ENABLE |
01215                     MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_RX_LN_SWAP_FORCE_ENABLE));
01216     } else {
01217         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01218                       params->phy_addr,
01219                       MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2,
01220                       MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_RX_LN_SWAP, 0);
01221     }
01222 
01223     if (tx_lane_swap != 0x1b) {
01224         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01225                       params->phy_addr,
01226                       MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2,
01227                       MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_TX_LN_SWAP,
01228                       (tx_lane_swap |
01229                        MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_TX_LN_SWAP_ENABLE));
01230     } else {
01231         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01232                       params->phy_addr,
01233                       MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2,
01234                       MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_TX_LN_SWAP, 0);
01235     }
01236 }
01237 
01238 static void bnx2x_set_parallel_detection(struct link_params *params,
01239                        u8            phy_flags)
01240 {
01241     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01242     u16 control2;
01243 
01244     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01245                   params->phy_addr,
01246                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01247                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL2,
01248                   &control2);
01249     if (params->speed_cap_mask & PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G)
01250         control2 |= MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL2_PRL_DT_EN;
01251     else
01252         control2 &= ~MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL2_PRL_DT_EN;
01253     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "params->speed_cap_mask = 0x%x, control2 = 0x%x\n",
01254         params->speed_cap_mask, control2);
01255     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01256                   params->phy_addr,
01257                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01258                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL2,
01259                   control2);
01260 
01261     if ((phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) &&
01262          (params->speed_cap_mask &
01263             PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10G)) {
01264         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS\n");
01265 
01266         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01267                       params->phy_addr,
01268                 MDIO_REG_BANK_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT,
01269                 MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_LINK,
01270                 MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_LINK_CNT);
01271 
01272         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01273                       params->phy_addr,
01274                 MDIO_REG_BANK_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT,
01275                 MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_CONTROL,
01276                 &control2);
01277 
01278 
01279         control2 |=
01280             MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_CONTROL_PARDET10G_EN;
01281 
01282         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01283                       params->phy_addr,
01284                 MDIO_REG_BANK_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT,
01285                 MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_CONTROL,
01286                 control2);
01287 
01288         /* Disable parallel detection of HiG */
01289         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01290                       params->phy_addr,
01291                 MDIO_REG_BANK_XGXS_BLOCK2,
01292                 MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_UNICORE_MODE_10G,
01293                 MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_UNICORE_MODE_10G_CX4_XGXS |
01294                 MDIO_XGXS_BLOCK2_UNICORE_MODE_10G_HIGIG_XGXS);
01295     }
01296 }
01297 
01298 static void bnx2x_set_autoneg(struct link_params *params,
01299                 struct link_vars *vars,
01300                 u8 enable_cl73)
01301 {
01302     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01303     u16 reg_val;
01304 
01305     /* CL37 Autoneg */
01306 
01307     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01308                   params->phy_addr,
01309                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01310                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL, &reg_val);
01311 
01312     /* CL37 Autoneg Enabled */
01313     if (vars->line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG)
01314         reg_val |= MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_AN_EN;
01315     else /* CL37 Autoneg Disabled */
01316         reg_val &= ~(MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_AN_EN |
01317                  MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_RESTART_AN);
01318 
01319     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01320                   params->phy_addr,
01321                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01322                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL, reg_val);
01323 
01324     /* Enable/Disable Autodetection */
01325 
01326     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01327                   params->phy_addr,
01328                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01329                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1, &reg_val);
01330     reg_val &= ~(MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_SIGNAL_DETECT_EN |
01331             MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_INVERT_SIGNAL_DETECT);
01332     reg_val |= MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_FIBER_MODE;
01333     if (vars->line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG)
01334         reg_val |= MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_AUTODET;
01335     else
01336         reg_val &= ~MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_AUTODET;
01337 
01338     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01339                   params->phy_addr,
01340                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01341                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1, reg_val);
01342 
01343     /* Enable TetonII and BAM autoneg */
01344     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01345                   params->phy_addr,
01346                   MDIO_REG_BANK_BAM_NEXT_PAGE,
01347                   MDIO_BAM_NEXT_PAGE_MP5_NEXT_PAGE_CTRL,
01348               &reg_val);
01349     if (vars->line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG) {
01350         /* Enable BAM aneg Mode and TetonII aneg Mode */
01351         reg_val |= (MDIO_BAM_NEXT_PAGE_MP5_NEXT_PAGE_CTRL_BAM_MODE |
01352                 MDIO_BAM_NEXT_PAGE_MP5_NEXT_PAGE_CTRL_TETON_AN);
01353     } else {
01354         /* TetonII and BAM Autoneg Disabled */
01355         reg_val &= ~(MDIO_BAM_NEXT_PAGE_MP5_NEXT_PAGE_CTRL_BAM_MODE |
01356                  MDIO_BAM_NEXT_PAGE_MP5_NEXT_PAGE_CTRL_TETON_AN);
01357     }
01358     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01359                   params->phy_addr,
01360                   MDIO_REG_BANK_BAM_NEXT_PAGE,
01361                   MDIO_BAM_NEXT_PAGE_MP5_NEXT_PAGE_CTRL,
01362                   reg_val);
01363 
01364     if (enable_cl73) {
01365         /* Enable Cl73 FSM status bits */
01366         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01367                       params->phy_addr,
01368                       MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_USERB0,
01369                       MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_UCTRL,
01370                       0xe);
01371 
01372         /* Enable BAM Station Manager*/
01373         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01374             params->phy_addr,
01375             MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_USERB0,
01376             MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_BAM_CTRL1,
01377             MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_BAM_CTRL1_BAM_EN |
01378             MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_BAM_CTRL1_BAM_STATION_MNGR_EN |
01379             MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_BAM_CTRL1_BAM_NP_AFTER_BP_EN);
01380 
01381         /* Advertise CL73 link speeds */
01382         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01383                           params->phy_addr,
01384                           MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB1,
01385                           MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV2,
01386                           &reg_val);
01387         if (params->speed_cap_mask &
01388             PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10G)
01389             reg_val |= MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV2_ADVR_10G_KX4;
01390         if (params->speed_cap_mask &
01391             PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G)
01392             reg_val |= MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV2_ADVR_1000M_KX;
01393 
01394         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01395                       params->phy_addr,
01396                       MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB1,
01397                       MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV2,
01398                       reg_val);
01399 
01400         /* CL73 Autoneg Enabled */
01401         reg_val = MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL_AN_EN;
01402 
01403     } else /* CL73 Autoneg Disabled */
01404         reg_val = 0;
01405 
01406     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01407                   params->phy_addr,
01408                   MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB0,
01409                   MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL, reg_val);
01410 }
01411 
01412 /* program SerDes, forced speed */
01413 static void bnx2x_program_serdes(struct link_params *params,
01414                    struct link_vars *vars)
01415 {
01416     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01417     u16 reg_val;
01418 
01419     /* program duplex, disable autoneg and sgmii*/
01420     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01421                   params->phy_addr,
01422                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01423                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL, &reg_val);
01424     reg_val &= ~(MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_FULL_DUPLEX |
01425              MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_AN_EN |
01426              MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_MAN_SGMII_SP_MASK);
01427     if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
01428         reg_val |= MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_FULL_DUPLEX;
01429     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01430                   params->phy_addr,
01431                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01432                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL, reg_val);
01433 
01434     /* program speed
01435        - needed only if the speed is greater than 1G (2.5G or 10G) */
01436     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01437                       params->phy_addr,
01438                       MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01439                       MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1, &reg_val);
01440     /* clearing the speed value before setting the right speed */
01441     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL = 0x%x\n", reg_val);
01442 
01443     reg_val &= ~(MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1_FORCE_SPEED_MASK |
01444              MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1_FORCE_SPEED_SEL);
01445 
01446     if (!((vars->line_speed == SPEED_1000) ||
01447           (vars->line_speed == SPEED_100) ||
01448           (vars->line_speed == SPEED_10))) {
01449 
01450         reg_val |= (MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1_REFCLK_SEL_156_25M |
01451                 MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1_FORCE_SPEED_SEL);
01452         if (vars->line_speed == SPEED_10000)
01453             reg_val |=
01454                 MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1_FORCE_SPEED_10G_CX4;
01455         if (vars->line_speed == SPEED_13000)
01456             reg_val |=
01457                 MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1_FORCE_SPEED_13G;
01458     }
01459 
01460     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01461                       params->phy_addr,
01462                       MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01463                       MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_MISC1, reg_val);
01464 
01465 }
01466 
01467 static void bnx2x_set_brcm_cl37_advertisment(struct link_params *params)
01468 {
01469     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01470     u16 val = 0;
01471 
01472     /* configure the 48 bits for BAM AN */
01473 
01474     /* set extended capabilities */
01475     if (params->speed_cap_mask & PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_2_5G)
01476         val |= MDIO_OVER_1G_UP1_2_5G;
01477     if (params->speed_cap_mask & PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10G)
01478         val |= MDIO_OVER_1G_UP1_10G;
01479     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01480                   params->phy_addr,
01481                   MDIO_REG_BANK_OVER_1G,
01482                   MDIO_OVER_1G_UP1, val);
01483 
01484     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01485                   params->phy_addr,
01486                   MDIO_REG_BANK_OVER_1G,
01487                   MDIO_OVER_1G_UP3, 0x400);
01488 }
01489 
01490 static void bnx2x_calc_ieee_aneg_adv(struct link_params *params, u16 *ieee_fc)
01491 {
01492     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01493     *ieee_fc = MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_FULL_DUPLEX;
01494     /* resolve pause mode and advertisement
01495      * Please refer to Table 28B-3 of the 802.3ab-1999 spec */
01496 
01497     switch (params->req_flow_ctrl) {
01498     case BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_AUTO:
01499         if (params->req_fc_auto_adv == BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_BOTH) {
01500             *ieee_fc |=
01501                  MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH;
01502         } else {
01503             *ieee_fc |=
01504                MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC;
01505         }
01506         break;
01507     case BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX:
01508         *ieee_fc |=
01509                MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC;
01510         break;
01511 
01512     case BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX:
01513     case BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_BOTH:
01514         *ieee_fc |= MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH;
01515         break;
01516 
01517     case BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE:
01518     default:
01519         *ieee_fc |= MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_NONE;
01520         break;
01521     }
01522     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "ieee_fc = 0x%x\n", *ieee_fc);
01523 }
01524 
01525 static void bnx2x_set_ieee_aneg_advertisment(struct link_params *params,
01526                        u16 ieee_fc)
01527 {
01528     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01529     u16 val;
01530     /* for AN, we are always publishing full duplex */
01531 
01532     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01533                   params->phy_addr,
01534                   MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01535                   MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV, ieee_fc);
01536     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01537                   params->phy_addr,
01538                   MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB1,
01539                   MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV1, &val);
01540     val &= ~MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV1_PAUSE_BOTH;
01541     val |= ((ieee_fc<<3) & MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV1_PAUSE_MASK);
01542     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01543                   params->phy_addr,
01544                   MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB1,
01545                   MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV1, val);
01546 }
01547 
01548 static void bnx2x_restart_autoneg(struct link_params *params, u8 enable_cl73)
01549 {
01550     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01551     u16 mii_control;
01552 
01553     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_restart_autoneg\n");
01554     /* Enable and restart BAM/CL37 aneg */
01555 
01556     if (enable_cl73) {
01557         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01558                       params->phy_addr,
01559                       MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB0,
01560                       MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL,
01561                       &mii_control);
01562 
01563         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01564                 params->phy_addr,
01565                 MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB0,
01566                 MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL,
01567                 (mii_control |
01568                 MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL_AN_EN |
01569                 MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL_RESTART_AN));
01570     } else {
01571 
01572         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01573                       params->phy_addr,
01574                       MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01575                       MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
01576                       &mii_control);
01577         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
01578              "bnx2x_restart_autoneg mii_control before = 0x%x\n",
01579              mii_control);
01580         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01581                       params->phy_addr,
01582                       MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01583                       MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
01584                       (mii_control |
01585                        MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_AN_EN |
01586                        MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_RESTART_AN));
01587     }
01588 }
01589 
01590 static void bnx2x_initialize_sgmii_process(struct link_params *params,
01591                      struct link_vars *vars)
01592 {
01593     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01594     u16 control1;
01595 
01596     /* in SGMII mode, the unicore is always slave */
01597 
01598     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01599                   params->phy_addr,
01600                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01601                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1,
01602               &control1);
01603     control1 |= MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_INVERT_SIGNAL_DETECT;
01604     /* set sgmii mode (and not fiber) */
01605     control1 &= ~(MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_FIBER_MODE |
01606               MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_AUTODET |
01607               MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1_MSTR_MODE);
01608     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01609                   params->phy_addr,
01610                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01611                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_CONTROL1,
01612                   control1);
01613 
01614     /* if forced speed */
01615     if (!(vars->line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG)) {
01616         /* set speed, disable autoneg */
01617         u16 mii_control;
01618 
01619         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01620                       params->phy_addr,
01621                       MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01622                       MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
01623                       &mii_control);
01624         mii_control &= ~(MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_AN_EN |
01625                  MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_MAN_SGMII_SP_MASK|
01626                  MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_FULL_DUPLEX);
01627 
01628         switch (vars->line_speed) {
01629         case SPEED_100:
01630             mii_control |=
01631                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_MAN_SGMII_SP_100;
01632             break;
01633         case SPEED_1000:
01634             mii_control |=
01635                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_MAN_SGMII_SP_1000;
01636             break;
01637         case SPEED_10:
01638             /* there is nothing to set for 10M */
01639             break;
01640         default:
01641             /* invalid speed for SGMII */
01642             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Invalid line_speed 0x%x\n",
01643                   vars->line_speed);
01644             break;
01645         }
01646 
01647         /* setting the full duplex */
01648         if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
01649             mii_control |=
01650                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_FULL_DUPLEX;
01651         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01652                       params->phy_addr,
01653                       MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01654                       MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
01655                       mii_control);
01656 
01657     } else { /* AN mode */
01658         /* enable and restart AN */
01659         bnx2x_restart_autoneg(params, 0);
01660     }
01661 }
01662 
01663 
01664 /*
01665  * link management
01666  */
01667 
01668 static void bnx2x_pause_resolve(struct link_vars *vars, u32 pause_result)
01669 {                       /*  LD      LP   */
01670     switch (pause_result) {         /* ASYM P ASYM P */
01671     case 0xb:                   /*   1  0   1  1 */
01672         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX;
01673         break;
01674 
01675     case 0xe:                   /*   1  1   1  0 */
01676         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX;
01677         break;
01678 
01679     case 0x5:                   /*   0  1   0  1 */
01680     case 0x7:                   /*   0  1   1  1 */
01681     case 0xd:                   /*   1  1   0  1 */
01682     case 0xf:                   /*   1  1   1  1 */
01683         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_BOTH;
01684         break;
01685 
01686     default:
01687         break;
01688     }
01689     if (pause_result & (1<<0))
01690         vars->link_status |= LINK_STATUS_LINK_PARTNER_SYMMETRIC_PAUSE;
01691     if (pause_result & (1<<1))
01692         vars->link_status |= LINK_STATUS_LINK_PARTNER_ASYMMETRIC_PAUSE;
01693 }
01694 
01695 static u8 bnx2x_ext_phy_resolve_fc(struct link_params *params,
01696                   struct link_vars *vars)
01697 {
01698     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01699     u8 ext_phy_addr;
01700     u16 ld_pause;       /* local */
01701     u16 lp_pause;       /* link partner */
01702     u16 pause_result;
01703     u8 ret = 0;
01704     u32 ext_phy_type;
01705     u8 port = params->port;
01706     ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
01707     ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
01708     /* read twice */
01709 
01710     if (vars->autoneg & AUTO_NEG_COMPLETE) {
01711         ret = 1;
01712         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
01713                   ext_phy_type,
01714                   ext_phy_addr,
01715                   MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01716                   MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE, &ld_pause);
01717         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
01718                   ext_phy_type,
01719                   ext_phy_addr,
01720                   MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01721                   MDIO_AN_REG_LP_AUTO_NEG, &lp_pause);
01722         pause_result = (ld_pause &
01723                 MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE_MASK) >> 8;
01724         pause_result |= (lp_pause &
01725                  MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE_MASK) >> 10;
01726         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Ext PHY pause result 0x%x \n",
01727            pause_result);
01728         bnx2x_pause_resolve(vars, pause_result);
01729         if (vars->flow_ctrl == BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE &&
01730              ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073) {
01731             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
01732                       ext_phy_type,
01733                       ext_phy_addr,
01734                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01735                       MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LD, &ld_pause);
01736 
01737             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
01738                       ext_phy_type,
01739                       ext_phy_addr,
01740                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01741                       MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LP, &lp_pause);
01742             pause_result = (ld_pause &
01743                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH) >> 5;
01744             pause_result |= (lp_pause &
01745                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH) >> 7;
01746 
01747             bnx2x_pause_resolve(vars, pause_result);
01748             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Ext PHY CL37 pause result 0x%x \n",
01749                  pause_result);
01750         }
01751     }
01752     return ret;
01753 }
01754 
01755 u8 bnx2x_direct_parallel_detect_used(struct link_params *params)
01756 {
01757     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01758     u16 pd_10g, status2_1000x;
01759     if (params->req_line_speed != SPEED_AUTO_NEG)
01760         return 0;
01761     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01762                   params->phy_addr,
01763                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01764                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_STATUS2,
01765                   &status2_1000x);
01766     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01767                   params->phy_addr,
01768                   MDIO_REG_BANK_SERDES_DIGITAL,
01769                   MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_STATUS2,
01770                   &status2_1000x);
01771     if (status2_1000x & MDIO_SERDES_DIGITAL_A_1000X_STATUS2_AN_DISABLED) {
01772         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "1G parallel detect link on port %d\n",
01773              params->port);
01774         return 1;
01775     }
01776 
01777     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01778                   params->phy_addr,
01779                   MDIO_REG_BANK_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT,
01780                   MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_STATUS,
01781                   &pd_10g);
01782 
01783     if (pd_10g & MDIO_10G_PARALLEL_DETECT_PAR_DET_10G_STATUS_PD_LINK) {
01784         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "10G parallel detect link on port %d\n",
01785              params->port);
01786         return 1;
01787     }
01788     return 0;
01789 }
01790 
01791 static void bnx2x_flow_ctrl_resolve(struct link_params *params,
01792                   struct link_vars *vars,
01793                   u32 gp_status)
01794 {
01795     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01796     u16 ld_pause;   /* local driver */
01797     u16 lp_pause;   /* link partner */
01798     u16 pause_result;
01799 
01800     vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
01801 
01802     /* resolve from gp_status in case of AN complete and not sgmii */
01803     if (params->req_flow_ctrl != BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_AUTO)
01804                 vars->flow_ctrl = params->req_flow_ctrl;
01805     else if (params->req_line_speed != SPEED_AUTO_NEG)
01806         vars->flow_ctrl = params->req_fc_auto_adv;
01807     else if (XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config) !=
01808          PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT)
01809         bnx2x_ext_phy_resolve_fc(params, vars);
01810     else if ((gp_status & MDIO_AN_CL73_OR_37_COMPLETE) &&
01811            (!(vars->phy_flags & PHY_SGMII_FLAG))) {
01812         if (bnx2x_direct_parallel_detect_used(params)) {
01813             vars->flow_ctrl = params->req_fc_auto_adv;
01814             return;
01815         }
01816         if ((gp_status &
01817             (MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_CL73_AUTONEG_COMPLETE |
01818              MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_CL73_MR_LP_NP_AN_ABLE)) ==
01819             (MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_CL73_AUTONEG_COMPLETE |
01820              MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_CL73_MR_LP_NP_AN_ABLE)) {
01821 
01822             CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01823                           params->phy_addr,
01824                           MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB1,
01825                           MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV1,
01826                           &ld_pause);
01827             CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01828                          params->phy_addr,
01829                          MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB1,
01830                          MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_LP_ADV1,
01831                          &lp_pause);
01832             pause_result = (ld_pause &
01833                     MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_ADV1_PAUSE_MASK)
01834                     >> 8;
01835             pause_result |= (lp_pause &
01836                     MDIO_CL73_IEEEB1_AN_LP_ADV1_PAUSE_MASK)
01837                     >> 10;
01838             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "pause_result CL73 0x%x\n",
01839                  pause_result);
01840         } else {
01841             CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01842                           params->phy_addr,
01843                           MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01844                           MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV,
01845                           &ld_pause);
01846             CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01847                           params->phy_addr,
01848                 MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
01849                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_LINK_PARTNER_ABILITY1,
01850                 &lp_pause);
01851             pause_result = (ld_pause &
01852                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_MASK)>>5;
01853             pause_result |= (lp_pause &
01854                 MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_MASK)>>7;
01855             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "pause_result CL37 0x%x\n",
01856                  pause_result);
01857         }
01858         bnx2x_pause_resolve(vars, pause_result);
01859     }
01860     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "flow_ctrl 0x%x\n", vars->flow_ctrl);
01861 }
01862 
01863 static void bnx2x_check_fallback_to_cl37(struct link_params *params)
01864 {
01865     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01866     u16 rx_status, ustat_val, cl37_fsm_recieved;
01867     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_check_fallback_to_cl37\n");
01868     /* Step 1: Make sure signal is detected */
01869     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01870                   params->phy_addr,
01871                   MDIO_REG_BANK_RX0,
01872                   MDIO_RX0_RX_STATUS,
01873                   &rx_status);
01874     if ((rx_status & MDIO_RX0_RX_STATUS_SIGDET) !=
01875         (MDIO_RX0_RX_STATUS_SIGDET)) {
01876         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Signal is not detected. Restoring CL73."
01877                  "rx_status(0x80b0) = 0x%x\n", rx_status);
01878         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01879                       params->phy_addr,
01880                       MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB0,
01881                       MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL,
01882                       MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL_AN_EN);
01883         return;
01884     }
01885     /* Step 2: Check CL73 state machine */
01886     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01887                   params->phy_addr,
01888                   MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_USERB0,
01889                   MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_USTAT1,
01890                   &ustat_val);
01891     if ((ustat_val &
01892          (MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_USTAT1_LINK_STATUS_CHECK |
01893           MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_USTAT1_AN_GOOD_CHECK_BAM37)) !=
01894         (MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_USTAT1_LINK_STATUS_CHECK |
01895           MDIO_CL73_USERB0_CL73_USTAT1_AN_GOOD_CHECK_BAM37)) {
01896         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "CL73 state-machine is not stable. "
01897                  "ustat_val(0x8371) = 0x%x\n", ustat_val);
01898         return;
01899     }
01900     /* Step 3: Check CL37 Message Pages received to indicate LP
01901     supports only CL37 */
01902     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01903                   params->phy_addr,
01904                   MDIO_REG_BANK_REMOTE_PHY,
01905                   MDIO_REMOTE_PHY_MISC_RX_STATUS,
01906                   &cl37_fsm_recieved);
01907     if ((cl37_fsm_recieved &
01908          (MDIO_REMOTE_PHY_MISC_RX_STATUS_CL37_FSM_RECEIVED_OVER1G_MSG |
01909          MDIO_REMOTE_PHY_MISC_RX_STATUS_CL37_FSM_RECEIVED_BRCM_OUI_MSG)) !=
01910         (MDIO_REMOTE_PHY_MISC_RX_STATUS_CL37_FSM_RECEIVED_OVER1G_MSG |
01911           MDIO_REMOTE_PHY_MISC_RX_STATUS_CL37_FSM_RECEIVED_BRCM_OUI_MSG)) {
01912         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "No CL37 FSM were received. "
01913                  "misc_rx_status(0x8330) = 0x%x\n",
01914              cl37_fsm_recieved);
01915         return;
01916     }
01917     /* The combined cl37/cl73 fsm state information indicating that we are
01918     connected to a device which does not support cl73, but does support
01919     cl37 BAM. In this case we disable cl73 and restart cl37 auto-neg */
01920     /* Disable CL73 */
01921     CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
01922                   params->phy_addr,
01923                   MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB0,
01924                   MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL,
01925                   0);
01926     /* Restart CL37 autoneg */
01927     bnx2x_restart_autoneg(params, 0);
01928     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Disabling CL73, and restarting CL37 autoneg\n");
01929 }
01930 static void bnx2x_an_resolve(struct link_params *params,
01931                    struct link_vars *vars,
01932                    u32 gp_status)
01933 
01934 {
01935     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
01936     u16 val;
01937     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
01938     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
01939     switch(ext_phy_type) {
01940     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
01941         if (gp_status & MDIO_AN_CL73_OR_37_COMPLETE) {
01942             vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_COMPLETE;
01943             vars->link_status |=
01944                 LINK_STATUS_AUTO_NEGOTIATE_COMPLETE;
01945         }
01946 
01947         if (bnx2x_direct_parallel_detect_used(params)) {
01948             vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_PARALLEL_DETECTION_USED;
01949             vars->link_status |=
01950                 LINK_STATUS_PARALLEL_DETECTION_USED;
01951         }
01952         break;
01953     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481:
01954     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
01955         if (vars->line_speed < SPEED_10000) {
01956             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
01957                       ext_phy_type,
01958                       ext_phy_addr,
01959                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01960                       MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_MII_STATUS,
01961                       &val);
01962             if (val & (1<<5)) {
01963                 vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_COMPLETE;
01964                 vars->link_status |=
01965                     LINK_STATUS_AUTO_NEGOTIATE_COMPLETE;
01966             }
01967             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
01968                       ext_phy_type,
01969                       ext_phy_addr,
01970                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01971                       MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_AN_EXPANSION,
01972                       &val);
01973             if ((val & (1<<0)) == 0) {
01974                 vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_PARALLEL_DETECTION_USED;
01975                 vars->link_status |=
01976                     LINK_STATUS_PARALLEL_DETECTION_USED;
01977             }
01978             break;
01979         };
01980         /* Else fall-through*/
01981     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
01982     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101:
01983         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
01984                   ext_phy_type,
01985                   ext_phy_addr,
01986                   MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01987                   MDIO_AN_REG_STATUS, &val);
01988         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
01989                   ext_phy_type,
01990                   ext_phy_addr,
01991                   MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
01992                   MDIO_AN_REG_STATUS, &val);
01993         if (val & (1<<5)) {
01994             vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_COMPLETE;
01995             vars->link_status |=
01996                 LINK_STATUS_AUTO_NEGOTIATE_COMPLETE;
01997         }
01998         if ((val & (1<<0)) == 0) {
01999             vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_PARALLEL_DETECTION_USED;
02000             vars->link_status |=
02001                 LINK_STATUS_PARALLEL_DETECTION_USED;
02002         }
02003         break;
02004     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
02005     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
02006         vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_COMPLETE;
02007         vars->link_status |= LINK_STATUS_AUTO_NEGOTIATE_COMPLETE;
02008         break;
02009     default:
02010         break;
02011     }
02012     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "AN result for port %d: 0x%x\n", params->port,
02013          vars->autoneg);
02014 }
02015 
02016 static u8 bnx2x_link_settings_status(struct link_params *params,
02017                    struct link_vars *vars,
02018                    u32 gp_status,
02019                    u8 ext_phy_link_up)
02020 {
02021     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02022     u16 new_line_speed;
02023     u8 rc = 0;
02024     vars->link_status = 0;
02025     vars->autoneg = 0;
02026     if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG) {
02027         vars->link_status |= LINK_STATUS_AUTO_NEGOTIATE_ENABLED;
02028         vars->autoneg |= AUTO_NEG_ENABLED;
02029     }
02030     if (gp_status & MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_LINK_STATUS) {
02031         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "phy link up gp_status=0x%x\n",
02032              gp_status);
02033 
02034         vars->phy_link_up = 1;
02035         vars->link_status |= LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP;
02036 
02037         if (gp_status & MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_DUPLEX_STATUS)
02038             vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
02039         else
02040             vars->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02041 
02042         if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG)
02043             bnx2x_an_resolve(params, vars, gp_status);
02044 
02045         bnx2x_flow_ctrl_resolve(params, vars, gp_status);
02046 
02047         switch (gp_status & GP_STATUS_SPEED_MASK) {
02048         case GP_STATUS_10M:
02049             new_line_speed = SPEED_10;
02050             if (vars->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
02051                 vars->link_status |= LINK_10TFD;
02052             else
02053                 vars->link_status |= LINK_10THD;
02054             break;
02055 
02056         case GP_STATUS_100M:
02057             new_line_speed = SPEED_100;
02058             if (vars->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
02059                 vars->link_status |= LINK_100TXFD;
02060             else
02061                 vars->link_status |= LINK_100TXHD;
02062             break;
02063 
02064         case GP_STATUS_1G:
02065         case GP_STATUS_1G_KX:
02066             new_line_speed = SPEED_1000;
02067             if (vars->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
02068                 vars->link_status |= LINK_1000TFD;
02069             else
02070                 vars->link_status |= LINK_1000THD;
02071             break;
02072 
02073         case GP_STATUS_2_5G:
02074             new_line_speed = SPEED_2500;
02075             if (vars->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
02076                 vars->link_status |= LINK_2500TFD;
02077             else
02078                 vars->link_status |= LINK_2500THD;
02079             break;
02080 
02081         case GP_STATUS_5G:
02082         case GP_STATUS_6G:
02083             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
02084                  "link speed unsupported  gp_status 0x%x\n",
02085                   gp_status);
02086             return -EINVAL;
02087 
02088         case GP_STATUS_10G_KX4:
02089         case GP_STATUS_10G_HIG:
02090         case GP_STATUS_10G_CX4:
02091             new_line_speed = SPEED_10000;
02092             vars->link_status |= LINK_10GTFD;
02093             break;
02094 
02095         case GP_STATUS_12G_HIG:
02096             new_line_speed = SPEED_12000;
02097             vars->link_status |= LINK_12GTFD;
02098             break;
02099 
02100         case GP_STATUS_12_5G:
02101             new_line_speed = SPEED_12500;
02102             vars->link_status |= LINK_12_5GTFD;
02103             break;
02104 
02105         case GP_STATUS_13G:
02106             new_line_speed = SPEED_13000;
02107             vars->link_status |= LINK_13GTFD;
02108             break;
02109 
02110         case GP_STATUS_15G:
02111             new_line_speed = SPEED_15000;
02112             vars->link_status |= LINK_15GTFD;
02113             break;
02114 
02115         case GP_STATUS_16G:
02116             new_line_speed = SPEED_16000;
02117             vars->link_status |= LINK_16GTFD;
02118             break;
02119 
02120         default:
02121             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
02122                   "link speed unsupported gp_status 0x%x\n",
02123                   gp_status);
02124             return -EINVAL;
02125         }
02126 
02127         /* Upon link speed change set the NIG into drain mode.
02128         Comes to deals with possible FIFO glitch due to clk change
02129         when speed is decreased without link down indicator */
02130         if (new_line_speed != vars->line_speed) {
02131             if (XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config) !=
02132                  PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT &&
02133                 ext_phy_link_up) {
02134                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Internal link speed %d is"
02135                         " different than the external"
02136                         " link speed %d\n", new_line_speed,
02137                       vars->line_speed);
02138                 vars->phy_link_up = 0;
02139                 return 0;
02140             }
02141             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE
02142                     + params->port*4, 0);
02143             msleep(1);
02144         }
02145         vars->line_speed = new_line_speed;
02146         if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX)
02147             vars->link_status |=
02148                 LINK_STATUS_TX_FLOW_CONTROL_ENABLED;
02149 
02150         if (vars->flow_ctrl & BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX)
02151             vars->link_status |=
02152                 LINK_STATUS_RX_FLOW_CONTROL_ENABLED;
02153 
02154         if (!ext_phy_link_up)
02155             vars->link_status = 0;
02156     } else { /* link_down */
02157         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "phy link down\n");
02158 
02159         vars->phy_link_up = 0;
02160 
02161         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
02162         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
02163         vars->autoneg = AUTO_NEG_DISABLED;
02164         vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_NONE;
02165 
02166         if ((params->req_line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG) &&
02167             ((XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config) ==
02168              PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT))) {
02169             /* Check signal is detected */
02170             bnx2x_check_fallback_to_cl37(params);
02171         }
02172     }
02173 
02174     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "gp_status 0x%x  phy_link_up %x line_speed %x \n",
02175          gp_status, vars->phy_link_up, vars->line_speed);
02176     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "duplex %x  flow_ctrl 0x%x"
02177          " autoneg 0x%x\n",
02178          vars->duplex,
02179          vars->flow_ctrl, vars->autoneg);
02180     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "link_status 0x%x\n", vars->link_status);
02181 
02182     return rc;
02183 }
02184 
02185 static void bnx2x_set_gmii_tx_driver(struct link_params *params)
02186 {
02187     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02188     u16 lp_up2;
02189     u16 tx_driver;
02190     u16 bank;
02191 
02192     /* read precomp */
02193     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
02194                   params->phy_addr,
02195                   MDIO_REG_BANK_OVER_1G,
02196                   MDIO_OVER_1G_LP_UP2, &lp_up2);
02197 
02198     /* bits [10:7] at lp_up2, positioned at [15:12] */
02199     lp_up2 = (((lp_up2 & MDIO_OVER_1G_LP_UP2_PREEMPHASIS_MASK) >>
02200            MDIO_OVER_1G_LP_UP2_PREEMPHASIS_SHIFT) <<
02201           MDIO_TX0_TX_DRIVER_PREEMPHASIS_SHIFT);
