02202 
02203     if (lp_up2 == 0)
02204         return;
02205 
02206     for (bank = MDIO_REG_BANK_TX0; bank <= MDIO_REG_BANK_TX3;
02207           bank += (MDIO_REG_BANK_TX1 - MDIO_REG_BANK_TX0)) {
02208         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
02209                       params->phy_addr,
02210                       bank,
02211                       MDIO_TX0_TX_DRIVER, &tx_driver);
02212 
02213         /* replace tx_driver bits [15:12] */
02214         if (lp_up2 !=
02215             (tx_driver & MDIO_TX0_TX_DRIVER_PREEMPHASIS_MASK)) {
02216             tx_driver &= ~MDIO_TX0_TX_DRIVER_PREEMPHASIS_MASK;
02217             tx_driver |= lp_up2;
02218             CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
02219                           params->phy_addr,
02220                           bank,
02221                           MDIO_TX0_TX_DRIVER, tx_driver);
02222         }
02223     }
02224 }
02225 
02226 static u8 bnx2x_emac_program(struct link_params *params,
02227                u32 line_speed, u32 duplex)
02228 {
02229     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02230     u8 port = params->port;
02231     u16 mode = 0;
02232 
02233     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "setting link speed & duplex\n");
02234     bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, GRCBASE_EMAC0 + port*0x400 +
02235              EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE,
02236              (EMAC_MODE_25G_MODE |
02237              EMAC_MODE_PORT_MII_10M |
02238              EMAC_MODE_HALF_DUPLEX));
02239     switch (line_speed) {
02240     case SPEED_10:
02241         mode |= EMAC_MODE_PORT_MII_10M;
02242         break;
02243 
02244     case SPEED_100:
02245         mode |= EMAC_MODE_PORT_MII;
02246         break;
02247 
02248     case SPEED_1000:
02249         mode |= EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII;
02250         break;
02251 
02252     case SPEED_2500:
02253         mode |= (EMAC_MODE_25G_MODE | EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII);
02254         break;
02255 
02256     default:
02257         /* 10G not valid for EMAC */
02258         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Invalid line_speed 0x%x\n", line_speed);
02259         return -EINVAL;
02260     }
02261 
02262     if (duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)
02263         mode |= EMAC_MODE_HALF_DUPLEX;
02264     bnx2x_bits_en(bp,
02265             GRCBASE_EMAC0 + port*0x400 + EMAC_REG_EMAC_MODE,
02266             mode);
02267 
02268     bnx2x_set_led(params, LED_MODE_OPER, line_speed);
02269     return 0;
02270 }
02271 
02272 /*****************************************************************************/
02273 /*                   External Phy section                    */
02274 /*****************************************************************************/
02275 void bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port)
02276 {
02277     bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_1,
02278                MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_LOW, port);
02279     msleep(1);
02280     bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_1,
02281               MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH, port);
02282 }
02283 
02284 static void bnx2x_ext_phy_reset(struct link_params *params,
02285                   struct link_vars   *vars)
02286 {
02287     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02288     u32 ext_phy_type;
02289     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02290 
02291     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Port %x: bnx2x_ext_phy_reset\n", params->port);
02292     ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
02293     /* The PHY reset is controled by GPIO 1
02294      * Give it 1ms of reset pulse
02295      */
02296     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
02297 
02298         switch (ext_phy_type) {
02299         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
02300             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS Direct\n");
02301             break;
02302 
02303         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705:
02304         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706:
02305             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8705/8706\n");
02306 
02307             /* Restore normal power mode*/
02308             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
02309                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02310                       params->port);
02311 
02312             /* HW reset */
02313             bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, params->port);
02314 
02315             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
02316                        ext_phy_type,
02317                        ext_phy_addr,
02318                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02319                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, 0xa040);
02320             break;
02321 
02322         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
02323             break;
02324 
02325         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
02326 
02327             /* Restore normal power mode*/
02328             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
02329                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02330                       params->port);
02331 
02332             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_1,
02333                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02334                       params->port);
02335 
02336             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
02337                        ext_phy_type,
02338                        ext_phy_addr,
02339                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02340                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
02341                        1<<15);
02342             break;
02343 
02344         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
02345             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8072\n");
02346 
02347             /* Unset Low Power Mode and SW reset */
02348             /* Restore normal power mode*/
02349             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
02350                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02351                       params->port);
02352 
02353             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
02354                        ext_phy_type,
02355                        ext_phy_addr,
02356                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02357                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
02358                        1<<15);
02359             break;
02360 
02361         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
02362             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8073\n");
02363 
02364             /* Restore normal power mode*/
02365             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
02366                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02367                       params->port);
02368 
02369             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_1,
02370                        MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02371                       params->port);
02372             break;
02373 
02374         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101:
02375             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS SFX7101\n");
02376 
02377             /* Restore normal power mode*/
02378             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
02379                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02380                       params->port);
02381 
02382             /* HW reset */
02383             bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, params->port);
02384             break;
02385 
02386         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481:
02387             /* Restore normal power mode*/
02388             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
02389                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH,
02390                       params->port);
02391 
02392             /* HW reset */
02393             bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, params->port);
02394 
02395             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
02396                        ext_phy_type,
02397                        ext_phy_addr,
02398                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02399                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
02400                        1<<15);
02401             break;
02402         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
02403             break;
02404         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_FAILURE:
02405             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS PHY Failure detected\n");
02406             break;
02407 
02408         default:
02409             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BAD XGXS ext_phy_config 0x%x\n",
02410                params->ext_phy_config);
02411             break;
02412         }
02413 
02414     } else { /* SerDes */
02415         ext_phy_type = SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
02416         switch (ext_phy_type) {
02417         case PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
02418             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes Direct\n");
02419             break;
02420 
02421         case PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM5482:
02422             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes 5482\n");
02423             bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, params->port);
02424             break;
02425 
02426         default:
02427             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BAD SerDes ext_phy_config 0x%x\n",
02428                  params->ext_phy_config);
02429             break;
02430         }
02431     }
02432 }
02433 
02434 static void bnx2x_save_spirom_version(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02435                     u32 shmem_base, u32 spirom_ver)
02436 {
02437     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "FW version 0x%x:0x%x for port %d\n",
02438          (u16)(spirom_ver>>16), (u16)spirom_ver, port);
02439     REG_WR(bp, shmem_base +
02440            offsetof(struct shmem_region,
02441                 port_mb[port].ext_phy_fw_version),
02442             spirom_ver);
02443 }
02444 
02445 static void bnx2x_save_bcm_spirom_ver(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02446                     u32 ext_phy_type, u8 ext_phy_addr,
02447                     u32 shmem_base)
02448 {
02449     u16 fw_ver1, fw_ver2;
02450 
02451     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02452               MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER1, &fw_ver1);
02453     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02454               MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2, &fw_ver2);
02455     bnx2x_save_spirom_version(bp, port, shmem_base,
02456                 (u32)(fw_ver1<<16 | fw_ver2));
02457 }
02458 
02459 
02460 static void bnx2x_save_8481_spirom_version(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02461                      u8 ext_phy_addr, u32 shmem_base)
02462 {
02463     u16 val, fw_ver1, fw_ver2, cnt;
02464     /* For the 32 bits registers in 8481, access via MDIO2ARM interface.*/
02465     /* (1) set register 0xc200_0014(SPI_BRIDGE_CTRL_2) to 0x03000000 */
02466     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02467                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02468                ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02469                0xA819, 0x0014);
02470     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02471                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02472                ext_phy_addr,
02473                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02474                0xA81A,
02475                0xc200);
02476     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02477                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02478                ext_phy_addr,
02479                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02480                0xA81B,
02481                0x0000);
02482     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02483                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02484                ext_phy_addr,
02485                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02486                0xA81C,
02487                0x0300);
02488     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02489                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02490                ext_phy_addr,
02491                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02492                0xA817,
02493                0x0009);
02494 
02495     for (cnt = 0; cnt < 100; cnt++) {
02496         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02497                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02498                   ext_phy_addr,
02499                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02500                   0xA818,
02501                   &val);
02502         if (val & 1)
02503             break;
02504         udelay(5);
02505     }
02506     if (cnt == 100) {
02507         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Unable to read 8481 phy fw version(1)\n");
02508         bnx2x_save_spirom_version(bp, port,
02509                     shmem_base, 0);
02510         return;
02511     }
02512 
02513 
02514     /* 2) read register 0xc200_0000 (SPI_FW_STATUS) */
02515     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02516                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02517                ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02518                0xA819, 0x0000);
02519     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02520                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02521                ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02522                0xA81A, 0xc200);
02523     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02524                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02525                ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02526                0xA817, 0x000A);
02527     for (cnt = 0; cnt < 100; cnt++) {
02528         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02529                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02530                   ext_phy_addr,
02531                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02532                   0xA818,
02533                   &val);
02534         if (val & 1)
02535             break;
02536         udelay(5);
02537     }
02538     if (cnt == 100) {
02539         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Unable to read 8481 phy fw version(2)\n");
02540         bnx2x_save_spirom_version(bp, port,
02541                     shmem_base, 0);
02542         return;
02543     }
02544 
02545     /* lower 16 bits of the register SPI_FW_STATUS */
02546     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02547               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02548               ext_phy_addr,
02549               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02550               0xA81B,
02551               &fw_ver1);
02552     /* upper 16 bits of register SPI_FW_STATUS */
02553     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02554               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
02555               ext_phy_addr,
02556               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02557               0xA81C,
02558               &fw_ver2);
02559 
02560     bnx2x_save_spirom_version(bp, port,
02561                 shmem_base, (fw_ver2<<16) | fw_ver1);
02562 }
02563 
02564 static void bnx2x_bcm8072_external_rom_boot(struct link_params *params)
02565 {
02566     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02567     u8 port = params->port;
02568     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02569     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
02570 
02571     /* Need to wait 200ms after reset */
02572     msleep(200);
02573     /* Boot port from external ROM
02574      * Set ser_boot_ctl bit in the MISC_CTRL1 register
02575      */
02576     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02577                 MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02578                 MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL1, 0x0001);
02579 
02580     /* Reset internal microprocessor */
02581     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02582               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02583               MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02584               MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_RESET_INTERNAL_MP);
02585     /* set micro reset = 0 */
02586     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02587                 MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02588                 MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02589                 MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_MICRO_RESET);
02590     /* Reset internal microprocessor */
02591     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02592               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02593               MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02594               MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_RESET_INTERNAL_MP);
02595     /* wait for 100ms for code download via SPI port */
02596     msleep(100);
02597 
02598     /* Clear ser_boot_ctl bit */
02599     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02600                 MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02601                 MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL1, 0x0000);
02602     /* Wait 100ms */
02603     msleep(100);
02604 
02605     bnx2x_save_bcm_spirom_ver(bp, port,
02606                 ext_phy_type,
02607                 ext_phy_addr,
02608                 params->shmem_base);
02609 }
02610 
02611 static u8 bnx2x_8073_is_snr_needed(struct link_params *params)
02612 {
02613     /* This is only required for 8073A1, version 102 only */
02614 
02615     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02616     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02617     u16 val;
02618 
02619     /* Read 8073 HW revision*/
02620     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
02621               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
02622               ext_phy_addr,
02623               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02624               MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_CHIP_REV, &val);
02625 
02626     if (val != 1) {
02627         /* No need to workaround in 8073 A1 */
02628         return 0;
02629     }
02630 
02631     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
02632               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
02633               ext_phy_addr,
02634               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02635               MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2, &val);
02636 
02637     /* SNR should be applied only for version 0x102 */
02638     if (val != 0x102)
02639         return 0;
02640 
02641     return 1;
02642 }
02643 
02644 static u8 bnx2x_bcm8073_xaui_wa(struct link_params *params)
02645 {
02646     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02647     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02648     u16 val, cnt, cnt1 ;
02649 
02650     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
02651               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
02652               ext_phy_addr,
02653               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02654               MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_CHIP_REV, &val);
02655 
02656     if (val > 0) {
02657         /* No need to workaround in 8073 A1 */
02658         return 0;
02659     }
02660     /* XAUI workaround in 8073 A0: */
02661 
02662     /* After loading the boot ROM and restarting Autoneg,
02663     poll Dev1, Reg $C820: */
02664 
02665     for (cnt = 0; cnt < 1000; cnt++) {
02666         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
02667                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
02668                   ext_phy_addr,
02669                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02670                   MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_SPEED_LINK_STATUS,
02671                   &val);
02672           /* If bit [14] = 0 or bit [13] = 0, continue on with
02673            system initialization (XAUI work-around not required,
02674             as these bits indicate 2.5G or 1G link up). */
02675         if (!(val & (1<<14)) || !(val & (1<<13))) {
02676             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XAUI work-around not required\n");
02677             return 0;
02678         } else if (!(val & (1<<15))) {
02679             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "clc bit 15 went off\n");
02680              /* If bit 15 is 0, then poll Dev1, Reg $C841 until
02681               it's MSB (bit 15) goes to 1 (indicating that the
02682               XAUI workaround has completed),
02683               then continue on with system initialization.*/
02684             for (cnt1 = 0; cnt1 < 1000; cnt1++) {
02685                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
02686                     PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
02687                     ext_phy_addr,
02688                     MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02689                     MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_XAUI_WA, &val);
02690                 if (val & (1<<15)) {
02691                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
02692                       "XAUI workaround has completed\n");
02693                     return 0;
02694                  }
02695                  msleep(3);
02696             }
02697             break;
02698         }
02699         msleep(3);
02700     }
02701     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Warning: XAUI work-around timeout !!!\n");
02702     return -EINVAL;
02703 }
02704 
02705 static void bnx2x_bcm8073_bcm8727_external_rom_boot(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02706                           u8 ext_phy_addr,
02707                           u32 ext_phy_type,
02708                           u32 shmem_base)
02709 {
02710     /* Boot port from external ROM  */
02711     /* EDC grst */
02712     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02713                ext_phy_type,
02714                ext_phy_addr,
02715                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02716                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02717                0x0001);
02718 
02719     /* ucode reboot and rst */
02720     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02721                ext_phy_type,
02722                ext_phy_addr,
02723                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02724                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02725                0x008c);
02726 
02727     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02728                ext_phy_type,
02729                ext_phy_addr,
02730                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02731                MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL1, 0x0001);
02732 
02733     /* Reset internal microprocessor */
02734     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02735                ext_phy_type,
02736                ext_phy_addr,
02737                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02738                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02739                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_MICRO_RESET);
02740 
02741     /* Release srst bit */
02742     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02743                ext_phy_type,
02744                ext_phy_addr,
02745                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02746                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02747                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_RESET_INTERNAL_MP);
02748 
02749     /* wait for 100ms for code download via SPI port */
02750     msleep(100);
02751 
02752     /* Clear ser_boot_ctl bit */
02753     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02754                ext_phy_type,
02755                ext_phy_addr,
02756                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02757                MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL1, 0x0000);
02758 
02759     bnx2x_save_bcm_spirom_ver(bp, port,
02760                 ext_phy_type,
02761                 ext_phy_addr,
02762                 shmem_base);
02763 }
02764 
02765 static void bnx2x_bcm8073_external_rom_boot(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02766                       u8 ext_phy_addr,
02767                       u32 shmem_base)
02768 {
02769     bnx2x_bcm8073_bcm8727_external_rom_boot(bp, port, ext_phy_addr,
02770                      PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
02771                      shmem_base);
02772 }
02773 
02774 static void bnx2x_bcm8727_external_rom_boot(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02775                       u8 ext_phy_addr,
02776                       u32 shmem_base)
02777 {
02778     bnx2x_bcm8073_bcm8727_external_rom_boot(bp, port, ext_phy_addr,
02779                      PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
02780                      shmem_base);
02781 
02782 }
02783 
02784 static void bnx2x_bcm8726_external_rom_boot(struct link_params *params)
02785 {
02786     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02787     u8 port = params->port;
02788     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02789     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
02790 
02791     /* Need to wait 100ms after reset */
02792     msleep(100);
02793 
02794     /* Micro controller re-boot */
02795     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02796                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02797                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02798                0x018B);
02799 
02800     /* Set soft reset */
02801     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02802                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02803                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02804                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_MICRO_RESET);
02805 
02806     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02807                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02808                MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL1, 0x0001);
02809 
02810     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02811                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02812                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL,
02813                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL_ROM_RESET_INTERNAL_MP);
02814 
02815     /* wait for 150ms for microcode load */
02816     msleep(150);
02817 
02818     /* Disable serial boot control, tristates pins SS_N, SCK, MOSI, MISO */
02819     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
02820                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02821                MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL1, 0x0000);
02822 
02823     msleep(200);
02824     bnx2x_save_bcm_spirom_ver(bp, port,
02825                 ext_phy_type,
02826                 ext_phy_addr,
02827                 params->shmem_base);
02828 }
02829 
02830 static void bnx2x_sfp_set_transmitter(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
02831                     u32 ext_phy_type, u8 ext_phy_addr,
02832                     u8 tx_en)
02833 {
02834     u16 val;
02835 
02836     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting transmitter tx_en=%x for port %x\n",
02837          tx_en, port);
02838     /* Disable/Enable transmitter ( TX laser of the SFP+ module.)*/
02839     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02840               ext_phy_type,
02841               ext_phy_addr,
02842               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02843               MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
02844               &val);
02845 
02846     if (tx_en)
02847         val &= ~(1<<15);
02848     else
02849         val |= (1<<15);
02850 
02851     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02852                ext_phy_type,
02853                ext_phy_addr,
02854                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02855                MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
02856                val);
02857 }
02858 
02859 static u8 bnx2x_8726_read_sfp_module_eeprom(struct link_params *params,
02860                       u16 addr, u8 byte_cnt, u8 *o_buf)
02861 {
02862     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02863     u16 val = 0;
02864     u16 i;
02865     u8 port = params->port;
02866     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02867     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
02868 
02869     if (byte_cnt > 16) {
02870         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Reading from eeprom is"
02871                 " is limited to 0xf\n");
02872         return -EINVAL;
02873     }
02874     /* Set the read command byte count */
02875     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02876                ext_phy_type,
02877                ext_phy_addr,
02878                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02879                MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_BYTE_CNT,
02880                (byte_cnt | 0xa000));
02881 
02882     /* Set the read command address */
02883     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02884                ext_phy_type,
02885                ext_phy_addr,
02886                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02887                MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_MEM_ADDR,
02888                addr);
02889 
02890     /* Activate read command */
02891     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02892                ext_phy_type,
02893                ext_phy_addr,
02894                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02895                MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL,
02896                0x2c0f);
02897 
02898     /* Wait up to 500us for command complete status */
02899     for (i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
02900         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02901                   ext_phy_type,
02902                   ext_phy_addr,
02903                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02904                   MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL, &val);
02905         if ((val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK) ==
02906             MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_STATUS_COMPLETE)
02907             break;
02908         udelay(5);
02909     }
02910 
02911     if ((val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK) !=
02912             MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_STATUS_COMPLETE) {
02913         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
02914              "Got bad status 0x%x when reading from SFP+ EEPROM\n",
02915              (val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK));
02916         return -EINVAL;
02917     }
02918 
02919     /* Read the buffer */
02920     for (i = 0; i < byte_cnt; i++) {
02921         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02922                   ext_phy_type,
02923                   ext_phy_addr,
02924                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02925                   MDIO_PMA_REG_8726_TWO_WIRE_DATA_BUF + i, &val);
02926         o_buf[i] = (u8)(val & MDIO_PMA_REG_8726_TWO_WIRE_DATA_MASK);
02927     }
02928 
02929     for (i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
02930         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02931                   ext_phy_type,
02932                   ext_phy_addr,
02933                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02934                   MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL, &val);
02935         if ((val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK) ==
02936             MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_STATUS_IDLE)
02937             return 0;;
02938         msleep(1);
02939     }
02940     return -EINVAL;
02941 }
02942 
02943 static u8 bnx2x_8727_read_sfp_module_eeprom(struct link_params *params,
02944                       u16 addr, u8 byte_cnt, u8 *o_buf)
02945 {
02946     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
02947     u16 val, i;
02948     u8 port = params->port;
02949     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
02950     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
02951 
02952     if (byte_cnt > 16) {
02953         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Reading from eeprom is"
02954                 " is limited to 0xf\n");
02955         return -EINVAL;
02956     }
02957 
02958     /* Need to read from 1.8000 to clear it */
02959     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
02960               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
02961               ext_phy_addr,
02962               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02963               MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL,
02964               &val);
02965 
02966     /* Set the read command byte count */
02967     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02968                ext_phy_type,
02969                ext_phy_addr,
02970                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02971                MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_BYTE_CNT,
02972                ((byte_cnt < 2) ? 2 : byte_cnt));
02973 
02974     /* Set the read command address */
02975     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02976                ext_phy_type,
02977                ext_phy_addr,
02978                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02979                MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_MEM_ADDR,
02980                addr);
02981     /* Set the destination address */
02982     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02983                ext_phy_type,
02984                ext_phy_addr,
02985                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02986                0x8004,
02987                MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_TWO_WIRE_DATA_BUF);
02988 
02989     /* Activate read command */
02990     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
02991                ext_phy_type,
02992                ext_phy_addr,
02993                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
02994                MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL,
02995                0x8002);
02996     /* Wait appropriate time for two-wire command to finish before
02997     polling the status register */
02998     msleep(1);
02999 
03000     /* Wait up to 500us for command complete status */
03001     for (i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
03002         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
03003                   ext_phy_type,
03004                   ext_phy_addr,
03005                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03006                   MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL, &val);
03007         if ((val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK) ==
03008             MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_STATUS_COMPLETE)
03009             break;
03010         udelay(5);
03011     }
03012 
03013     if ((val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK) !=
03014             MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_STATUS_COMPLETE) {
03015         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
03016              "Got bad status 0x%x when reading from SFP+ EEPROM\n",
03017              (val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK));
03018         return -EINVAL;
03019     }
03020 
03021     /* Read the buffer */
03022     for (i = 0; i < byte_cnt; i++) {
03023         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
03024                   ext_phy_type,
03025                   ext_phy_addr,
03026                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03027                   MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_TWO_WIRE_DATA_BUF + i, &val);
03028         o_buf[i] = (u8)(val & MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_TWO_WIRE_DATA_MASK);
03029     }
03030 
03031     for (i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
03032         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
03033                   ext_phy_type,
03034                   ext_phy_addr,
03035                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03036                   MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL, &val);
03037         if ((val & MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_CTRL_STATUS_MASK) ==
03038             MDIO_PMA_REG_SFP_TWO_WIRE_STATUS_IDLE)
03039             return 0;;
03040         msleep(1);
03041     }
03042 
03043     return -EINVAL;
03044 }
03045 
03046 u8 bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(struct link_params *params, u16 addr,
03047                      u8 byte_cnt, u8 *o_buf)
03048 {
03049     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03050 
03051     if (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726)
03052         return bnx2x_8726_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params, addr,
03053                                byte_cnt, o_buf);
03054     else if (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727)
03055         return bnx2x_8727_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params, addr,
03056                                byte_cnt, o_buf);
03057     return -EINVAL;
03058 }
03059 
03060 static u8 bnx2x_get_edc_mode(struct link_params *params,
03061                   u16 *edc_mode)
03062 {
03063     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03064     u8 val, check_limiting_mode = 0;
03065     *edc_mode = EDC_MODE_LIMITING;
03066 
03067     /* First check for copper cable */
03068     if (bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params,
03069                        SFP_EEPROM_CON_TYPE_ADDR,
03070                        1,
03071                        &val) != 0) {
03072         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Failed to read from SFP+ module EEPROM\n");
03073         return -EINVAL;
03074     }
03075 
03076     switch (val) {
03077     case SFP_EEPROM_CON_TYPE_VAL_COPPER:
03078     {
03079         u8 copper_module_type;
03080 
03081         /* Check if its active cable( includes SFP+ module)
03082         of passive cable*/
03083         if (bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params,
03084                            SFP_EEPROM_FC_TX_TECH_ADDR,
03085                            1,
03086                            &copper_module_type) !=
03087             0) {
03088             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
03089                 "Failed to read copper-cable-type"
03090                 " from SFP+ EEPROM\n");
03091             return -EINVAL;
03092         }
03093 
03094         if (copper_module_type &
03095             SFP_EEPROM_FC_TX_TECH_BITMASK_COPPER_ACTIVE) {
03096             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Active Copper cable detected\n");
03097             check_limiting_mode = 1;
03098         } else if (copper_module_type &
03099             SFP_EEPROM_FC_TX_TECH_BITMASK_COPPER_PASSIVE) {
03100                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Passive Copper"
03101                         " cable detected\n");
03102                 *edc_mode =
03103                       EDC_MODE_PASSIVE_DAC;
03104         } else {
03105             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Unknown copper-cable-"
03106                      "type 0x%x !!!\n", copper_module_type);
03107             return -EINVAL;
03108         }
03109         break;
03110     }
03111     case SFP_EEPROM_CON_TYPE_VAL_LC:
03112         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Optic module detected\n");
03113         check_limiting_mode = 1;
03114         break;
03115     default:
03116         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Unable to determine module type 0x%x !!!\n",
03117              val);
03118         return -EINVAL;
03119     }
03120 
03121     if (check_limiting_mode) {
03122         u8 options[SFP_EEPROM_OPTIONS_SIZE];
03123         if (bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params,
03124                            SFP_EEPROM_OPTIONS_ADDR,
03125                            SFP_EEPROM_OPTIONS_SIZE,
03126                            options) != 0) {
03127             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Failed to read Option"
03128                 " field from module EEPROM\n");
03129             return -EINVAL;
03130         }
03131         if ((options[0] & SFP_EEPROM_OPTIONS_LINEAR_RX_OUT_MASK))
03132             *edc_mode = EDC_MODE_LINEAR;
03133         else
03134             *edc_mode = EDC_MODE_LIMITING;
03135     }
03136     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "EDC mode is set to 0x%x\n", *edc_mode);
03137     return 0;
03138 }
03139 
03140 /* This function read the relevant field from the module ( SFP+ ),
03141     and verify it is compliant with this board */
03142 static u8 bnx2x_verify_sfp_module(struct link_params *params)
03143 {
03144     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03145     u32 val;
03146     u32 fw_resp;
03147     char vendor_name[SFP_EEPROM_VENDOR_NAME_SIZE+1];
03148     char vendor_pn[SFP_EEPROM_PART_NO_SIZE+1];
03149 
03150     val = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
03151              offsetof(struct shmem_region, dev_info.
03152                   port_feature_config[params->port].config));
03153     if ((val & PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_MASK) ==
03154         PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_NO_ENFORCEMENT) {
03155         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "NOT enforcing module verification\n");
03156         return 0;
03157     }
03158 
03159     /* Ask the FW to validate the module */
03160     if (!(params->feature_config_flags &
03161           FEATURE_CONFIG_BC_SUPPORTS_OPT_MDL_VRFY)) {
03162         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "FW does not support OPT MDL "
03163                 "verification\n");
03164         return -EINVAL;
03165     }
03166 
03167     fw_resp = bnx2x_fw_command(bp, DRV_MSG_CODE_VRFY_OPT_MDL);
03168     if (fw_resp == FW_MSG_CODE_VRFY_OPT_MDL_SUCCESS) {
03169         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Approved module\n");
03170         return 0;
03171     }
03172 
03173     /* format the warning message */
03174     if (bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params,
03175                        SFP_EEPROM_VENDOR_NAME_ADDR,
03176                        SFP_EEPROM_VENDOR_NAME_SIZE,
03177                        (u8 *)vendor_name))
03178         vendor_name[0] = '\0';
03179     else
03180         vendor_name[SFP_EEPROM_VENDOR_NAME_SIZE] = '\0';
03181     if (bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params,
03182                        SFP_EEPROM_PART_NO_ADDR,
03183                        SFP_EEPROM_PART_NO_SIZE,
03184                        (u8 *)vendor_pn))
03185         vendor_pn[0] = '\0';
03186     else
03187         vendor_pn[SFP_EEPROM_PART_NO_SIZE] = '\0';
03188 
03189     printk(KERN_INFO PFX  "Warning: "
03190              "Unqualified SFP+ module "
03191              "detected on %s, Port %d from %s part number %s\n"
03192             , bp->dev->name, params->port,
03193             vendor_name, vendor_pn);
03194     return -EINVAL;
03195 }
03196 
03197 static u8 bnx2x_bcm8726_set_limiting_mode(struct link_params *params,
03198                     u16 edc_mode)
03199 {
03200     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03201     u8 port = params->port;
03202     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03203     u16 cur_limiting_mode;
03204 
03205     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
03206               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726,
03207               ext_phy_addr,
03208               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03209               MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2,
03210               &cur_limiting_mode);
03211     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Current Limiting mode is 0x%x\n",
03212          cur_limiting_mode);
03213 
03214     if (edc_mode == EDC_MODE_LIMITING) {
03215         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
03216              "Setting LIMITING MODE\n");
03217         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03218                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726,
03219                    ext_phy_addr,
03220                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03221                    MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2,
03222                    EDC_MODE_LIMITING);
03223     } else { /* LRM mode ( default )*/
03224 
03225         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting LRM MODE\n");
03226 
03227         /* Changing to LRM mode takes quite few seconds.
03228         So do it only if current mode is limiting
03229         ( default is LRM )*/
03230         if (cur_limiting_mode != EDC_MODE_LIMITING)
03231             return 0;
03232 
03233         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03234                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726,
03235                    ext_phy_addr,
03236                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03237                    MDIO_PMA_REG_LRM_MODE,
03238                    0);
03239         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03240                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726,
03241                    ext_phy_addr,
03242                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03243                    MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2,
03244                    0x128);
03245         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03246                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726,
03247                    ext_phy_addr,
03248                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03249                    MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL0,
03250                    0x4008);
03251         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03252                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726,
03253                    ext_phy_addr,
03254                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03255                    MDIO_PMA_REG_LRM_MODE,
03256                    0xaaaa);
03257     }
03258     return 0;
03259 }
03260 
03261 static u8 bnx2x_bcm8727_set_limiting_mode(struct link_params *params,
03262                     u16 edc_mode)
03263 {
03264     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03265     u8 port = params->port;
03266     u16 phy_identifier;
03267     u16 rom_ver2_val;
03268     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03269 
03270     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
03271                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
03272                ext_phy_addr,
03273                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03274                MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
03275                &phy_identifier);
03276 
03277     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03278                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
03279                ext_phy_addr,
03280                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03281                MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
03282                (phy_identifier & ~(1<<9)));
03283 
03284     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
03285               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
03286               ext_phy_addr,
03287               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03288               MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2,
03289               &rom_ver2_val);
03290     /* Keep the MSB 8-bits, and set the LSB 8-bits with the edc_mode */
03291     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03292                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
03293                ext_phy_addr,
03294                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03295                MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER2,
03296                (rom_ver2_val & 0xff00) | (edc_mode & 0x00ff));
03297 
03298     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03299                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
03300                ext_phy_addr,
03301                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03302                MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
03303                (phy_identifier | (1<<9)));
03304 
03305     return 0;
03306 }
03307 
03308 
03309 static u8 bnx2x_wait_for_sfp_module_initialized(struct link_params *params)
03310 {
03311     u8 val;
03312     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03313     u16 timeout;
03314     /* Initialization time after hot-plug may take up to 300ms for some
03315     phys type ( e.g. JDSU ) */
03316     for (timeout = 0; timeout < 60; timeout++) {
03317         if (bnx2x_read_sfp_module_eeprom(params, 1, 1, &val)
03318             == 0) {
03319             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SFP+ module initialization "
03320                      "took %d ms\n", timeout * 5);
03321             return 0;
03322         }
03323         msleep(5);
03324     }
03325     return -EINVAL;
03326 }
03327 
03328 static void bnx2x_8727_power_module(struct bnx2x *bp,
03329                   struct link_params *params,
03330                   u8 ext_phy_addr, u8 is_power_up) {
03331     /* Make sure GPIOs are not using for LED mode */
03332     u16 val;
03333     u8 port = params->port;
03334     /*
03335      * In the GPIO register, bit 4 is use to detemine if the GPIOs are
03336      * operating as INPUT or as OUTPUT. Bit 1 is for input, and 0 for
03337      * output
03338      * Bits 0-1 determine the gpios value for OUTPUT in case bit 4 val is 0
03339      * Bits 8-9 determine the gpios value for INPUT in case bit 4 val is 1
03340      * where the 1st bit is the over-current(only input), and 2nd bit is
03341      * for power( only output )
03342     */
03343 
03344     /*
03345      * In case of NOC feature is disabled and power is up, set GPIO control
03346      *  as input to enable listening of over-current indication
03347      */
03348 
03349     if (!(params->feature_config_flags &
03350           FEATURE_CONFIG_BCM8727_NOC) && is_power_up)
03351         val = (1<<4);
03352     else
03353         /*
03354          * Set GPIO control to OUTPUT, and set the power bit
03355          * to according to the is_power_up
03356          */
03357         val = ((!(is_power_up)) << 1);
03358 
03359     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
03360                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
03361                ext_phy_addr,
03362                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03363                MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_GPIO_CTRL,
03364                val);
03365 }
03366 
03367 static u8 bnx2x_sfp_module_detection(struct link_params *params)
03368 {
03369     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03370     u16 edc_mode;
03371     u8 rc = 0;
03372     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03373     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03374     u32 val = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
03375                  offsetof(struct shmem_region, dev_info.
03376                      port_feature_config[params->port].config));
03377 
03378     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SFP+ module plugged in/out detected on port %d\n",
03379          params->port);
03380 
03381     if (bnx2x_get_edc_mode(params, &edc_mode) != 0) {
03382         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Failed to get valid module type\n");
03383         return -EINVAL;
03384     } else if (bnx2x_verify_sfp_module(params) !=
03385            0) {
03386         /* check SFP+ module compatibility */
03387         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Module verification failed!!\n");
03388         rc = -EINVAL;
03389         /* Turn on fault module-detected led */
03390         bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_0,
03391                   MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_HIGH,
03392                   params->port);
03393         if ((ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727) &&
03394             ((val & PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_MASK) ==
03395              PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_POWER_DOWN)) {
03396             /* Shutdown SFP+ module */
03397             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Shutdown SFP+ module!!\n");
03398             bnx2x_8727_power_module(bp, params,
03399                           ext_phy_addr, 0);
03400             return rc;
03401         }
03402     } else {
03403         /* Turn off fault module-detected led */
03404         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Turn off fault module-detected led\n");
03405         bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_0,
03406                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_LOW,
03407                       params->port);
03408     }
03409 
03410     /* power up the SFP module */
03411     if (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727)
03412         bnx2x_8727_power_module(bp, params, ext_phy_addr, 1);
03413 
03414     /* Check and set limiting mode / LRM mode on 8726.
03415     On 8727 it is done automatically */
03416     if (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726)
03417         bnx2x_bcm8726_set_limiting_mode(params, edc_mode);
03418     else
03419         bnx2x_bcm8727_set_limiting_mode(params, edc_mode);
03420     /*
03421      * Enable transmit for this module if the module is approved, or
03422      * if unapproved modules should also enable the Tx laser
03423      */
03424     if (rc == 0 ||
03425         (val & PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_MASK) !=
03426         PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_DISABLE_TX_LASER)
03427         bnx2x_sfp_set_transmitter(bp, params->port,
03428                     ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr, 1);
03429     else
03430         bnx2x_sfp_set_transmitter(bp, params->port,
03431                     ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr, 0);
03432 
03433     return rc;
03434 }
03435 
03436 void bnx2x_handle_module_detect_int(struct link_params *params)
03437 {
03438     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03439     u32 gpio_val;
03440     u8 port = params->port;
03441 
03442     /* Set valid module led off */
03443     bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_0,
03444               MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_HIGH,
03445               params->port);
03446 
03447     /* Get current gpio val refelecting module plugged in / out*/
03448     gpio_val = bnx2x_get_gpio(bp,  MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_3, port);
03449 
03450     /* Call the handling function in case module is detected */
03451     if (gpio_val == 0) {
03452 
03453         bnx2x_set_gpio_int(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_3,
03454                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_INT_OUTPUT_CLR,
03455                       port);
03456 
03457         if (bnx2x_wait_for_sfp_module_initialized(params) ==
03458             0)
03459             bnx2x_sfp_module_detection(params);
03460         else
03461             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SFP+ module is not initialized\n");
03462     } else {
03463         u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03464 
03465         u32 ext_phy_type =
03466             XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03467         u32 val = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
03468                      offsetof(struct shmem_region, dev_info.
03469                           port_feature_config[params->port].
03470                           config));
03471 
03472         bnx2x_set_gpio_int(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_3,
03473                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_INT_OUTPUT_SET,
03474                       port);
03475         /* Module was plugged out. */
03476         /* Disable transmit for this module */
03477         if ((val & PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_MASK) ==
03478             PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_DISABLE_TX_LASER)
03479             bnx2x_sfp_set_transmitter(bp, params->port,
03480                         ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr, 0);
03481     }
03482 }
03483 
03484 static void bnx2x_bcm807x_force_10G(struct link_params *params)
03485 {
03486     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03487     u8 port = params->port;
03488     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03489     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03490 
03491     /* Force KR or KX */
03492     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03493                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03494                MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
03495                0x2040);
03496     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03497                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03498                MDIO_PMA_REG_10G_CTRL2,
03499                0x000b);
03500     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03501                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03502                MDIO_PMA_REG_BCM_CTRL,
03503                0x0000);
03504     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03505                MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03506                MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL,
03507                0x0000);
03508 }
03509 
03510 static void bnx2x_bcm8073_set_xaui_low_power_mode(struct link_params *params)
03511 {
03512     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03513     u8 port = params->port;
03514     u16 val;
03515     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03516     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03517 
03518     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03519               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
03520               ext_phy_addr,
03521               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03522               MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_CHIP_REV, &val);
03523 
03524     if (val == 0) {
03525         /* Mustn't set low power mode in 8073 A0 */
03526         return;
03527     }
03528 
03529     /* Disable PLL sequencer (use read-modify-write to clear bit 13) */
03530     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03531                MDIO_XS_DEVAD,
03532                MDIO_XS_PLL_SEQUENCER, &val);
03533     val &= ~(1<<13);
03534     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03535                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, MDIO_XS_PLL_SEQUENCER, val);
03536 
03537     /* PLL controls */
03538     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03539                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x805E, 0x1077);
03540     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03541                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x805D, 0x0000);
03542     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03543                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x805C, 0x030B);
03544     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03545                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x805B, 0x1240);
03546     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03547                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x805A, 0x2490);
03548 
03549     /* Tx Controls */
03550     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03551                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x80A7, 0x0C74);
03552     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03553                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x80A6, 0x9041);
03554     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03555                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x80A5, 0x4640);
03556 
03557     /* Rx Controls */
03558     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03559                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x80FE, 0x01C4);
03560     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03561                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x80FD, 0x9249);
03562     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03563                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, 0x80FC, 0x2015);
03564 
03565     /* Enable PLL sequencer  (use read-modify-write to set bit 13) */
03566     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03567               MDIO_XS_DEVAD,
03568               MDIO_XS_PLL_SEQUENCER, &val);
03569     val |= (1<<13);
03570     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
03571                MDIO_XS_DEVAD, MDIO_XS_PLL_SEQUENCER, val);
03572 }
03573 
03574 static void bnx2x_8073_set_pause_cl37(struct link_params *params,
03575                   struct link_vars *vars)
03576 {
03577     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03578     u16 cl37_val;
03579     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03580     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03581 
03582     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03583               ext_phy_type,
03584               ext_phy_addr,
03585               MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03586               MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LD, &cl37_val);
03587 
03588     cl37_val &= ~MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH;
03589     /* Please refer to Table 28B-3 of 802.3ab-1999 spec. */
03590 
03591     if ((vars->ieee_fc &
03592         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_SYMMETRIC) ==
03593         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_SYMMETRIC) {
03594         cl37_val |=  MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_SYMMETRIC;
03595     }
03596     if ((vars->ieee_fc &
03597         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC) ==
03598         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC) {
03599         cl37_val |=  MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC;
03600     }
03601     if ((vars->ieee_fc &
03602         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH) ==
03603         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH) {
03604         cl37_val |= MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH;
03605     }
03606     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
03607          "Ext phy AN advertize cl37 0x%x\n", cl37_val);
03608 
03609     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03610                ext_phy_type,
03611                ext_phy_addr,
03612                MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03613                MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LD, cl37_val);
03614     msleep(500);
03615 }
03616 
03617 static void bnx2x_ext_phy_set_pause(struct link_params *params,
03618                   struct link_vars *vars)
03619 {
03620     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03621     u16 val;
03622     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03623     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03624 
03625     /* read modify write pause advertizing */
03626     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03627               ext_phy_type,
03628               ext_phy_addr,
03629               MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03630               MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE, &val);
03631 
03632     val &= ~MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH;
03633 
03634     /* Please refer to Table 28B-3 of 802.3ab-1999 spec. */
03635 
03636     if ((vars->ieee_fc &
03637         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC) ==
03638         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC) {
03639         val |=  MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE_ASYMMETRIC;
03640     }
03641     if ((vars->ieee_fc &
03642         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH) ==
03643         MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_AUTO_NEG_ADV_PAUSE_BOTH) {
03644         val |=
03645          MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE_PAUSE;
03646     }
03647     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
03648          "Ext phy AN advertize 0x%x\n", val);
03649     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03650                ext_phy_type,
03651                ext_phy_addr,
03652                MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03653                MDIO_AN_REG_ADV_PAUSE, val);
03654 }
03655 static void bnx2x_set_preemphasis(struct link_params *params)
03656 {
03657     u16 bank, i = 0;
03658     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03659 
03660     for (bank = MDIO_REG_BANK_RX0, i = 0; bank <= MDIO_REG_BANK_RX3;
03661           bank += (MDIO_REG_BANK_RX1-MDIO_REG_BANK_RX0), i++) {
03662             CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
03663                           params->phy_addr,
03664                           bank,
03665                           MDIO_RX0_RX_EQ_BOOST,
03666                           params->xgxs_config_rx[i]);
03667     }
03668 
03669     for (bank = MDIO_REG_BANK_TX0, i = 0; bank <= MDIO_REG_BANK_TX3;
03670               bank += (MDIO_REG_BANK_TX1 - MDIO_REG_BANK_TX0), i++) {
03671             CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
03672                           params->phy_addr,
03673                           bank,
03674                           MDIO_TX0_TX_DRIVER,
03675                           params->xgxs_config_tx[i]);
03676     }
03677 }
03678 
03679 
03680 static void bnx2x_8481_set_led4(struct link_params *params,
03681                   u32 ext_phy_type, u8 ext_phy_addr)
03682 {
03683     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03684 
03685     /* PHYC_CTL_LED_CTL */
03686     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03687                ext_phy_type,
03688                ext_phy_addr,
03689                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03690                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LINK_SIGNAL, 0xa482);
03691 
03692     /* Unmask LED4 for 10G link */
03693     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03694                ext_phy_type,
03695                ext_phy_addr,
03696                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03697                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_SIGNAL_MASK, (1<<6));
03698     /* 'Interrupt Mask' */
03699     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03700                ext_phy_type,
03701                ext_phy_addr,
03702                MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03703                0xFFFB, 0xFFFD);
03704 }
03705 static void bnx2x_8481_set_legacy_led_mode(struct link_params *params,
03706                      u32 ext_phy_type, u8 ext_phy_addr)
03707 {
03708     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03709 
03710     /* LED1 (10G Link): Disable LED1 when 10/100/1000 link */
03711     /* LED2 (1G/100/10 Link): Enable LED2 when 10/100/1000 link) */
03712     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03713                ext_phy_type,
03714                ext_phy_addr,
03715                MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03716                MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_SHADOW,
03717                (1<<15) | (0xd << 10) | (0xc<<4) | 0xe);
03718 }
03719 
03720 static void bnx2x_8481_set_10G_led_mode(struct link_params *params,
03721                       u32 ext_phy_type, u8 ext_phy_addr)
03722 {
03723     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03724     u16 val1;
03725 
03726     /* LED1 (10G Link) */
03727     /* Enable continuse based on source 7(10G-link) */
03728     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03729                ext_phy_type,
03730                ext_phy_addr,
03731                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03732                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LINK_SIGNAL,
03733                &val1);
03734     /* Set bit 2 to 0, and bits [1:0] to 10 */
03735     val1 &= ~((1<<0) | (1<<2) | (1<<7)); /* Clear bits 0,2,7*/
03736     val1 |= ((1<<1) | (1<<6)); /* Set bit 1, 6 */
03737 
03738     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03739                ext_phy_type,
03740                ext_phy_addr,
03741                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03742                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LINK_SIGNAL,
03743                val1);
03744 
03745     /* Unmask LED1 for 10G link */
03746     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03747               ext_phy_type,
03748               ext_phy_addr,
03749               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03750               MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LED1_MASK,
03751               &val1);
03752     /* Set bit 2 to 0, and bits [1:0] to 10 */
03753     val1 |= (1<<7);
03754     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03755                ext_phy_type,
03756                ext_phy_addr,
03757                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03758                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LED1_MASK,
03759                val1);
03760 
03761     /* LED2 (1G/100/10G Link) */
03762     /* Mask LED2 for 10G link */
03763     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03764                ext_phy_type,
03765                ext_phy_addr,
03766                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03767                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LED2_MASK,
03768                0);
03769 
03770     /* Unmask LED3 for 10G link */
03771     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03772                ext_phy_type,
03773                ext_phy_addr,
03774                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03775                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LED3_MASK,
03776                0x6);
03777     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03778                ext_phy_type,
03779                ext_phy_addr,
03780                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03781                MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_LED3_BLINK,
03782                0);
03783 }
03784 
03785 
03786 static void bnx2x_init_internal_phy(struct link_params *params,
03787                   struct link_vars *vars,
03788                   u8 enable_cl73)
03789 {
03790     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03791 
03792     if (!(vars->phy_flags & PHY_SGMII_FLAG)) {
03793         if ((XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config) ==
03794              PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) &&
03795             (params->feature_config_flags &
03796              FEATURE_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_PREEMPHASIS_ENABLED))
03797             bnx2x_set_preemphasis(params);
03798 
03799         /* forced speed requested? */
03800         if (vars->line_speed != SPEED_AUTO_NEG ||
03801             ((XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config) ==
03802              PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) &&
03803               params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_EXT)) {
03804             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "not SGMII, no AN\n");
03805 
03806             /* disable autoneg */
03807             bnx2x_set_autoneg(params, vars, 0);
03808 
03809             /* program speed and duplex */
03810             bnx2x_program_serdes(params, vars);
03811 
03812         } else { /* AN_mode */
03813             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "not SGMII, AN\n");
03814 
03815             /* AN enabled */
03816             bnx2x_set_brcm_cl37_advertisment(params);
03817 
03818             /* program duplex & pause advertisement (for aneg) */
03819             bnx2x_set_ieee_aneg_advertisment(params,
03820                                vars->ieee_fc);
03821 
03822             /* enable autoneg */
03823             bnx2x_set_autoneg(params, vars, enable_cl73);
03824 
03825             /* enable and restart AN */
03826             bnx2x_restart_autoneg(params, enable_cl73);
03827         }
03828 
03829     } else { /* SGMII mode */
03830         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SGMII\n");
03831 
03832         bnx2x_initialize_sgmii_process(params, vars);
03833     }
03834 }
03835 
03836 static u8 bnx2x_ext_phy_init(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars)
03837 {
03838     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
03839     u32 ext_phy_type;
03840     u8 ext_phy_addr;
03841     u16 cnt;
03842     u16 ctrl = 0;
03843     u16 val = 0;
03844     u8 rc = 0;
03845 
03846     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
03847         ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
03848 
03849         ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
03850         /* Make sure that the soft reset is off (expect for the 8072:
03851          * due to the lock, it will be done inside the specific
03852          * handling)
03853          */
03854         if ((ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) &&
03855             (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_FAILURE) &&
03856            (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_NOT_CONN) &&
03857             (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072) &&
03858             (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073)) {
03859             /* Wait for soft reset to get cleared upto 1 sec */
03860             for (cnt = 0; cnt < 1000; cnt++) {
03861                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03862                           ext_phy_type,
03863                           ext_phy_addr,
03864                           MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03865                           MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, &ctrl);
03866                 if (!(ctrl & (1<<15)))
03867                     break;
03868                 msleep(1);
03869             }
03870             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "control reg 0x%x (after %d ms)\n",
03871                  ctrl, cnt);
03872         }
03873 
03874         switch (ext_phy_type) {
03875         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
03876             break;
03877 
03878         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705:
03879             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8705\n");
03880 
03881             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03882                        ext_phy_type,
03883                        ext_phy_addr,
03884                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03885                        MDIO_PMA_REG_MISC_CTRL,
03886                        0x8288);
03887             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03888                        ext_phy_type,
03889                        ext_phy_addr,
03890                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03891                        MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
03892                        0x7fbf);
03893             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03894                        ext_phy_type,
03895                        ext_phy_addr,
03896                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03897                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CMU_PLL_BYPASS,
03898                        0x0100);
03899             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03900                        ext_phy_type,
03901                        ext_phy_addr,
03902                        MDIO_WIS_DEVAD,
03903                        MDIO_WIS_REG_LASI_CNTL, 0x1);
03904 
03905             /* BCM8705 doesn't have microcode, hence the 0 */
03906             bnx2x_save_spirom_version(bp, params->port,
03907                         params->shmem_base, 0);
03908             break;
03909 
03910         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706:
03911             /* Wait until fw is loaded */
03912             for (cnt = 0; cnt < 100; cnt++) {
03913                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
03914                           ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03915                           MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER1, &val);
03916                 if (val)
03917                     break;
03918                 msleep(10);
03919             }
03920             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8706 is initialized "
03921                 "after %d ms\n", cnt);
03922             if ((params->feature_config_flags &
03923                  FEATURE_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_PREEMPHASIS_ENABLED)) {
03924                 u8 i;
03925                 u16 reg;
03926                 for (i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
03927                     reg = MDIO_XS_8706_REG_BANK_RX0 +
03928                         i*(MDIO_XS_8706_REG_BANK_RX1 -
03929                            MDIO_XS_8706_REG_BANK_RX0);
03930                     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
03931                               ext_phy_type,
03932                               ext_phy_addr,
03933                               MDIO_XS_DEVAD,
03934                               reg, &val);
03935                     /* Clear first 3 bits of the control */
03936                     val &= ~0x7;
03937                     /* Set control bits according to
03938                     configuation */
03939                     val |= (params->xgxs_config_rx[i] &
03940                         0x7);
03941                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting RX"
03942                          "Equalizer to BCM8706 reg 0x%x"
03943                          " <-- val 0x%x\n", reg, val);
03944                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03945                                ext_phy_type,
03946                                ext_phy_addr,
03947                                MDIO_XS_DEVAD,
03948                                reg, val);
03949                 }
03950             }
03951             /* Force speed */
03952             if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_10000) {
03953                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8706 force 10Gbps\n");
03954 
03955                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03956                            ext_phy_type,
03957                            ext_phy_addr,
03958                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03959                            MDIO_PMA_REG_DIGITAL_CTRL,
03960                            0x400);
03961                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
03962                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
03963                            MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL, 1);
03964             } else {
03965                 /* Force 1Gbps using autoneg with 1G
03966                 advertisment */
03967 
03968                 /* Allow CL37 through CL73 */
03969                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8706 AutoNeg\n");
03970                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03971                            ext_phy_type,
03972                            ext_phy_addr,
03973                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03974                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_CL73,
03975                            0x040c);
03976 
03977                 /* Enable Full-Duplex advertisment on CL37 */
03978                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03979                            ext_phy_type,
03980                            ext_phy_addr,
03981                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03982                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LP,
03983                            0x0020);
03984                 /* Enable CL37 AN */
03985                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03986                            ext_phy_type,
03987                            ext_phy_addr,
03988                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03989                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_AN,
03990                            0x1000);
03991                 /* 1G support */
03992                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
03993                            ext_phy_type,
03994                            ext_phy_addr,
03995                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
03996                            MDIO_AN_REG_ADV, (1<<5));
03997 
03998                 /* Enable clause 73 AN */
03999                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04000                            ext_phy_type,
04001                            ext_phy_addr,
04002                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04003                            MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL,
04004                            0x1200);
04005                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04006                            ext_phy_type,
04007                            ext_phy_addr,
04008                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04009                            MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
04010                            0x0400);
04011                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04012                            ext_phy_type,
04013                            ext_phy_addr,
04014                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04015                            MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL, 0x0004);
04016 
04017             }
04018             bnx2x_save_bcm_spirom_ver(bp, params->port,
04019                         ext_phy_type,
04020                         ext_phy_addr,
04021                         params->shmem_base);
04022             break;
04023         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
04024             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Initializing BCM8726\n");
04025             bnx2x_bcm8726_external_rom_boot(params);
04026 
04027             /* Need to call module detected on initialization since
04028             the module detection triggered by actual module
04029             insertion might occur before driver is loaded, and when
04030             driver is loaded, it reset all registers, including the
04031             transmitter */
04032             bnx2x_sfp_module_detection(params);
04033 
04034             /* Set Flow control */
04035             bnx2x_ext_phy_set_pause(params, vars);
04036             if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_1000) {
04037                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting 1G force\n");
04038                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04039                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04040                            MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, 0x40);
04041                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04042                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04043                            MDIO_PMA_REG_10G_CTRL2, 0xD);
04044                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04045                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04046                            MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL, 0x5);
04047                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04048                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04049                            MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
04050                            0x400);
04051             } else if ((params->req_line_speed ==
04052                     SPEED_AUTO_NEG) &&
04053                    ((params->speed_cap_mask &
04054                      PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G))) {
04055                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting 1G clause37 \n");
04056                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04057                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04058                            MDIO_AN_REG_ADV, 0x20);
04059                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04060                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04061                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_CL73, 0x040c);
04062                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04063                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04064                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LD, 0x0020);
04065                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04066                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04067                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_AN, 0x1000);
04068                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04069                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04070                            MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, 0x1200);
04071 
04072                 /* Enable RX-ALARM control to receive
04073                 interrupt for 1G speed change */
04074                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04075                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04076                            MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL, 0x4);
04077                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04078                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04079                            MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
04080                            0x400);
04081 
04082             } else { /* Default 10G. Set only LASI control */
04083                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04084                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04085                            MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL, 1);
04086             }
04087 
04088             /* Set TX PreEmphasis if needed */
04089             if ((params->feature_config_flags &
04090                  FEATURE_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_PREEMPHASIS_ENABLED)) {
04091                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting TX_CTRL1 0x%x,"
04092                      "TX_CTRL2 0x%x\n",
04093                      params->xgxs_config_tx[0],
04094                      params->xgxs_config_tx[1]);
04095                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04096                            ext_phy_type,
04097                            ext_phy_addr,
04098                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04099                            MDIO_PMA_REG_8726_TX_CTRL1,
04100                            params->xgxs_config_tx[0]);
04101 
04102                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04103                            ext_phy_type,
04104                            ext_phy_addr,
04105                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04106                            MDIO_PMA_REG_8726_TX_CTRL2,
04107                            params->xgxs_config_tx[1]);
04108             }
04109             break;
04110         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
04111         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
04112         {
04113             u16 tmp1;
04114             u16 rx_alarm_ctrl_val;
04115             u16 lasi_ctrl_val;
04116             if (ext_phy_type ==
04117                 PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072) {
04118                 rx_alarm_ctrl_val = 0x400;
04119                 lasi_ctrl_val = 0x0004;
04120             } else {
04121                 rx_alarm_ctrl_val = (1<<2);
04122                 lasi_ctrl_val = 0x0004;
04123             }
04124 
04125             /* enable LASI */
04126             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04127                    ext_phy_type,
04128                    ext_phy_addr,
04129                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04130                    MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
04131                    rx_alarm_ctrl_val);
04132 
04133             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04134                        ext_phy_type,
04135                        ext_phy_addr,
04136                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04137                        MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL,
04138                        lasi_ctrl_val);
04139 
04140             bnx2x_8073_set_pause_cl37(params, vars);
04141 
04142             if (ext_phy_type ==
04143                 PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072)
04144                 bnx2x_bcm8072_external_rom_boot(params);
04145             else
04146                 /* In case of 8073 with long xaui lines,
04147                 don't set the 8073 xaui low power*/
04148                 bnx2x_bcm8073_set_xaui_low_power_mode(params);
04149 
04150             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04151                       ext_phy_type,
04152                       ext_phy_addr,
04153                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04154                       MDIO_PMA_REG_M8051_MSGOUT_REG,
04155                       &tmp1);
04156 
04157             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04158                       ext_phy_type,
04159                       ext_phy_addr,
04160                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04161                       MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM, &tmp1);
04162 
04163             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Before rom RX_ALARM(port1):"
04164                          "0x%x\n", tmp1);
04165 
04166             /* If this is forced speed, set to KR or KX
04167              * (all other are not supported)
04168              */
04169             if (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_EXT) {
