04170                 bnx2x_bcm807x_force_10G(params);
04171                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04172                     "Forced speed 10G on 807X\n");
04173                 break;
04174             } else {
04175                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04176                            ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr,
04177                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04178                            MDIO_PMA_REG_BCM_CTRL,
04179                            0x0002);
04180             }
04181             if (params->req_line_speed != SPEED_AUTO_NEG) {
04182                 if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_10000) {
04183                     val = (1<<7);
04184                 } else if (params->req_line_speed ==
04185                        SPEED_2500) {
04186                     val = (1<<5);
04187                     /* Note that 2.5G works only
04188                     when used with 1G advertisment */
04189                 } else
04190                     val = (1<<5);
04191             } else {
04192 
04193                 val = 0;
04194                 if (params->speed_cap_mask &
04195                     PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10G)
04196                     val |= (1<<7);
04197 
04198                 /* Note that 2.5G works only when
04199                 used with 1G advertisment */
04200                 if (params->speed_cap_mask &
04201                     (PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G |
04202                      PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_2_5G))
04203                     val |= (1<<5);
04204                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04205                      "807x autoneg val = 0x%x\n", val);
04206             }
04207 
04208             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04209                        ext_phy_type,
04210                        ext_phy_addr,
04211                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04212                        MDIO_AN_REG_ADV, val);
04213             if (ext_phy_type ==
04214                 PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073) {
04215                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04216                           ext_phy_type,
04217                           ext_phy_addr,
04218                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04219                           MDIO_AN_REG_8073_2_5G, &tmp1);
04220 
04221                 if (((params->speed_cap_mask &
04222                       PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_2_5G) &&
04223                      (params->req_line_speed ==
04224                       SPEED_AUTO_NEG)) ||
04225                     (params->req_line_speed ==
04226                      SPEED_2500)) {
04227                     u16 phy_ver;
04228                     /* Allow 2.5G for A1 and above */
04229                     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04230                      PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
04231                      ext_phy_addr,
04232                      MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04233                      MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_CHIP_REV, &phy_ver);
04234                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Add 2.5G\n");
04235                     if (phy_ver > 0)
04236                         tmp1 |= 1;
04237                     else
04238                         tmp1 &= 0xfffe;
04239                 } else {
04240                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Disable 2.5G\n");
04241                     tmp1 &= 0xfffe;
04242                 }
04243 
04244                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04245                            ext_phy_type,
04246                            ext_phy_addr,
04247                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04248                            MDIO_AN_REG_8073_2_5G, tmp1);
04249             }
04250 
04251             /* Add support for CL37 (passive mode) II */
04252 
04253             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04254                        ext_phy_type,
04255                        ext_phy_addr,
04256                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04257                        MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LD,
04258                        &tmp1);
04259 
04260             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04261                        ext_phy_type,
04262                        ext_phy_addr,
04263                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04264                        MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_FC_LD, (tmp1 |
04265                        ((params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL) ?
04266                        0x20 : 0x40)));
04267 
04268             /* Add support for CL37 (passive mode) III */
04269             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04270                        ext_phy_type,
04271                        ext_phy_addr,
04272                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04273                        MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_AN, 0x1000);
04274 
04275             if (ext_phy_type ==
04276                 PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073) {
04277                 /* The SNR will improve about 2db by changing
04278                 BW and FEE main tap. Rest commands are executed
04279                 after link is up*/
04280                 /*Change FFE main cursor to 5 in EDC register*/
04281                 if (bnx2x_8073_is_snr_needed(params))
04282                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04283                             ext_phy_type,
04284                             ext_phy_addr,
04285                             MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04286                             MDIO_PMA_REG_EDC_FFE_MAIN,
04287                             0xFB0C);
04288 
04289                 /* Enable FEC (Forware Error Correction)
04290                 Request in the AN */
04291                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04292                           ext_phy_type,
04293                           ext_phy_addr,
04294                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04295                           MDIO_AN_REG_ADV2, &tmp1);
04296 
04297                 tmp1 |= (1<<15);
04298 
04299                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04300                            ext_phy_type,
04301                            ext_phy_addr,
04302                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04303                            MDIO_AN_REG_ADV2, tmp1);
04304 
04305             }
04306 
04307             bnx2x_ext_phy_set_pause(params, vars);
04308 
04309             /* Restart autoneg */
04310             msleep(500);
04311             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04312                        ext_phy_type,
04313                        ext_phy_addr,
04314                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04315                        MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, 0x1200);
04316             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "807x Autoneg Restart: "
04317                "Advertise 1G=%x, 10G=%x\n",
04318                ((val & (1<<5)) > 0),
04319                ((val & (1<<7)) > 0));
04320             break;
04321         }
04322 
04323         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
04324         {
04325             u16 tmp1;
04326             u16 rx_alarm_ctrl_val;
04327             u16 lasi_ctrl_val;
04328 
04329             /* Enable PMD link, MOD_ABS_FLT, and 1G link alarm */
04330 
04331             u16 mod_abs;
04332             rx_alarm_ctrl_val = (1<<2) | (1<<5) ;
04333             lasi_ctrl_val = 0x0004;
04334 
04335             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Initializing BCM8727\n");
04336             /* enable LASI */
04337             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04338                        ext_phy_type,
04339                        ext_phy_addr,
04340                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04341                        MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
04342                        rx_alarm_ctrl_val);
04343 
04344             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04345                        ext_phy_type,
04346                        ext_phy_addr,
04347                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04348                        MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL,
04349                        lasi_ctrl_val);
04350 
04351             /* Initially configure  MOD_ABS to interrupt when
04352             module is presence( bit 8) */
04353             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04354                       ext_phy_type,
04355                       ext_phy_addr,
04356                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04357                       MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER, &mod_abs);
04358             /* Set EDC off by setting OPTXLOS signal input to low
04359             (bit 9).
04360             When the EDC is off it locks onto a reference clock and
04361             avoids becoming 'lost'.*/
04362             mod_abs &= ~((1<<8) | (1<<9));
04363             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04364                        ext_phy_type,
04365                        ext_phy_addr,
04366                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04367                        MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER, mod_abs);
04368 
04369             /* Make MOD_ABS give interrupt on change */
04370             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04371                       ext_phy_type,
04372                       ext_phy_addr,
04373                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04374                       MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_PCS_OPT_CTRL,
04375                       &val);
04376             val |= (1<<12);
04377             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04378                        ext_phy_type,
04379                        ext_phy_addr,
04380                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04381                        MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_PCS_OPT_CTRL,
04382                        val);
04383 
04384             /* Set 8727 GPIOs to input to allow reading from the
04385             8727 GPIO0 status which reflect SFP+ module
04386             over-current */
04387 
04388             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04389                        PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04390                        ext_phy_addr,
04391                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04392                        MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_PCS_OPT_CTRL,
04393                        &val);
04394             val &= 0xff8f; /* Reset bits 4-6 */
04395             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04396                        PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04397                        ext_phy_addr,
04398                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04399                        MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_PCS_OPT_CTRL,
04400                        val);
04401 
04402             bnx2x_8727_power_module(bp, params, ext_phy_addr, 1);
04403             bnx2x_bcm8073_set_xaui_low_power_mode(params);
04404 
04405             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04406                       ext_phy_type,
04407                       ext_phy_addr,
04408                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04409                       MDIO_PMA_REG_M8051_MSGOUT_REG,
04410                       &tmp1);
04411 
04412             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04413                       ext_phy_type,
04414                       ext_phy_addr,
04415                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04416                       MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM, &tmp1);
04417 
04418             /* Set option 1G speed */
04419             if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_1000) {
04420 
04421                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting 1G force\n");
04422                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04423                            ext_phy_type,
04424                            ext_phy_addr,
04425                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04426                            MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, 0x40);
04427                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04428                            ext_phy_type,
04429                            ext_phy_addr,
04430                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04431                            MDIO_PMA_REG_10G_CTRL2, 0xD);
04432                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04433                       ext_phy_type,
04434                       ext_phy_addr,
04435                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04436                       MDIO_PMA_REG_10G_CTRL2, &tmp1);
04437                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "1.7 = 0x%x \n", tmp1);
04438 
04439             } else if ((params->req_line_speed ==
04440                     SPEED_AUTO_NEG) &&
04441                    ((params->speed_cap_mask &
04442                      PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G))) {
04443 
04444                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting 1G clause37 \n");
04445                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04446                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04447                            MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_MISC_CTRL, 0);
04448                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04449                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04450                            MDIO_AN_REG_CL37_AN, 0x1300);
04451             } else {
04452                 /* Since the 8727 has only single reset pin,
04453                 need to set the 10G registers although it is
04454                 default */
04455                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04456                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04457                            MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, 0x0020);
04458                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04459                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04460                            0x7, 0x0100);
04461                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04462                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04463                            MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, 0x2040);
04464                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04465                            ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04466                            MDIO_PMA_REG_10G_CTRL2, 0x0008);
04467             }
04468 
04469             /* Set 2-wire transfer rate to 400Khz since 100Khz
04470             is not operational */
04471             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04472                        ext_phy_type,
04473                        ext_phy_addr,
04474                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04475                        MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_TWO_WIRE_SLAVE_ADDR,
04476                        0xa101);
04477 
04478             /* Set TX PreEmphasis if needed */
04479             if ((params->feature_config_flags &
04480                  FEATURE_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_PREEMPHASIS_ENABLED)) {
04481                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting TX_CTRL1 0x%x,"
04482                      "TX_CTRL2 0x%x\n",
04483                      params->xgxs_config_tx[0],
04484                      params->xgxs_config_tx[1]);
04485                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04486                            ext_phy_type,
04487                            ext_phy_addr,
04488                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04489                            MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_TX_CTRL1,
04490                            params->xgxs_config_tx[0]);
04491 
04492                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04493                            ext_phy_type,
04494                            ext_phy_addr,
04495                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04496                            MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_TX_CTRL2,
04497                            params->xgxs_config_tx[1]);
04498             }
04499 
04500             break;
04501         }
04502 
04503         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101:
04504         {
04505             u16 fw_ver1, fw_ver2;
04506             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04507                 "Setting the SFX7101 LASI indication\n");
04508 
04509             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04510                        ext_phy_type,
04511                        ext_phy_addr,
04512                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04513                        MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_CTRL, 0x1);
04514             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04515               "Setting the SFX7101 LED to blink on traffic\n");
04516             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04517                        ext_phy_type,
04518                        ext_phy_addr,
04519                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04520                        MDIO_PMA_REG_7107_LED_CNTL, (1<<3));
04521 
04522             bnx2x_ext_phy_set_pause(params, vars);
04523             /* Restart autoneg */
04524             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04525                       ext_phy_type,
04526                       ext_phy_addr,
04527                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04528                       MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, &val);
04529             val |= 0x200;
04530             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04531                        ext_phy_type,
04532                        ext_phy_addr,
04533                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04534                        MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, val);
04535 
04536             /* Save spirom version */
04537             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04538                       ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04539                       MDIO_PMA_REG_7101_VER1, &fw_ver1);
04540 
04541             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04542                       ext_phy_addr, MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04543                       MDIO_PMA_REG_7101_VER2, &fw_ver2);
04544 
04545             bnx2x_save_spirom_version(params->bp, params->port,
04546                         params->shmem_base,
04547                         (u32)(fw_ver1<<16 | fw_ver2));
04548             break;
04549         }
04550         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481:
04551         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
04552             /* This phy uses the NIG latch mechanism since link
04553                 indication arrives through its LED4 and not via
04554                 its LASI signal, so we get steady signal
04555                 instead of clear on read */
04556             bnx2x_bits_en(bp, NIG_REG_LATCH_BC_0 + params->port*4,
04557                     1 << NIG_LATCH_BC_ENABLE_MI_INT);
04558 
04559             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04560                        PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
04561                        ext_phy_addr,
04562                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04563                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, 0x0000);
04564 
04565             bnx2x_8481_set_led4(params, ext_phy_type, ext_phy_addr);
04566             if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG) {
04567 
04568                 u16 autoneg_val, an_1000_val, an_10_100_val;
04569                 /* set 1000 speed advertisement */
04570                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04571                           ext_phy_type,
04572                           ext_phy_addr,
04573                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04574                           MDIO_AN_REG_8481_1000T_CTRL,
04575                           &an_1000_val);
04576 
04577                 bnx2x_ext_phy_set_pause(params, vars);
04578 
04579                 if (params->speed_cap_mask &
04580                     PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G) {
04581                     an_1000_val |= (1<<8);
04582                     if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
04583                         an_1000_val |= (1<<9);
04584                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Advertising 1G\n");
04585                 } else
04586                     an_1000_val &= ~((1<<8) | (1<<9));
04587 
04588                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04589                            ext_phy_type,
04590                            ext_phy_addr,
04591                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04592                            MDIO_AN_REG_8481_1000T_CTRL,
04593                            an_1000_val);
04594 
04595                 /* set 100 speed advertisement */
04596                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04597                           ext_phy_type,
04598                           ext_phy_addr,
04599                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04600                           MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_AN_ADV,
04601                           &an_10_100_val);
04602 
04603                 if (params->speed_cap_mask &
04604                  (PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_100M_FULL |
04605                   PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_100M_HALF)) {
04606                     an_10_100_val |= (1<<7);
04607                     if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
04608                         an_10_100_val |= (1<<8);
04609                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04610                         "Advertising 100M\n");
04611                 } else
04612                     an_10_100_val &= ~((1<<7) | (1<<8));
04613 
04614                 /* set 10 speed advertisement */
04615                 if (params->speed_cap_mask &
04616                   (PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10M_FULL |
04617                    PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10M_HALF)) {
04618                     an_10_100_val |= (1<<5);
04619                     if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
04620                         an_10_100_val |= (1<<6);
04621                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Advertising 10M\n");
04622                      }
04623                 else
04624                     an_10_100_val &= ~((1<<5) | (1<<6));
04625 
04626                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04627                            ext_phy_type,
04628                            ext_phy_addr,
04629                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04630                            MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_AN_ADV,
04631                            an_10_100_val);
04632 
04633                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04634                           ext_phy_type,
04635                           ext_phy_addr,
04636                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04637                           MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_MII_CTRL,
04638                           &autoneg_val);
04639 
04640                 /* Disable forced speed */
04641                 autoneg_val &= ~(1<<6|1<<13);
04642 
04643                 /* Enable autoneg and restart autoneg
04644                 for legacy speeds */
04645                 autoneg_val |= (1<<9|1<<12);
04646 
04647                 if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
04648                     autoneg_val |= (1<<8);
04649                 else
04650                     autoneg_val &= ~(1<<8);
04651 
04652                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04653                            ext_phy_type,
04654                            ext_phy_addr,
04655                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04656                            MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_MII_CTRL,
04657                            autoneg_val);
04658 
04659                 if (params->speed_cap_mask &
04660                     PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10G) {
04661                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Advertising 10G\n");
04662                     /* Restart autoneg for 10G*/
04663 
04664             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04665                        ext_phy_type,
04666                        ext_phy_addr,
04667                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04668                        MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, 0x3200);
04669                 }
04670             } else {
04671                 /* Force speed */
04672                 u16 autoneg_ctrl, pma_ctrl;
04673                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04674                           ext_phy_type,
04675                           ext_phy_addr,
04676                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04677                           MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_MII_CTRL,
04678                           &autoneg_ctrl);
04679 
04680                 /* Disable autoneg */
04681                 autoneg_ctrl &= ~(1<<12);
04682 
04683                 /* Set 1000 force */
04684                 switch (params->req_line_speed) {
04685                 case SPEED_10000:
04686                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04687                         "Unable to set 10G force !\n");
04688                     break;
04689                 case SPEED_1000:
04690                     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04691                               ext_phy_type,
04692                               ext_phy_addr,
04693                               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04694                               MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
04695                               &pma_ctrl);
04696                     autoneg_ctrl &= ~(1<<13);
04697                     autoneg_ctrl |= (1<<6);
04698                     pma_ctrl &= ~(1<<13);
04699                     pma_ctrl |= (1<<6);
04700                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04701                         "Setting 1000M force\n");
04702                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04703                                ext_phy_type,
04704                                ext_phy_addr,
04705                                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04706                                MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
04707                                pma_ctrl);
04708                     break;
04709                 case SPEED_100:
04710                     autoneg_ctrl |= (1<<13);
04711                     autoneg_ctrl &= ~(1<<6);
04712                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04713                         "Setting 100M force\n");
04714                     break;
04715                 case SPEED_10:
04716                     autoneg_ctrl &= ~(1<<13);
04717                     autoneg_ctrl &= ~(1<<6);
04718                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04719                         "Setting 10M force\n");
04720                     break;
04721                 }
04722 
04723                 /* Duplex mode */
04724                 if (params->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL) {
04725                     autoneg_ctrl |= (1<<8);
04726                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04727                         "Setting full duplex\n");
04728                 } else
04729                     autoneg_ctrl &= ~(1<<8);
04730 
04731                 /* Update autoneg ctrl and pma ctrl */
04732                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04733                            ext_phy_type,
04734                            ext_phy_addr,
04735                            MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
04736                            MDIO_AN_REG_8481_LEGACY_MII_CTRL,
04737                            autoneg_ctrl);
04738             }
04739 
04740             /* Save spirom version */
04741             bnx2x_save_8481_spirom_version(bp, params->port,
04742                              ext_phy_addr,
04743                              params->shmem_base);
04744             break;
04745         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_FAILURE:
04746             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
04747                  "XGXS PHY Failure detected 0x%x\n",
04748                  params->ext_phy_config);
04749             rc = -EINVAL;
04750             break;
04751         default:
04752             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BAD XGXS ext_phy_config 0x%x\n",
04753                   params->ext_phy_config);
04754             rc = -EINVAL;
04755             break;
04756         }
04757 
04758     } else { /* SerDes */
04759 
04760         ext_phy_type = SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
04761         switch (ext_phy_type) {
04762         case PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
04763             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes Direct\n");
04764             break;
04765 
04766         case PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM5482:
04767             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes 5482\n");
04768             break;
04769 
04770         default:
04771             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BAD SerDes ext_phy_config 0x%x\n",
04772                params->ext_phy_config);
04773             break;
04774         }
04775     }
04776     return rc;
04777 }
04778 
04779 static void bnx2x_8727_handle_mod_abs(struct link_params *params)
04780 {
04781     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
04782     u16 mod_abs, rx_alarm_status;
04783     u8 ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
04784     u32 val = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
04785                  offsetof(struct shmem_region, dev_info.
04786                       port_feature_config[params->port].
04787                       config));
04788     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04789               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04790               ext_phy_addr,
04791               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04792               MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER, &mod_abs);
04793     if (mod_abs & (1<<8)) {
04794 
04795         /* Module is absent */
04796         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "MOD_ABS indication "
04797                 "show module is absent\n");
04798 
04799         /* 1. Set mod_abs to detect next module
04800         presence event
04801            2. Set EDC off by setting OPTXLOS signal input to low
04802             (bit 9).
04803             When the EDC is off it locks onto a reference clock and
04804             avoids becoming 'lost'.*/
04805         mod_abs &= ~((1<<8)|(1<<9));
04806         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04807                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04808                    ext_phy_addr,
04809                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04810                    MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER, mod_abs);
04811 
04812         /* Clear RX alarm since it stays up as long as
04813         the mod_abs wasn't changed */
04814         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04815                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04816                   ext_phy_addr,
04817                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04818                   MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM, &rx_alarm_status);
04819 
04820     } else {
04821         /* Module is present */
04822         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "MOD_ABS indication "
04823                 "show module is present\n");
04824         /* First thing, disable transmitter,
04825         and if the module is ok, the
04826         module_detection will enable it*/
04827 
04828         /* 1. Set mod_abs to detect next module
04829         absent event ( bit 8)
04830            2. Restore the default polarity of the OPRXLOS signal and
04831         this signal will then correctly indicate the presence or
04832         absence of the Rx signal. (bit 9) */
04833         mod_abs |= ((1<<8)|(1<<9));
04834         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
04835                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04836                ext_phy_addr,
04837                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04838                MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER, mod_abs);
04839 
04840         /* Clear RX alarm since it stays up as long as
04841         the mod_abs wasn't changed. This is need to be done
04842         before calling the module detection, otherwise it will clear
04843         the link update alarm */
04844         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04845                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04846                   ext_phy_addr,
04847                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04848                   MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM, &rx_alarm_status);
04849 
04850 
04851         if ((val & PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_MASK) ==
04852             PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_DISABLE_TX_LASER)
04853             bnx2x_sfp_set_transmitter(bp, params->port,
04854                     PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
04855                     ext_phy_addr, 0);
04856 
04857         if (bnx2x_wait_for_sfp_module_initialized(params)
04858             == 0)
04859             bnx2x_sfp_module_detection(params);
04860         else
04861             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SFP+ module is not initialized\n");
04862     }
04863 
04864     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8727 RX_ALARM_STATUS 0x%x\n",
04865          rx_alarm_status);
04866     /* No need to check link status in case of
04867     module plugged in/out */
04868 }
04869 
04870 
04871 static u8 bnx2x_ext_phy_is_link_up(struct link_params *params,
04872                  struct link_vars *vars,
04873                  u8 is_mi_int)
04874 {
04875     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
04876     u32 ext_phy_type;
04877     u8 ext_phy_addr;
04878     u16 val1 = 0, val2;
04879     u16 rx_sd, pcs_status;
04880     u8 ext_phy_link_up = 0;
04881     u8 port = params->port;
04882 
04883     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
04884         ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
04885         ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
04886         switch (ext_phy_type) {
04887         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
04888             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS Direct\n");
04889             ext_phy_link_up = 1;
04890             break;
04891 
04892         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705:
04893             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8705\n");
04894             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04895                       ext_phy_addr,
04896                       MDIO_WIS_DEVAD,
04897                       MDIO_WIS_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val1);
04898             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8705 LASI status 0x%x\n", val1);
04899 
04900             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04901                       ext_phy_addr,
04902                       MDIO_WIS_DEVAD,
04903                       MDIO_WIS_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val1);
04904             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8705 LASI status 0x%x\n", val1);
04905 
04906             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04907                       ext_phy_addr,
04908                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04909                       MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_SD, &rx_sd);
04910 
04911             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04912                       ext_phy_addr,
04913                       1,
04914                       0xc809, &val1);
04915             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04916                       ext_phy_addr,
04917                       1,
04918                       0xc809, &val1);
04919 
04920             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8705 1.c809 val=0x%x\n", val1);
04921             ext_phy_link_up = ((rx_sd & 0x1) && (val1 & (1<<9))
04922                        && ((val1 & (1<<8)) == 0));
04923             if (ext_phy_link_up)
04924                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
04925             break;
04926 
04927         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706:
04928         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
04929             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 8706/8726\n");
04930             /* Clear RX Alarm*/
04931             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04932                       ext_phy_addr,
04933                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD, MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM,
04934                       &val2);
04935             /* clear LASI indication*/
04936             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04937                       ext_phy_addr,
04938                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD, MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_STATUS,
04939                       &val1);
04940             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04941                       ext_phy_addr,
04942                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD, MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_STATUS,
04943                       &val2);
04944             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8706/8726 LASI status 0x%x-->"
04945                      "0x%x\n", val1, val2);
04946 
04947             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04948                       ext_phy_addr,
04949                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD, MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_SD,
04950                       &rx_sd);
04951             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04952                       ext_phy_addr,
04953                       MDIO_PCS_DEVAD, MDIO_PCS_REG_STATUS,
04954                       &pcs_status);
04955             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04956                       ext_phy_addr,
04957                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD, MDIO_AN_REG_LINK_STATUS,
04958                       &val2);
04959             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
04960                       ext_phy_addr,
04961                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD, MDIO_AN_REG_LINK_STATUS,
04962                       &val2);
04963 
04964             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8706/8726 rx_sd 0x%x"
04965                "  pcs_status 0x%x 1Gbps link_status 0x%x\n",
04966                rx_sd, pcs_status, val2);
04967             /* link is up if both bit 0 of pmd_rx_sd and
04968              * bit 0 of pcs_status are set, or if the autoneg bit
04969                1 is set
04970              */
04971             ext_phy_link_up = ((rx_sd & pcs_status & 0x1) ||
04972                        (val2 & (1<<1)));
04973             if (ext_phy_link_up) {
04974                 if (ext_phy_type ==
04975                      PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726) {
04976                     /* If transmitter is disabled,
04977                     ignore false link up indication */
04978                     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
04979                            ext_phy_type,
04980                            ext_phy_addr,
04981                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
04982                            MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
04983                            &val1);
04984                     if (val1 & (1<<15)) {
04985                         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Tx is "
04986                                 "disabled\n");
04987                         ext_phy_link_up = 0;
04988                         break;
04989                     }
04990                 }
04991                 if (val2 & (1<<1))
04992                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
04993                 else
04994                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
04995             }
04996             break;
04997 
04998         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
04999         {
05000             u16 link_status = 0;
05001             u16 rx_alarm_status;
05002             /* Check the LASI */
05003             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05004                       ext_phy_type,
05005                       ext_phy_addr,
05006                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05007                       MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM, &rx_alarm_status);
05008 
05009             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8727 RX_ALARM_STATUS 0x%x\n",
05010                  rx_alarm_status);
05011 
05012             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05013                       ext_phy_type,
05014                       ext_phy_addr,
05015                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05016                       MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val1);
05017 
05018             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05019                  "8727 LASI status 0x%x\n",
05020                  val1);
05021 
05022             /* Clear MSG-OUT */
05023             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05024                       ext_phy_type,
05025                       ext_phy_addr,
05026                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05027                       MDIO_PMA_REG_M8051_MSGOUT_REG,
05028                       &val1);
05029 
05030             /*
05031              * If a module is present and there is need to check
05032              * for over current
05033              */
05034             if (!(params->feature_config_flags &
05035                   FEATURE_CONFIG_BCM8727_NOC) &&
05036                 !(rx_alarm_status & (1<<5))) {
05037                 /* Check over-current using 8727 GPIO0 input*/
05038                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05039                           ext_phy_type,
05040                           ext_phy_addr,
05041                           MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05042                           MDIO_PMA_REG_8727_GPIO_CTRL,
05043                           &val1);
05044 
05045                 if ((val1 & (1<<8)) == 0) {
05046                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8727 Power fault"
05047                              " has been detected on "
05048                              "port %d\n",
05049                          params->port);
05050                     printk(KERN_ERR PFX  "Error:  Power"
05051                          " fault on %s Port %d has"
05052                          " been detected and the"
05053                          " power to that SFP+ module"
05054                          " has been removed to prevent"
05055                          " failure of the card. Please"
05056                          " remove the SFP+ module and"
05057                          " restart the system to clear"
05058                          " this error.\n"
05059             , bp->dev->name, params->port);
05060                     /*
05061                      * Disable all RX_ALARMs except for
05062                      * mod_abs
05063                      */
05064                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
05065                              ext_phy_type,
05066                              ext_phy_addr,
05067                              MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05068                              MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
05069                              (1<<5));
05070 
05071                     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05072                             ext_phy_type,
05073                             ext_phy_addr,
05074                             MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05075                             MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
05076                             &val1);
05077                     /* Wait for module_absent_event */
05078                     val1 |= (1<<8);
05079                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
05080                             ext_phy_type,
05081                             ext_phy_addr,
05082                             MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05083                             MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
05084                             val1);
05085                     /* Clear RX alarm */
05086                     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05087                               ext_phy_type,
05088                               ext_phy_addr,
05089                               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05090                               MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM,
05091                               &rx_alarm_status);
05092                     break;
05093                 }
05094             } /* Over current check */
05095 
05096             /* When module absent bit is set, check module */
05097             if (rx_alarm_status & (1<<5)) {
05098                 bnx2x_8727_handle_mod_abs(params);
05099                 /* Enable all mod_abs and link detection bits */
05100                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
05101                            ext_phy_type,
05102                            ext_phy_addr,
05103                            MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05104                            MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM_CTRL,
05105                            ((1<<5) | (1<<2)));
05106             }
05107 
05108             /* If transmitter is disabled,
05109             ignore false link up indication */
05110             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05111                       ext_phy_type,
05112                       ext_phy_addr,
05113                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05114                       MDIO_PMA_REG_PHY_IDENTIFIER,
05115                       &val1);
05116             if (val1 & (1<<15)) {
05117                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Tx is disabled\n");
05118                 ext_phy_link_up = 0;
05119                 break;
05120             }
05121 
05122             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05123                       ext_phy_type,
05124                       ext_phy_addr,
05125                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05126                       MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_SPEED_LINK_STATUS,
05127                       &link_status);
05128 
05129             /* Bits 0..2 --> speed detected,
05130                bits 13..15--> link is down */
05131             if ((link_status & (1<<2)) &&
05132                 (!(link_status & (1<<15)))) {
05133                 ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05134                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
05135             } else if ((link_status & (1<<0)) &&
05136                    (!(link_status & (1<<13)))) {
05137                 ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05138                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
05139                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05140                      "port %x: External link"
05141                      " up in 1G\n", params->port);
05142             } else {
05143                 ext_phy_link_up = 0;
05144                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05145                      "port %x: External link"
05146                      " is down\n", params->port);
05147             }
05148             break;
05149         }
05150 
05151         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
05152         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
05153         {
05154             u16 link_status = 0;
05155             u16 an1000_status = 0;
05156 
05157             if (ext_phy_type ==
05158                  PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072) {
05159                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05160                       ext_phy_type,
05161                       ext_phy_addr,
05162                       MDIO_PCS_DEVAD,
05163                       MDIO_PCS_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val1);
05164                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05165                       ext_phy_type,
05166                       ext_phy_addr,
05167                       MDIO_PCS_DEVAD,
05168                       MDIO_PCS_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val2);
05169                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05170                      "870x LASI status 0x%x->0x%x\n",
05171                      val1, val2);
05172             } else {
05173                 /* In 8073, port1 is directed through emac0 and
05174                  * port0 is directed through emac1
05175                  */
05176                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05177                           ext_phy_type,
05178                           ext_phy_addr,
05179                           MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05180                           MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val1);
05181 
05182                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05183                      "8703 LASI status 0x%x\n",
05184                       val1);
05185             }
05186 
05187             /* clear the interrupt LASI status register */
05188             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05189                       ext_phy_type,
05190                       ext_phy_addr,
05191                       MDIO_PCS_DEVAD,
05192                       MDIO_PCS_REG_STATUS, &val2);
05193             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05194                       ext_phy_type,
05195                       ext_phy_addr,
05196                       MDIO_PCS_DEVAD,
05197                       MDIO_PCS_REG_STATUS, &val1);
05198             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "807x PCS status 0x%x->0x%x\n",
05199                val2, val1);
05200             /* Clear MSG-OUT */
05201             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05202                       ext_phy_type,
05203                       ext_phy_addr,
05204                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05205                       MDIO_PMA_REG_M8051_MSGOUT_REG,
05206                       &val1);
05207 
05208             /* Check the LASI */
05209             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05210                       ext_phy_type,
05211                       ext_phy_addr,
05212                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05213                       MDIO_PMA_REG_RX_ALARM, &val2);
05214 
05215             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "KR 0x9003 0x%x\n", val2);
05216 
05217             /* Check the link status */
05218             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05219                       ext_phy_type,
05220                       ext_phy_addr,
05221                       MDIO_PCS_DEVAD,
05222                       MDIO_PCS_REG_STATUS, &val2);
05223             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "KR PCS status 0x%x\n", val2);
05224 
05225             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05226                       ext_phy_type,
05227                       ext_phy_addr,
05228                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05229                       MDIO_PMA_REG_STATUS, &val2);
05230             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05231                       ext_phy_type,
05232                       ext_phy_addr,
05233                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05234                       MDIO_PMA_REG_STATUS, &val1);
05235             ext_phy_link_up = ((val1 & 4) == 4);
05236             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "PMA_REG_STATUS=0x%x\n", val1);
05237             if (ext_phy_type ==
05238                 PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073) {
05239 
05240                 if (ext_phy_link_up &&
05241                     ((params->req_line_speed !=
05242                     SPEED_10000))) {
05243                     if (bnx2x_bcm8073_xaui_wa(params)
05244                          != 0) {
05245                         ext_phy_link_up = 0;
05246                         break;
05247                     }
05248                 }
05249                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05250                           ext_phy_type,
05251                           ext_phy_addr,
05252                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05253                           MDIO_AN_REG_LINK_STATUS,
05254                           &an1000_status);
05255                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05256                           ext_phy_type,
05257                           ext_phy_addr,
05258                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05259                           MDIO_AN_REG_LINK_STATUS,
05260                           &an1000_status);
05261 
05262                 /* Check the link status on 1.1.2 */
05263                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05264                           ext_phy_type,
05265                           ext_phy_addr,
05266                           MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05267                           MDIO_PMA_REG_STATUS, &val2);
05268                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05269                           ext_phy_type,
05270                           ext_phy_addr,
05271                           MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05272                           MDIO_PMA_REG_STATUS, &val1);
05273                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "KR PMA status 0x%x->0x%x,"
05274                          "an_link_status=0x%x\n",
05275                       val2, val1, an1000_status);
05276 
05277                 ext_phy_link_up = (((val1 & 4) == 4) ||
05278                         (an1000_status & (1<<1)));
05279                 if (ext_phy_link_up &&
05280                     bnx2x_8073_is_snr_needed(params)) {
05281                     /* The SNR will improve about 2dbby
05282                     changing the BW and FEE main tap.*/
05283 
05284                     /* The 1st write to change FFE main
05285                     tap is set before restart AN */
05286                     /* Change PLL Bandwidth in EDC
05287                     register */
05288                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type,
05289                             ext_phy_addr,
05290                             MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05291                             MDIO_PMA_REG_PLL_BANDWIDTH,
05292                             0x26BC);
05293 
05294                     /* Change CDR Bandwidth in EDC
05295                     register */
05296                     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, ext_phy_type,
05297                             ext_phy_addr,
05298                             MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05299                             MDIO_PMA_REG_CDR_BANDWIDTH,
05300                             0x0333);
05301                 }
05302                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05303                        ext_phy_type,
05304                        ext_phy_addr,
05305                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05306                        MDIO_PMA_REG_8073_SPEED_LINK_STATUS,
05307                        &link_status);
05308 
05309                 /* Bits 0..2 --> speed detected,
05310                    bits 13..15--> link is down */
05311                 if ((link_status & (1<<2)) &&
05312                     (!(link_status & (1<<15)))) {
05313                     ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05314                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
05315                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05316                          "port %x: External link"
05317                          " up in 10G\n", params->port);
05318                 } else if ((link_status & (1<<1)) &&
05319                        (!(link_status & (1<<14)))) {
05320                     ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05321                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_2500;
05322                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05323                          "port %x: External link"
05324                          " up in 2.5G\n", params->port);
05325                 } else if ((link_status & (1<<0)) &&
05326                        (!(link_status & (1<<13)))) {
05327                     ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05328                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
05329                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05330                          "port %x: External link"
05331                          " up in 1G\n", params->port);
05332                 } else {
05333                     ext_phy_link_up = 0;
05334                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05335                          "port %x: External link"
05336                          " is down\n", params->port);
05337                 }
05338             } else {
05339                 /* See if 1G link is up for the 8072 */
05340                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05341                           ext_phy_type,
05342                           ext_phy_addr,
05343                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05344                           MDIO_AN_REG_LINK_STATUS,
05345                           &an1000_status);
05346                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05347                           ext_phy_type,
05348                           ext_phy_addr,
05349                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05350                           MDIO_AN_REG_LINK_STATUS,
05351                           &an1000_status);
05352                 if (an1000_status & (1<<1)) {
05353                     ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05354                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
05355                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05356                          "port %x: External link"
05357                          " up in 1G\n", params->port);
05358                 } else if (ext_phy_link_up) {
05359                     ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05360                     vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
05361                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05362                          "port %x: External link"
05363                          " up in 10G\n", params->port);
05364                 }
05365             }
05366 
05367 
05368             break;
05369         }
05370         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101:
05371             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05372                       ext_phy_addr,
05373                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05374                       MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val2);
05375             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05376                       ext_phy_addr,
05377                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05378                       MDIO_PMA_REG_LASI_STATUS, &val1);
05379             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05380                  "10G-base-T LASI status 0x%x->0x%x\n",
05381                   val2, val1);
05382             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05383                       ext_phy_addr,
05384                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05385                       MDIO_PMA_REG_STATUS, &val2);
05386             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05387                       ext_phy_addr,
05388                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05389                       MDIO_PMA_REG_STATUS, &val1);
05390             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05391                  "10G-base-T PMA status 0x%x->0x%x\n",
05392                  val2, val1);
05393             ext_phy_link_up = ((val1 & 4) == 4);
05394             /* if link is up
05395              * print the AN outcome of the SFX7101 PHY
05396              */
05397             if (ext_phy_link_up) {
05398                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05399                           ext_phy_type,
05400                           ext_phy_addr,
05401                           MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05402                           MDIO_AN_REG_MASTER_STATUS,
05403                           &val2);
05404                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
05405                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05406                      "SFX7101 AN status 0x%x->Master=%x\n",
05407                       val2,
05408                      (val2 & (1<<14)));
05409             }
05410             break;
05411         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481:
05412         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
05413             /* Check 10G-BaseT link status */
05414             /* Check PMD signal ok */
05415             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05416                               ext_phy_addr,
05417                               MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05418                               0xFFFA,
05419                               &val1);
05420             bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05421                       ext_phy_addr,
05422                       MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05423                       MDIO_PMA_REG_8481_PMD_SIGNAL,
05424                       &val2);
05425             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "PMD_SIGNAL 1.a811 = 0x%x\n", val2);
05426 
05427             /* Check link 10G */
05428             if (val2 & (1<<11)) {
05429                 vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
05430                 ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05431                 bnx2x_8481_set_10G_led_mode(params,
05432                               ext_phy_type,
05433                               ext_phy_addr);
05434             } else { /* Check Legacy speed link */
05435                 u16 legacy_status, legacy_speed;
05436 
05437                 /* Enable expansion register 0x42
05438                 (Operation mode status) */
05439                 bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port,
05440                      ext_phy_type,
05441                      ext_phy_addr,
05442                      MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05443                      MDIO_AN_REG_8481_EXPANSION_REG_ACCESS,
05444                      0xf42);
05445 
05446                 /* Get legacy speed operation status */
05447                 bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, params->port,
05448                       ext_phy_type,
05449                       ext_phy_addr,
05450                       MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
05451                       MDIO_AN_REG_8481_EXPANSION_REG_RD_RW,
05452                       &legacy_status);
05453 
05454                 DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Legacy speed status"
05455                          " = 0x%x\n", legacy_status);
05456                 ext_phy_link_up = ((legacy_status & (1<<11))
05457                            == (1<<11));
05458                 if (ext_phy_link_up) {
05459                     legacy_speed = (legacy_status & (3<<9));
05460                     if (legacy_speed == (0<<9))
05461                         vars->line_speed = SPEED_10;
05462                     else if (legacy_speed == (1<<9))
05463                         vars->line_speed =
05464                             SPEED_100;
05465                     else if (legacy_speed == (2<<9))
05466                         vars->line_speed =
05467                             SPEED_1000;
05468                     else /* Should not happen */
05469                         vars->line_speed = 0;
05470 
05471                     if (legacy_status & (1<<8))
05472                         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
05473                     else
05474                         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
05475 
05476                     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Link is up "
05477                              "in %dMbps, is_duplex_full"
05478                              "= %d\n",
05479                         vars->line_speed,
05480                         (vars->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL));
05481                     bnx2x_8481_set_legacy_led_mode(params,
05482                                  ext_phy_type,
05483                                  ext_phy_addr);
05484                 }
05485             }
05486             break;
05487         default:
05488             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "BAD XGXS ext_phy_config 0x%x\n",
05489                params->ext_phy_config);
05490             ext_phy_link_up = 0;
05491             break;
05492         }
05493         /* Set SGMII mode for external phy */
05494         if (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) {
05495             if (vars->line_speed < SPEED_1000)
05496                 vars->phy_flags |= PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
05497             else
05498                 vars->phy_flags &= ~PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
05499         }
05500 
05501     } else { /* SerDes */
05502         ext_phy_type = SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
05503         switch (ext_phy_type) {
05504         case PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
05505             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes Direct\n");
05506             ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05507             break;
05508 
05509         case PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM5482:
05510             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes 5482\n");
05511             ext_phy_link_up = 1;
05512             break;
05513 
05514         default:
05515             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05516                  "BAD SerDes ext_phy_config 0x%x\n",
05517                  params->ext_phy_config);
05518             ext_phy_link_up = 0;
05519             break;
05520         }
05521     }
05522 
05523     return ext_phy_link_up;
05524 }
05525 
05526 static void bnx2x_link_int_enable(struct link_params *params)
05527 {
05528     u8 port = params->port;
05529     u32 ext_phy_type;
05530     u32 mask;
05531     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
05532 
05533     /* setting the status to report on link up
05534        for either XGXS or SerDes */
05535 
05536     if (params->switch_cfg == SWITCH_CFG_10G) {
05537         mask = (NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK10G |
05538             NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS);
05539         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enabled XGXS interrupt\n");
05540         ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
05541         if ((ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) &&
05542             (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_FAILURE) &&
05543             (ext_phy_type !=
05544                 PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_NOT_CONN)) {
05545             mask |= NIG_MASK_MI_INT;
05546             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enabled external phy int\n");
05547         }
05548 
05549     } else { /* SerDes */
05550         mask = NIG_MASK_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS;
05551         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enabled SerDes interrupt\n");
05552         ext_phy_type = SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
05553         if ((ext_phy_type !=
05554                 PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) &&
05555             (ext_phy_type !=
05556                 PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_NOT_CONN)) {
05557             mask |= NIG_MASK_MI_INT;
05558             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "enabled external phy int\n");
05559         }
05560     }
05561     bnx2x_bits_en(bp,
05562               NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
05563               mask);
05564 
05565     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "port %x, is_xgxs %x, int_status 0x%x\n", port,
05566          (params->switch_cfg == SWITCH_CFG_10G),
05567          REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4));
05568     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, " int_mask 0x%x, MI_INT %x, SERDES_LINK %x\n",
05569          REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4),
05570          REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_STATUS_MISC_MI_INT + port*0x18),
05571          REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_SERDES0_STATUS_LINK_STATUS+port*0x3c));
05572     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, " 10G %x, XGXS_LINK %x\n",
05573        REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_STATUS_LINK10G + port*0x68),
05574        REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_STATUS_LINK_STATUS + port*0x68));
05575 }
05576 
05577 static void bnx2x_8481_rearm_latch_signal(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
05578                     u8 is_mi_int)
05579 {
05580     u32 latch_status = 0, is_mi_int_status;
05581     /* Disable the MI INT ( external phy int )
05582      * by writing 1 to the status register. Link down indication
05583      * is high-active-signal, so in this case we need to write the
05584      * status to clear the XOR
05585      */
05586     /* Read Latched signals */
05587     latch_status = REG_RD(bp,
05588                   NIG_REG_LATCH_STATUS_0 + port*8);
05589     is_mi_int_status = REG_RD(bp,
05590                   NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4);
05591     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "original_signal = 0x%x, nig_status = 0x%x,"
05592              "latch_status = 0x%x\n",
05593          is_mi_int, is_mi_int_status, latch_status);
05594     /* Handle only those with latched-signal=up.*/
05595     if (latch_status & 1) {
05596         /* For all latched-signal=up,Write original_signal to status */
05597         if (is_mi_int)
05598             bnx2x_bits_en(bp,
05599                     NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0
05600                     + port*4,
05601                     NIG_STATUS_EMAC0_MI_INT);
05602         else
05603             bnx2x_bits_dis(bp,
05604                      NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0
05605                      + port*4,
05606                      NIG_STATUS_EMAC0_MI_INT);
05607         /* For all latched-signal=up : Re-Arm Latch signals */
05608         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LATCH_STATUS_0 + port*8,
05609                (latch_status & 0xfffe) | (latch_status & 1));
05610     }
05611 }
05612 /*
05613  * link management
05614  */
05615 static void bnx2x_link_int_ack(struct link_params *params,
05616                  struct link_vars *vars, u8 is_10g,
05617                  u8 is_mi_int)
05618 {
05619     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
05620     u8 port = params->port;
05621 
05622     /* first reset all status
05623      * we assume only one line will be change at a time */
05624     bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
05625              (NIG_STATUS_XGXS0_LINK10G |
05626               NIG_STATUS_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS |
05627               NIG_STATUS_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS));
05628     if ((XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config)
05629         == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481) ||
05630     (XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config)
05631         == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823)) {
05632         bnx2x_8481_rearm_latch_signal(bp, port, is_mi_int);
05633     }
05634     if (vars->phy_link_up) {
05635         if (is_10g) {
05636             /* Disable the 10G link interrupt
05637              * by writing 1 to the status register
05638              */
05639             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "10G XGXS phy link up\n");
05640             bnx2x_bits_en(bp,
05641                       NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
05642                       NIG_STATUS_XGXS0_LINK10G);
05643 
05644         } else if (params->switch_cfg == SWITCH_CFG_10G) {
05645             /* Disable the link interrupt
05646              * by writing 1 to the relevant lane
05647              * in the status register
05648              */
05649             u32 ser_lane = ((params->lane_config &
05650                     PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_MASK) >>
05651                     PORT_HW_CFG_LANE_SWAP_CFG_MASTER_SHIFT);
05652 
05653             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "%d speed XGXS phy link up\n",
05654                  vars->line_speed);
05655             bnx2x_bits_en(bp,
05656                       NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
05657                       ((1 << ser_lane) <<
05658                        NIG_STATUS_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS_SIZE));
05659 
05660         } else { /* SerDes */
05661             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "SerDes phy link up\n");
05662             /* Disable the link interrupt
05663              * by writing 1 to the status register
05664              */
05665             bnx2x_bits_en(bp,
05666                       NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
05667                       NIG_STATUS_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS);
05668         }
05669 
05670     } else { /* link_down */
05671     }
05672 }
05673 
05674 static u8 bnx2x_format_ver(u32 num, u8 *str, u16 len)
05675 {
05676     u8 *str_ptr = str;
05677     u32 mask = 0xf0000000;
05678     u8 shift = 8*4;
05679     u8 digit;
05680     if (len < 10) {
05681         /* Need more than 10chars for this format */
05682         *str_ptr = '\0';
05683         return -EINVAL;
05684     }
05685     while (shift > 0) {
05686 
05687         shift -= 4;
05688         digit = ((num & mask) >> shift);
05689         if (digit < 0xa)
05690             *str_ptr = digit + '0';
05691         else
05692             *str_ptr = digit - 0xa + 'a';
05693         str_ptr++;
05694         mask = mask >> 4;
05695         if (shift == 4*4) {
05696             *str_ptr = ':';
05697             str_ptr++;
05698         }
05699     }
05700     *str_ptr = '\0';
05701     return 0;
05702 }
05703 
05704 u8 bnx2x_get_ext_phy_fw_version(struct link_params *params, u8 driver_loaded,
05705                   u8 *version, u16 len)
05706 {
05707     struct bnx2x *bp;
05708     u32 ext_phy_type = 0;
05709     u32 spirom_ver = 0;
05710     u8 status;
05711 
05712     if (version == NULL || params == NULL)
05713         return -EINVAL;
05714     bp = params->bp;
05715 
05716     spirom_ver = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
05717            offsetof(struct shmem_region,
05718                 port_mb[params->port].ext_phy_fw_version));
05719 
05720     status = 0;
05721     /* reset the returned value to zero */
05722     ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
05723     switch (ext_phy_type) {
05724     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101:
05725 
05726         if (len < 5)
05727             return -EINVAL;
05728 
05729         version[0] = (spirom_ver & 0xFF);
05730         version[1] = (spirom_ver & 0xFF00) >> 8;
05731         version[2] = (spirom_ver & 0xFF0000) >> 16;
05732         version[3] = (spirom_ver & 0xFF000000) >> 24;
05733         version[4] = '\0';
05734 
05735         break;
05736     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
05737     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
05738     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
05739     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706:
05740     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
05741         status = bnx2x_format_ver(spirom_ver, version, len);
05742         break;
05743     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481:
05744     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
05745         spirom_ver = ((spirom_ver & 0xF80) >> 7) << 16 |
05746             (spirom_ver & 0x7F);
05747         status = bnx2x_format_ver(spirom_ver, version, len);
05748         break;
05749     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
05750     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705:
05751         version[0] = '\0';
05752         break;
05753 
05754     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_FAILURE:
05755         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_get_ext_phy_fw_version:"
05756                     " type is FAILURE!\n");
05757         status = -EINVAL;
05758         break;
05759 
05760     default:
05761         break;
05762     }
05763     return status;
05764 }
05765 
05766 static void bnx2x_set_xgxs_loopback(struct link_params *params,
05767                   struct link_vars *vars,
05768                   u8 is_10g)
05769 {
05770     u8 port = params->port;
05771     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
05772 
05773     if (is_10g) {
05774         u32 md_devad;
05775 
05776         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 10G loopback enable\n");
05777 
05778         /* change the uni_phy_addr in the nig */
05779         md_devad = REG_RD(bp, (NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_MD_DEVAD +
05780                       port*0x18));
05781 
05782         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_MD_DEVAD + port*0x18, 0x5);
05783 
05784         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, 0,
05785                    params->phy_addr,
05786                    5,
05787                    (MDIO_REG_BANK_AER_BLOCK +
05788                 (MDIO_AER_BLOCK_AER_REG & 0xf)),
05789                    0x2800);
05790 
05791         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port, 0,
05792                    params->phy_addr,
05793                    5,
05794                    (MDIO_REG_BANK_CL73_IEEEB0 +
05795                 (MDIO_CL73_IEEEB0_CL73_AN_CONTROL & 0xf)),
05796                    0x6041);
05797         msleep(200);
05798         /* set aer mmd back */
05799         bnx2x_set_aer_mmd(params, vars);
05800 
05801         /* and md_devad */
05802         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_MD_DEVAD + port*0x18,
05803                 md_devad);
05804 
05805     } else {
05806         u16 mii_control;
05807 
05808         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "XGXS 1G loopback enable\n");
05809 
05810         CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, port,
05811                       params->phy_addr,
05812                       MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
05813                       MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
05814                       &mii_control);
05815 
05816         CL45_WR_OVER_CL22(bp, port,
05817                       params->phy_addr,
05818                       MDIO_REG_BANK_COMBO_IEEE0,
05819                       MDIO_COMBO_IEEE0_MII_CONTROL,
05820                       (mii_control |
05821                        MDIO_COMBO_IEEO_MII_CONTROL_LOOPBACK));
05822     }
05823 }
05824 
05825 
05826 static void bnx2x_ext_phy_loopback(struct link_params *params)
05827 {
05828     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
05829     u8 ext_phy_addr;
05830     u32 ext_phy_type;
05831 
05832     if (params->switch_cfg == SWITCH_CFG_10G) {
05833         ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
05834         ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
05835         /* CL37 Autoneg Enabled */
05836         switch (ext_phy_type) {
05837         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
05838         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_NOT_CONN:
05839             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05840                 "ext_phy_loopback: We should not get here\n");
05841             break;
05842         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705:
05843             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "ext_phy_loopback: 8705\n");
05844             break;
05845         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706:
05846             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "ext_phy_loopback: 8706\n");
05847             break;
05848         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
05849             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "PMA/PMD ext_phy_loopback: 8726\n");
05850             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05851                        ext_phy_addr,
05852                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
05853                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
05854                        0x0001);
05855             break;
05856         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101:
05857             /* SFX7101_XGXS_TEST1 */
05858             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, params->port, ext_phy_type,
05859                        ext_phy_addr,
05860                        MDIO_XS_DEVAD,
05861                        MDIO_XS_SFX7101_XGXS_TEST1,
05862                        0x100);
05863             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05864                 "ext_phy_loopback: set ext phy loopback\n");
05865             break;
05866         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
05867 
05868             break;
05869         } /* switch external PHY type */
05870     } else {
05871         /* serdes */
05872         ext_phy_type = SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
05873         ext_phy_addr = (params->ext_phy_config  &
05874         PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_ADDR_MASK)
05875         >> PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_ADDR_SHIFT;
05876     }
05877 }
05878 
05879 
05880 /*
05881  *------------------------------------------------------------------------
05882  * bnx2x_override_led_value -
05883  *
05884  * Override the led value of the requsted led
05885  *
05886  *------------------------------------------------------------------------
05887  */
05888 u8 bnx2x_override_led_value(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port,
05889               u32 led_idx, u32 value)
05890 {
05891     u32 reg_val;
05892 
05893     /* If port 0 then use EMAC0, else use EMAC1*/
05894     u32 emac_base = (port) ? GRCBASE_EMAC1 : GRCBASE_EMAC0;
05895 
05896     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05897          "bnx2x_override_led_value() port %x led_idx %d value %d\n",
05898          port, led_idx, value);
05899 
05900     switch (led_idx) {
05901     case 0: /* 10MB led */
05902         /* Read the current value of the LED register in
05903         the EMAC block */
05904         reg_val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
05905         /* Set the OVERRIDE bit to 1 */
05906         reg_val |= EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE;
05907         /* If value is 1, set the 10M_OVERRIDE bit,
05908         otherwise reset it.*/
05909         reg_val = (value == 1) ? (reg_val | EMAC_LED_10MB_OVERRIDE) :
05910             (reg_val & ~EMAC_LED_10MB_OVERRIDE);
05911         REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED, reg_val);
05912         break;
05913     case 1: /*100MB led    */
05914         /*Read the current value of the LED register in
05915         the EMAC block */
05916         reg_val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
05917         /*  Set the OVERRIDE bit to 1 */
05918         reg_val |= EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE;
05919         /*  If value is 1, set the 100M_OVERRIDE bit,
05920         otherwise reset it.*/
05921         reg_val = (value == 1) ? (reg_val | EMAC_LED_100MB_OVERRIDE) :
05922             (reg_val & ~EMAC_LED_100MB_OVERRIDE);
05923         REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED, reg_val);
05924         break;
05925     case 2: /* 1000MB led */
05926         /* Read the current value of the LED register in the
05927         EMAC block */
05928         reg_val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
05929         /* Set the OVERRIDE bit to 1 */
05930         reg_val |= EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE;
05931         /* If value is 1, set the 1000M_OVERRIDE bit, otherwise
05932         reset it. */
05933         reg_val = (value == 1) ? (reg_val | EMAC_LED_1000MB_OVERRIDE) :
05934             (reg_val & ~EMAC_LED_1000MB_OVERRIDE);
05935         REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED, reg_val);
05936         break;
05937     case 3: /* 2500MB led */
05938         /*  Read the current value of the LED register in the
05939         EMAC block*/
05940         reg_val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
05941         /* Set the OVERRIDE bit to 1 */
05942         reg_val |= EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE;
05943         /*  If value is 1, set the 2500M_OVERRIDE bit, otherwise
05944         reset it.*/
05945         reg_val = (value == 1) ? (reg_val | EMAC_LED_2500MB_OVERRIDE) :
05946             (reg_val & ~EMAC_LED_2500MB_OVERRIDE);
05947         REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED, reg_val);
05948         break;
05949     case 4: /*10G led */
05950         if (port == 0) {
05951             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_10G_P0,
05952                     value);
05953         } else {
05954             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_10G_P1,
05955                     value);
05956         }
05957         break;
05958     case 5: /* TRAFFIC led */
05959         /* Find if the traffic control is via BMAC or EMAC */
05960         if (port == 0)
05961             reg_val = REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_EMAC0_EN);
05962         else
05963             reg_val = REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_EMAC1_EN);
05964 
05965         /*  Override the traffic led in the EMAC:*/
05966         if (reg_val == 1) {
05967             /* Read the current value of the LED register in
05968             the EMAC block */
05969             reg_val = REG_RD(bp, emac_base +
05970                          EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
05971             /* Set the TRAFFIC_OVERRIDE bit to 1 */
05972             reg_val |= EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE;
05973             /* If value is 1, set the TRAFFIC bit, otherwise
05974             reset it.*/
05975             reg_val = (value == 1) ? (reg_val | EMAC_LED_TRAFFIC) :
05976                 (reg_val & ~EMAC_LED_TRAFFIC);
05977             REG_WR(bp, emac_base + EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED, reg_val);
05978         } else { /* Override the traffic led in the BMAC: */
