05979             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_OVERRIDE_TRAFFIC_P0
05980                    + port*4, 1);
05981             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_TRAFFIC_P0 + port*4,
05982                     value);
05983         }
05984         break;
05985     default:
05986         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
05987              "bnx2x_override_led_value() unknown led index %d "
05988              "(should be 0-5)\n", led_idx);
05989         return -EINVAL;
05990     }
05991 
05992     return 0;
05993 }
05994 
05995 
05996 u8 bnx2x_set_led(struct link_params *params, u8 mode, u32 speed)
05997 {
05998     u8 port = params->port;
05999     u16 hw_led_mode = params->hw_led_mode;
06000     u8 rc = 0;
06001     u32 tmp;
06002     u32 emac_base = port ? GRCBASE_EMAC1 : GRCBASE_EMAC0;
06003     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
06004     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06005     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_set_led: port %x, mode %d\n", port, mode);
06006     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "speed 0x%x, hw_led_mode 0x%x\n",
06007          speed, hw_led_mode);
06008     switch (mode) {
06009     case LED_MODE_OFF:
06010         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_10G_P0 + port*4, 0);
06011         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_MODE_P0 + port*4,
06012                SHARED_HW_CFG_LED_MAC1);
06013 
06014         tmp = EMAC_RD(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
06015         EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED, (tmp | EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE));
06016         break;
06017 
06018     case LED_MODE_OPER:
06019         if (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) {
06020             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_MODE_P0 + port*4, 0);
06021             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_10G_P0 + port*4, 1);
06022         } else {
06023             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_MODE_P0 + port*4,
06024                    hw_led_mode);
06025         }
06026 
06027         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_OVERRIDE_TRAFFIC_P0 +
06028                port*4, 0);
06029         /* Set blinking rate to ~15.9Hz */
06030         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_BLINK_RATE_P0 + port*4,
06031                LED_BLINK_RATE_VAL);
06032         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_BLINK_RATE_ENA_P0 +
06033                port*4, 1);
06034         tmp = EMAC_RD(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED);
06035         EMAC_WR(bp, EMAC_REG_EMAC_LED,
06036                 (tmp & (~EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE)));
06037 
06038         if (CHIP_IS_E1(bp) &&
06039             ((speed == SPEED_2500) ||
06040              (speed == SPEED_1000) ||
06041              (speed == SPEED_100) ||
06042              (speed == SPEED_10))) {
06043             /* On Everest 1 Ax chip versions for speeds less than
06044             10G LED scheme is different */
06045             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_OVERRIDE_TRAFFIC_P0
06046                    + port*4, 1);
06047             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_TRAFFIC_P0 +
06048                    port*4, 0);
06049             REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_LED_CONTROL_BLINK_TRAFFIC_P0 +
06050                    port*4, 1);
06051         }
06052         break;
06053 
06054     default:
06055         rc = -EINVAL;
06056         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_set_led: Invalid led mode %d\n",
06057              mode);
06058         break;
06059     }
06060     return rc;
06061 
06062 }
06063 
06064 u8 bnx2x_test_link(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars)
06065 {
06066     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06067     u16 gp_status = 0;
06068 
06069     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, params->port,
06070                   params->phy_addr,
06071                   MDIO_REG_BANK_GP_STATUS,
06072                   MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1,
06073                   &gp_status);
06074     /* link is up only if both local phy and external phy are up */
06075     if ((gp_status & MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1_LINK_STATUS) &&
06076         bnx2x_ext_phy_is_link_up(params, vars, 1))
06077         return 0;
06078 
06079     return -ESRCH;
06080 }
06081 
06082 static u8 bnx2x_link_initialize(struct link_params *params,
06083                   struct link_vars *vars)
06084 {
06085     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06086     u8 port = params->port;
06087     u8 rc = 0;
06088     u8 non_ext_phy;
06089     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
06090 
06091     /* Activate the external PHY */
06092     bnx2x_ext_phy_reset(params, vars);
06093 
06094     bnx2x_set_aer_mmd(params, vars);
06095 
06096     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG)
06097         bnx2x_set_master_ln(params);
06098 
06099     rc = bnx2x_reset_unicore(params);
06100     /* reset the SerDes and wait for reset bit return low */
06101     if (rc != 0)
06102         return rc;
06103 
06104     bnx2x_set_aer_mmd(params, vars);
06105 
06106     /* setting the masterLn_def again after the reset */
06107     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
06108         bnx2x_set_master_ln(params);
06109         bnx2x_set_swap_lanes(params);
06110     }
06111 
06112     if (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG) {
06113         if ((params->req_line_speed &&
06114             ((params->req_line_speed == SPEED_100) ||
06115              (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_10))) ||
06116             (!params->req_line_speed &&
06117              (params->speed_cap_mask >=
06118                PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_10M_FULL) &&
06119              (params->speed_cap_mask <
06120                PORT_HW_CFG_SPEED_CAPABILITY_D0_1G)
06121              ))  {
06122             vars->phy_flags |= PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
06123         } else {
06124             vars->phy_flags &= ~PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
06125         }
06126     }
06127     /* In case of external phy existance, the line speed would be the
06128      line speed linked up by the external phy. In case it is direct only,
06129       then the line_speed during initialization will be equal to the
06130        req_line_speed*/
06131     vars->line_speed = params->req_line_speed;
06132 
06133     bnx2x_calc_ieee_aneg_adv(params, &vars->ieee_fc);
06134 
06135     /* init ext phy and enable link state int */
06136     non_ext_phy = ((ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) ||
06137                (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_XGXS_10));
06138 
06139     if (non_ext_phy ||
06140         (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705) ||
06141         (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706) ||
06142         (ext_phy_type == PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726) ||
06143         (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_EXT_PHY)) {
06144         if (params->req_line_speed == SPEED_AUTO_NEG)
06145             bnx2x_set_parallel_detection(params, vars->phy_flags);
06146         bnx2x_init_internal_phy(params, vars, non_ext_phy);
06147     }
06148 
06149     if (!non_ext_phy)
06150         rc |= bnx2x_ext_phy_init(params, vars);
06151 
06152     bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
06153              (NIG_STATUS_XGXS0_LINK10G |
06154               NIG_STATUS_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS |
06155               NIG_STATUS_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS));
06156 
06157     return rc;
06158 
06159 }
06160 
06161 
06162 u8 bnx2x_phy_init(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars)
06163 {
06164     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06165     u32 val;
06166 
06167     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Phy Initialization started\n");
06168     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "req_speed %d, req_flowctrl %d\n",
06169          params->req_line_speed, params->req_flow_ctrl);
06170     vars->link_status = 0;
06171     vars->phy_link_up = 0;
06172     vars->link_up = 0;
06173     vars->line_speed = 0;
06174     vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
06175     vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
06176     vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_NONE;
06177 
06178     if (params->switch_cfg ==  SWITCH_CFG_1G)
06179         vars->phy_flags = PHY_SERDES_FLAG;
06180     else
06181         vars->phy_flags = PHY_XGXS_FLAG;
06182 
06183     /* disable attentions */
06184     bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + params->port*4,
06185                (NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS |
06186             NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK10G |
06187             NIG_MASK_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS |
06188             NIG_MASK_MI_INT));
06189 
06190     bnx2x_emac_init(params, vars);
06191 
06192     if (CHIP_REV_IS_FPGA(bp)) {
06193 
06194         vars->link_up = 1;
06195         vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
06196         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
06197         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
06198         vars->link_status = (LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP | LINK_10GTFD);
06199         /* enable on E1.5 FPGA */
06200         if (!CHIP_IS_E1(bp)) {
06201             vars->flow_ctrl |=
06202                     (BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_TX |
06203                      BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_RX);
06204             vars->link_status |=
06205                     (LINK_STATUS_TX_FLOW_CONTROL_ENABLED |
06206                      LINK_STATUS_RX_FLOW_CONTROL_ENABLED);
06207         }
06208 
06209         bnx2x_emac_enable(params, vars, 0);
06210         if (!(CHIP_IS_E2_NOT_PHASE0(params->chip_id)))
06211             bnx2x_pbf_update(params, vars->flow_ctrl,
06212                        vars->line_speed);
06213         /* disable drain */
06214         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE + params->port*4, 0);
06215 
06216         /* update shared memory */
06217         bnx2x_update_mng(params, vars->link_status);
06218 
06219         return 0;
06220 
06221     } else
06222     if (CHIP_REV_IS_EMUL(bp)) {
06223 
06224         vars->link_up = 1;
06225         vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
06226         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
06227         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
06228         vars->link_status = (LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP | LINK_10GTFD);
06229 
06230         bnx2x_bmac_enable(params, vars, 0);
06231 
06232         if (!(CHIP_IS_E2_NOT_PHASE0(params->chip_id)))
06233             bnx2x_pbf_update(params, vars->flow_ctrl,
06234                        vars->line_speed);
06235         /* Disable drain */
06236         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE
06237                     + params->port*4, 0);
06238 
06239         /* update shared memory */
06240         bnx2x_update_mng(params, vars->link_status);
06241 
06242         return 0;
06243 
06244     } else
06245     if (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_BMAC) {
06246 
06247         vars->link_up = 1;
06248         vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
06249         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
06250         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
06251         vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_BMAC;
06252 
06253         vars->phy_flags = PHY_XGXS_FLAG;
06254 
06255         bnx2x_phy_deassert(params, vars->phy_flags);
06256         /* set bmac loopback */
06257         bnx2x_bmac_enable(params, vars, 1);
06258 
06259         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE +
06260             params->port*4, 0);
06261 
06262     } else if (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_EMAC) {
06263 
06264         vars->link_up = 1;
06265         vars->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
06266         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
06267         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
06268         vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_EMAC;
06269 
06270         vars->phy_flags = PHY_XGXS_FLAG;
06271 
06272         bnx2x_phy_deassert(params, vars->phy_flags);
06273         /* set bmac loopback */
06274         bnx2x_emac_enable(params, vars, 1);
06275         bnx2x_emac_program(params, vars->line_speed,
06276                           vars->duplex);
06277         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE +
06278             params->port*4, 0);
06279 
06280     } else if ((params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_XGXS_10) ||
06281            (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_EXT_PHY)) {
06282 
06283         vars->link_up = 1;
06284         vars->line_speed = SPEED_10000;
06285         vars->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
06286         vars->flow_ctrl = BNX2X_FLOW_CTRL_NONE;
06287 
06288         vars->phy_flags = PHY_XGXS_FLAG;
06289 
06290         val = REG_RD(bp,
06291                  NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_PHY_ADDR+
06292                  params->port*0x18);
06293         params->phy_addr = (u8)val;
06294 
06295         bnx2x_phy_deassert(params, vars->phy_flags);
06296         bnx2x_link_initialize(params, vars);
06297 
06298         vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_BMAC;
06299 
06300         bnx2x_bmac_enable(params, vars, 0);
06301 
06302         if (params->loopback_mode == LOOPBACK_XGXS_10) {
06303             /* set 10G XGXS loopback */
06304             bnx2x_set_xgxs_loopback(params, vars, 1);
06305         } else {
06306             /* set external phy loopback */
06307             bnx2x_ext_phy_loopback(params);
06308         }
06309         REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE +
06310                 params->port*4, 0);
06311 
06312         bnx2x_set_led(params, LED_MODE_OPER, vars->line_speed);
06313     } else
06314     /* No loopback */
06315     {
06316         bnx2x_phy_deassert(params, vars->phy_flags);
06317         switch (params->switch_cfg) {
06318         case SWITCH_CFG_1G:
06319             vars->phy_flags |= PHY_SERDES_FLAG;
06320             if ((params->ext_phy_config &
06321                  PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_MASK) ==
06322                  PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM5482) {
06323                 vars->phy_flags |= PHY_SGMII_FLAG;
06324             }
06325 
06326             val = REG_RD(bp,
06327                      NIG_REG_SERDES0_CTRL_PHY_ADDR+
06328                      params->port*0x10);
06329 
06330             params->phy_addr = (u8)val;
06331 
06332             break;
06333         case SWITCH_CFG_10G:
06334             vars->phy_flags |= PHY_XGXS_FLAG;
06335             val = REG_RD(bp,
06336                  NIG_REG_XGXS0_CTRL_PHY_ADDR+
06337                  params->port*0x18);
06338             params->phy_addr = (u8)val;
06339 
06340             break;
06341         default:
06342             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Invalid switch_cfg\n");
06343             return -EINVAL;
06344         }
06345         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Phy address = 0x%x\n", params->phy_addr);
06346 
06347         bnx2x_link_initialize(params, vars);
06348         msleep(30);
06349         bnx2x_link_int_enable(params);
06350     }
06351     return 0;
06352 }
06353 
06354 static void bnx2x_8726_reset_phy(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port, u8 ext_phy_addr)
06355 {
06356     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "bnx2x_8726_reset_phy port %d\n", port);
06357 
06358     /* Set serial boot control for external load */
06359     bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06360                PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726, ext_phy_addr,
06361                MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06362                MDIO_PMA_REG_GEN_CTRL, 0x0001);
06363 }
06364 
06365 u8 bnx2x_link_reset(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars,
06366           u8 reset_ext_phy)
06367 {
06368     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06369     u32 ext_phy_config = params->ext_phy_config;
06370     u8 port = params->port;
06371     u32 ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(ext_phy_config);
06372     u32 val = REG_RD(bp, params->shmem_base +
06373                  offsetof(struct shmem_region, dev_info.
06374                       port_feature_config[params->port].
06375                       config));
06376     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Resetting the link of port %d\n", port);
06377     /* disable attentions */
06378     vars->link_status = 0;
06379     bnx2x_update_mng(params, vars->link_status);
06380     bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
06381              (NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS |
06382               NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK10G |
06383               NIG_MASK_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS |
06384               NIG_MASK_MI_INT));
06385 
06386     /* activate nig drain */
06387     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE + port*4, 1);
06388 
06389     /* disable nig egress interface */
06390     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0);
06391     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_EMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0);
06392 
06393     /* Stop BigMac rx */
06394     bnx2x_bmac_rx_disable(bp, params->chip_id, port);
06395 
06396     /* disable emac */
06397     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_EMAC0_EN + port*4, 0);
06398 
06399     msleep(10);
06400     /* The PHY reset is controled by GPIO 1
06401      * Hold it as vars low
06402      */
06403      /* clear link led */
06404     bnx2x_set_led(params, LED_MODE_OFF, 0);
06405     if (reset_ext_phy) {
06406         switch (ext_phy_type) {
06407         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT:
06408         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8072:
06409             break;
06410 
06411         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
06412         {
06413 
06414             /* Disable Transmitter */
06415             u8 ext_phy_addr =
06416                 XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
06417             if ((val & PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_MASK) ==
06418                 PORT_FEAT_CFG_OPT_MDL_ENFRCMNT_DISABLE_TX_LASER)
06419                 bnx2x_sfp_set_transmitter(bp, port,
06420                     PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
06421                     ext_phy_addr, 0);
06422             break;
06423         }
06424         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
06425             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Setting 8073 port %d into "
06426                  "low power mode\n",
06427                  port);
06428             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
06429                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_LOW,
06430                       port);
06431             break;
06432         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
06433         {
06434             u8 ext_phy_addr =
06435                 XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
06436             /* Set soft reset */
06437             bnx2x_8726_reset_phy(bp, params->port, ext_phy_addr);
06438             break;
06439         }
06440         case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
06441         {
06442             u8 ext_phy_addr =
06443                 XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(params->ext_phy_config);
06444             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06445                        PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
06446                        ext_phy_addr,
06447                        MDIO_AN_DEVAD,
06448                        MDIO_AN_REG_CTRL, 0x0000);
06449             bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06450                        PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8481,
06451                        ext_phy_addr,
06452                        MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06453                        MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL, 1);
06454             break;
06455         }
06456         default:
06457             /* HW reset */
06458             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_1,
06459                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_LOW,
06460                       port);
06461             bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
06462                       MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_LOW,
06463                       port);
06464             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "reset external PHY\n");
06465         }
06466     }
06467     /* reset the SerDes/XGXS */
06468     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_3_CLEAR,
06469            (0x1ff << (port*16)));
06470 
06471     /* reset BigMac */
06472     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC + MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_CLEAR,
06473            (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_BMAC0 << port));
06474 
06475     /* disable nig ingress interface */
06476     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_IN_EN + port*4, 0);
06477     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_IN_EN + port*4, 0);
06478     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_BMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0);
06479     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_EMAC0_OUT_EN + port*4, 0);
06480     vars->link_up = 0;
06481     return 0;
06482 }
06483 
06484 static u8 bnx2x_update_link_down(struct link_params *params,
06485                    struct link_vars *vars)
06486 {
06487     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06488     u8 port = params->port;
06489 
06490     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Port %x: Link is down\n", port);
06491     bnx2x_set_led(params, LED_MODE_OFF, 0);
06492 
06493     /* indicate no mac active */
06494     vars->mac_type = MAC_TYPE_NONE;
06495 
06496     /* update shared memory */
06497     vars->link_status = 0;
06498     vars->line_speed = 0;
06499     bnx2x_update_mng(params, vars->link_status);
06500 
06501     /* activate nig drain */
06502     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE + port*4, 1);
06503 
06504     /* disable emac */
06505     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_EMAC0_EN + port*4, 0);
06506 
06507     msleep(10);
06508 
06509     /* reset BigMac */
06510     bnx2x_bmac_rx_disable(bp, params->chip_id, params->port);
06511     REG_WR(bp, GRCBASE_MISC +
06512            MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_CLEAR,
06513            (MISC_REGISTERS_RESET_REG_2_RST_BMAC0 << port));
06514     return 0;
06515 }
06516 
06517 static u8 bnx2x_update_link_up(struct link_params *params,
06518                  struct link_vars *vars,
06519                  u8 link_10g, u32 gp_status)
06520 {
06521     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06522     u8 port = params->port;
06523     u8 rc = 0;
06524 
06525     vars->link_status |= LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP;
06526     if (link_10g) {
06527         bnx2x_bmac_enable(params, vars, 0);
06528         bnx2x_set_led(params, LED_MODE_OPER, SPEED_10000);
06529     } else {
06530         rc = bnx2x_emac_program(params, vars->line_speed,
06531                       vars->duplex);
06532 
06533         bnx2x_emac_enable(params, vars, 0);
06534 
06535         /* AN complete? */
06536         if (gp_status & MDIO_AN_CL73_OR_37_COMPLETE) {
06537             if (!(vars->phy_flags &
06538                   PHY_SGMII_FLAG))
06539                 bnx2x_set_gmii_tx_driver(params);
06540         }
06541     }
06542 
06543     /* PBF - link up */
06544     if (!(CHIP_IS_E2_NOT_PHASE0(params->chip_id)))
06545         rc |= bnx2x_pbf_update(params, vars->flow_ctrl,
06546                      vars->line_speed);
06547 
06548     /* disable drain */
06549     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_EGRESS_DRAIN0_MODE + port*4, 0);
06550 
06551     /* update shared memory */
06552     bnx2x_update_mng(params, vars->link_status);
06553     msleep(20);
06554     return rc;
06555 }
06556 /* This function should called upon link interrupt */
06557 /* In case vars->link_up, driver needs to
06558     1. Update the pbf
06559     2. Disable drain
06560     3. Update the shared memory
06561     4. Indicate link up
06562     5. Set LEDs
06563    Otherwise,
06564     1. Update shared memory
06565     2. Reset BigMac
06566     3. Report link down
06567     4. Unset LEDs
06568 */
06569 u8 bnx2x_link_update(struct link_params *params, struct link_vars *vars)
06570 {
06571     struct bnx2x *bp = params->bp;
06572     u8 port = params->port;
06573     u16 gp_status;
06574     u8 link_10g;
06575     u8 ext_phy_link_up, rc = 0;
06576     u32 ext_phy_type;
06577     u8 is_mi_int = 0;
06578 
06579     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "port %x, XGXS?%x, int_status 0x%x\n",
06580          port, (vars->phy_flags & PHY_XGXS_FLAG),
06581          REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_STATUS_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4));
06582 
06583     is_mi_int = (u8)(REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_EMAC0_STATUS_MISC_MI_INT +
06584                     port*0x18) > 0);
06585     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "int_mask 0x%x MI_INT %x, SERDES_LINK %x\n",
06586          REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4),
06587          is_mi_int,
06588          REG_RD(bp,
06589                 NIG_REG_SERDES0_STATUS_LINK_STATUS + port*0x3c));
06590 
06591     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, " 10G %x, XGXS_LINK %x\n",
06592       REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_STATUS_LINK10G + port*0x68),
06593       REG_RD(bp, NIG_REG_XGXS0_STATUS_LINK_STATUS + port*0x68));
06594 
06595     /* disable emac */
06596     REG_WR(bp, NIG_REG_NIG_EMAC0_EN + port*4, 0);
06597 
06598     ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(params->ext_phy_config);
06599 
06600     /* Check external link change only for non-direct */
06601     ext_phy_link_up = bnx2x_ext_phy_is_link_up(params, vars, is_mi_int);
06602 
06603     /* Read gp_status */
06604     CL45_RD_OVER_CL22(bp, port, params->phy_addr,
06605                   MDIO_REG_BANK_GP_STATUS,
06606                   MDIO_GP_STATUS_TOP_AN_STATUS1,
06607                   &gp_status);
06608 
06609     rc = bnx2x_link_settings_status(params, vars, gp_status,
06610                       ext_phy_link_up);
06611     if (rc != 0)
06612         return rc;
06613 
06614     /* anything 10 and over uses the bmac */
06615     link_10g = ((vars->line_speed == SPEED_10000) ||
06616             (vars->line_speed == SPEED_12000) ||
06617             (vars->line_speed == SPEED_12500) ||
06618             (vars->line_speed == SPEED_13000) ||
06619             (vars->line_speed == SPEED_15000) ||
06620             (vars->line_speed == SPEED_16000));
06621 
06622     bnx2x_link_int_ack(params, vars, link_10g, is_mi_int);
06623 
06624     /* In case external phy link is up, and internal link is down
06625     ( not initialized yet probably after link initialization, it needs
06626     to be initialized.
06627     Note that after link down-up as result of cable plug,
06628     the xgxs link would probably become up again without the need to
06629     initialize it*/
06630 
06631     if ((ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_SERDES_EXT_PHY_TYPE_DIRECT) &&
06632         (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8705) &&
06633         (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8706) &&
06634         (ext_phy_type != PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726) &&
06635         (ext_phy_link_up && !vars->phy_link_up))
06636         bnx2x_init_internal_phy(params, vars, 0);
06637 
06638     /* link is up only if both local phy and external phy are up */
06639     vars->link_up = (ext_phy_link_up && vars->phy_link_up);
06640 
06641     if (vars->link_up)
06642         rc = bnx2x_update_link_up(params, vars, link_10g, gp_status);
06643     else
06644         rc = bnx2x_update_link_down(params, vars);
06645 
06646     return rc;
06647 }
06648 
06649 static u8 bnx2x_8073_common_init_phy(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 shmem_base)
06650 {
06651     u8 ext_phy_addr[PORT_MAX];
06652     u16 val;
06653     s8 port;
06654 
06655     /* PART1 - Reset both phys */
06656     for (port = PORT_MAX - 1; port >= PORT_0; port--) {
06657         /* Extract the ext phy address for the port */
06658         u32 ext_phy_config = REG_RD(bp, shmem_base +
06659                     offsetof(struct shmem_region,
06660            dev_info.port_hw_config[port].external_phy_config));
06661 
06662         /* disable attentions */
06663         bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
06664                  (NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS |
06665                   NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK10G |
06666                   NIG_MASK_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS |
06667                   NIG_MASK_MI_INT));
06668 
06669         ext_phy_addr[port] = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(ext_phy_config);
06670 
06671         /* Need to take the phy out of low power mode in order
06672             to write to access its registers */
06673         bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
06674                   MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_HIGH, port);
06675 
06676         /* Reset the phy */
06677         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06678                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06679                    ext_phy_addr[port],
06680                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06681                    MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
06682                    1<<15);
06683     }
06684 
06685     /* Add delay of 150ms after reset */
06686     msleep(150);
06687 
06688     /* PART2 - Download firmware to both phys */
06689     for (port = PORT_MAX - 1; port >= PORT_0; port--) {
06690         u16 fw_ver1;
06691 
06692         bnx2x_bcm8073_external_rom_boot(bp, port,
06693                           ext_phy_addr[port], shmem_base);
06694 
06695         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port, PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06696                   ext_phy_addr[port],
06697                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06698                   MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER1, &fw_ver1);
06699         if (fw_ver1 == 0 || fw_ver1 == 0x4321) {
06700             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
06701                  "bnx2x_8073_common_init_phy port %x:"
06702                  "Download failed. fw version = 0x%x\n",
06703                  port, fw_ver1);
06704             return -EINVAL;
06705         }
06706 
06707         /* Only set bit 10 = 1 (Tx power down) */
06708         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
06709                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06710                   ext_phy_addr[port],
06711                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06712                   MDIO_PMA_REG_TX_POWER_DOWN, &val);
06713 
06714         /* Phase1 of TX_POWER_DOWN reset */
06715         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06716                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06717                    ext_phy_addr[port],
06718                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06719                    MDIO_PMA_REG_TX_POWER_DOWN,
06720                    (val | 1<<10));
06721     }
06722 
06723     /* Toggle Transmitter: Power down and then up with 600ms
06724        delay between */
06725     msleep(600);
06726 
06727     /* PART3 - complete TX_POWER_DOWN process, and set GPIO2 back to low */
06728     for (port = PORT_MAX - 1; port >= PORT_0; port--) {
06729         /* Phase2 of POWER_DOWN_RESET */
06730         /* Release bit 10 (Release Tx power down) */
06731         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
06732                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06733                   ext_phy_addr[port],
06734                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06735                   MDIO_PMA_REG_TX_POWER_DOWN, &val);
06736 
06737         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06738                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06739                    ext_phy_addr[port],
06740                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06741                    MDIO_PMA_REG_TX_POWER_DOWN, (val & (~(1<<10))));
06742         msleep(15);
06743 
06744         /* Read modify write the SPI-ROM version select register */
06745         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
06746                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06747                   ext_phy_addr[port],
06748                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06749                   MDIO_PMA_REG_EDC_FFE_MAIN, &val);
06750         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06751                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073,
06752                   ext_phy_addr[port],
06753                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06754                   MDIO_PMA_REG_EDC_FFE_MAIN, (val | (1<<12)));
06755 
06756         /* set GPIO2 back to LOW */
06757         bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_2,
06758                   MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_OUTPUT_LOW, port);
06759     }
06760     return 0;
06761 
06762 }
06763 
06764 static u8 bnx2x_8727_common_init_phy(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 shmem_base)
06765 {
06766     u8 ext_phy_addr[PORT_MAX];
06767     s8 port, first_port, i;
06768     u32 swap_val, swap_override;
06769     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Executing BCM8727 common init\n");
06770     swap_val = REG_RD(bp,  NIG_REG_PORT_SWAP);
06771     swap_override = REG_RD(bp,  NIG_REG_STRAP_OVERRIDE);
06772 
06773     bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, 1 ^ (swap_val && swap_override));
06774     msleep(5);
06775 
06776     if (swap_val && swap_override)
06777         first_port = PORT_0;
06778     else
06779         first_port = PORT_1;
06780 
06781     /* PART1 - Reset both phys */
06782     for (i = 0, port = first_port; i < PORT_MAX; i++, port = !port) {
06783         /* Extract the ext phy address for the port */
06784         u32 ext_phy_config = REG_RD(bp, shmem_base +
06785                     offsetof(struct shmem_region,
06786            dev_info.port_hw_config[port].external_phy_config));
06787 
06788         /* disable attentions */
06789         bnx2x_bits_dis(bp, NIG_REG_MASK_INTERRUPT_PORT0 + port*4,
06790                  (NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK_STATUS |
06791                   NIG_MASK_XGXS0_LINK10G |
06792                   NIG_MASK_SERDES0_LINK_STATUS |
06793                   NIG_MASK_MI_INT));
06794 
06795         ext_phy_addr[port] = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(ext_phy_config);
06796 
06797         /* Reset the phy */
06798         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06799                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
06800                    ext_phy_addr[port],
06801                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06802                    MDIO_PMA_REG_CTRL,
06803                    1<<15);
06804     }
06805 
06806     /* Add delay of 150ms after reset */
06807     msleep(150);
06808 
06809     /* PART2 - Download firmware to both phys */
06810     for (i = 0, port = first_port; i < PORT_MAX; i++, port = !port) {
06811         u16 fw_ver1;
06812 
06813         bnx2x_bcm8727_external_rom_boot(bp, port,
06814                           ext_phy_addr[port], shmem_base);
06815 
06816         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port, PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727,
06817                   ext_phy_addr[port],
06818                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06819                   MDIO_PMA_REG_ROM_VER1, &fw_ver1);
06820         if (fw_ver1 == 0 || fw_ver1 == 0x4321) {
06821             DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
06822                  "bnx2x_8727_common_init_phy port %x:"
06823                  "Download failed. fw version = 0x%x\n",
06824                  port, fw_ver1);
06825             return -EINVAL;
06826         }
06827     }
06828 
06829     return 0;
06830 }
06831 
06832 
06833 static u8 bnx2x_8726_common_init_phy(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 shmem_base)
06834 {
06835     u8 ext_phy_addr;
06836     u32 val;
06837     s8 port;
06838 
06839     /* Use port1 because of the static port-swap */
06840     /* Enable the module detection interrupt */
06841     val = REG_RD(bp, MISC_REG_GPIO_EVENT_EN);
06842     val |= ((1<<MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_3)|
06843         (1<<(MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_3 + MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_PORT_SHIFT)));
06844     REG_WR(bp, MISC_REG_GPIO_EVENT_EN, val);
06845 
06846     bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, 1);
06847     msleep(5);
06848     for (port = 0; port < PORT_MAX; port++) {
06849         /* Extract the ext phy address for the port */
06850         u32 ext_phy_config = REG_RD(bp, shmem_base +
06851                     offsetof(struct shmem_region,
06852             dev_info.port_hw_config[port].external_phy_config));
06853 
06854         ext_phy_addr = XGXS_EXT_PHY_ADDR(ext_phy_config);
06855         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "8726_common_init : ext_phy_addr = 0x%x\n",
06856              ext_phy_addr);
06857 
06858         bnx2x_8726_reset_phy(bp, port, ext_phy_addr);
06859 
06860         /* Set fault module detected LED on */
06861         bnx2x_set_gpio(bp, MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_0,
06862                   MISC_REGISTERS_GPIO_HIGH,
06863                   port);
06864     }
06865 
06866     return 0;
06867 }
06868 
06869 
06870 static u8 bnx2x_84823_common_init_phy(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 shmem_base)
06871 {
06872     /* HW reset */
06873     bnx2x_ext_phy_hw_reset(bp, 1);
06874     return 0;
06875 }
06876 u8 bnx2x_common_init_phy(struct bnx2x *bp, u32 shmem_base)
06877 {
06878     u8 rc = 0;
06879     u32 ext_phy_type;
06880 
06881     DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK, "Begin common phy init\n");
06882 
06883     /* Read the ext_phy_type for arbitrary port(0) */
06884     ext_phy_type = XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE(
06885             REG_RD(bp, shmem_base +
06886                offsetof(struct shmem_region,
06887                  dev_info.port_hw_config[0].external_phy_config)));
06888 
06889     switch (ext_phy_type) {
06890     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8073:
06891     {
06892         rc = bnx2x_8073_common_init_phy(bp, shmem_base);
06893         break;
06894     }
06895 
06896     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727:
06897     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8727_NOC:
06898         rc = bnx2x_8727_common_init_phy(bp, shmem_base);
06899         break;
06900 
06901     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM8726:
06902         /* GPIO1 affects both ports, so there's need to pull
06903         it for single port alone */
06904         rc = bnx2x_8726_common_init_phy(bp, shmem_base);
06905         break;
06906     case PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_BCM84823:
06907         rc = bnx2x_84823_common_init_phy(bp, shmem_base);
06908         break;
06909     default:
06910         DP(NETIF_MSG_LINK,
06911              "bnx2x_common_init_phy: ext_phy 0x%x not required\n",
06912              ext_phy_type);
06913         break;
06914     }
06915 
06916     return rc;
06917 }
06918 
06919 void bnx2x_sfx7101_sp_sw_reset(struct bnx2x *bp, u8 port, u8 phy_addr)
06920 {
06921     u16 val, cnt;
06922 
06923     bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
06924               PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101,
06925               phy_addr,
06926               MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06927               MDIO_PMA_REG_7101_RESET, &val);
06928 
06929     for (cnt = 0; cnt < 10; cnt++) {
06930         msleep(50);
06931         /* Writes a self-clearing reset */
06932         bnx2x_cl45_write(bp, port,
06933                    PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101,
06934                    phy_addr,
06935                    MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06936                    MDIO_PMA_REG_7101_RESET,
06937                    (val | (1<<15)));
06938         /* Wait for clear */
06939         bnx2x_cl45_read(bp, port,
06940                   PORT_HW_CFG_XGXS_EXT_PHY_TYPE_SFX7101,
06941                   phy_addr,
06942                   MDIO_PMA_DEVAD,
06943                   MDIO_PMA_REG_7101_RESET, &val);
06944 
06945         if ((val & (1<<15)) == 0)
06946             break;
06947     }
06948 }
